### [1] [Mitigating the contact resistance limitation of cavitated fine line Ag paste by Laser-Enhanced Contact Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08696)
*Donald Intal,Abasifreke Ebong,Vijay Upadhyaya,Brian Rounsaville,Ajeet Rohatgi,Dana Hankey,Marshall Tibbetts*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 空化辅助银浆（cavitated paste）在PERC太阳能电池中表现出明显的最佳烧成温度窗口（750°C），激光增强接触优化（LECO）可选择性恢复低温烧成导致的接触激活不足状态，从而在保持细线化优势的同时改善电性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空化辅助银浆（cavitated paste）是实现硅太阳能电池细线化、低银耗金属化的有前景途径，因其能改善浆料分散性、延长保质期并减少银消耗。然而，匹配商用浆料的接触性能仍是挑战，需要探索其最佳工艺条件。

Method: 在PERC太阳能电池上评估空化辅助银浆，采用720、740、750和762°C四种峰值烧成温度，并对比有无激光增强接触优化（LECO）处理的效果。通过电致发光（electroluminescence）和导电原子力显微镜（conductive AFM）进一步分析电流收集和局部导电特性。

Result: 结果显示明确的烧成温度窗口：720和740°C导致高串联电阻和降低的填充因子；750°C获得最佳的LECO前性能；762°C表现出额外的电学限制且LECO改善有限。LECO选择性恢复接触激活不足状态，在720°C将填充因子从76.8%提升至80.2%，在740°C从76.7%提升至79.8%。

Conclusion: 空化辅助银浆的性能主要由偏移的接触形成窗口（contact-formation window）决定。烧成工艺优化结合LECO处理为保留细线化优势同时改善电性能提供了实用途径。

Abstract: Cavitation-assisted Ag paste is a promising route for fine-line, low-silver metallization in silicon solar cells because it improves paste dispersion, extends shelf life, and reduces Ag consumption, but matching the contact performance of commercial pastes remains a challenge. Here, cavitated paste was evaluated on PERC solar cells at peak firing temperatures of 720, 740, 750, and 762 C, with and without laser-enhanced contact optimization (LECO). The results show a clear firing window: 720 and 740 °C produced high series resistance and reduced fill factor, 750 C gave the best pre-LECO performance, and 762 C showed additional electrical limitations with only limited LECO benefit. LECO selectively recovered the under-activated states, increasing fill factor from 76.8 to 80.2% at 720 C and from 76.7 to 79.8% at 740 C. Electroluminescence and conductive AFM further indicated improved current collection and stronger localized conduction after LECO. These results show that cavitated paste performance is governed primarily by a shifted contact-formation window, and that firing optimization combined with LECO provides a practical route to retain the fine-line advantage while improving electrical performance.

</details>


<div id='nucl-ex'></div>

# nucl-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [New limits on the Pauli forbidden transitions in 12C nuclei obtained with the complete Borexino dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08950)
*Borexino collaboration,D. Basilico,G. Bellini,J. Benziger,R. Biondi,B. Caccianiga,A. Caminata,A. Chepurnov,D. D Angelo,A. Derbin,A. Di Giacinto,V. Di Marcello,X. F. Ding,A. Di Ludovico,L. Di Noto,I. Drachnev,D. Franco,C. Galbiati,C. Ghiano,M. Giammarchi,A. Goretti,M. Gromov,D. Guffanti,Aldo Ianni,Andrea Ianni,A. Jany,V. Kobychev,G. Korga,S. Kumaran,M. Laubenstein,E. Litvinovich,P. Lombardi,I. Lomskaya,L. Ludhova,I. Machulin,J. Martyn,E. Meroni,L. Miramonti,M. Misiaszek,V. Muratova,L. Oberauer,V. Orekhov,F. Ortica,M. Pallavicini,L. Pelicci,O. Penek,L. Pietrofaccia,N. Pilipenko,A. Pocar,G. Raikov,M. T. Ranalli,G. Ranucci,A. Razeto,A. Re,N. Rossi,S. Schonert,D. Semenov,G. Settanta,M. Skorokhvatov,A. Singhal,O. Smirnov,A. Sotnikov,R. Tartaglia,G. Testera,E. Unzhakov,A. Vishneva,R. B. Vogelaar,F. von Feilitzsch,M. Wojcik,M. Wurm,S. Zavatarelli,K. Zuber,G. Zuzel*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 利用Borexino探测器2007-2021年数据，对碳-12核中核子的泡利不相容原理进行了最严格的实验检验，获得了多个禁戒跃迁寿命的下限和相对强度的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验碳-12核中核子是否违反泡利不相容原理（Pauli exclusion principle, PEP），通过寻找核子从1P₃/₂壳层到已填满的1S₁/₂壳层的非泡利跃迁（non-Paulian transitions）。

Method: 使用Borexino探测器2007-2021年的完整数据集，搜索非泡利跃迁中发射的γ量子、中子、质子、电子和正电子，利用探测器极低的背景水平、大质量和长测量时间进行高灵敏度探测。

Result: 获得了迄今为止最严格的碳-12核非泡利禁戒跃迁寿命下限：γ跃迁≥1.1×10³²年，质子发射≥1.0×10³¹年，中子发射≥2.0×10³¹年，β⁻衰变≥6.4×10³⁰年，β⁺衰变≥6.6×10³⁰年（90%置信水平）。

Conclusion: 非泡利电磁、强和弱跃迁的相对强度上限分别为δ²_γ≤1.0×10⁻⁵⁷、δ²_N≤7.0×10⁻⁶¹和δ²_β≤9.6×10⁻³⁶（90%置信水平），为泡利不相容原理在核子层面的有效性提供了迄今为止最严格的实验约束。

Abstract: The Pauli exclusion principle (PEP) was tested for nucleons in $\rm{^{12}C}$ nuclei using the Borexino dataset from 2007 to 2021. %the complete Borexino detector data. The approach consists of searching for $γ$-quanta, neutrons, protons, as well as electrons and positrons emitted in non-Paulian transitions of nucleons from the $1P_{3/2}$ shell to the filled $1S_{1/2}$ shell. Due to the uniquely low background level, the large mass, and long measurement time of the Borexino detector, the most stringent experimental constraints to date on the lifetime of the $\rm{^{12}C}$ nucleus with respect to PEP-forbidden transitions were obtained: $τ({^{12}\rm{C}}\rightarrow{^{12}\widetilde{\rm{C}}}+γ) \geq {1.1\times10^{32}}$ y, $τ({^{12}\rm{C}}\rightarrow{^{11}\widetilde{\rm{B}}}+ p) \geq {1.0\times10^{31}}$ y, $τ({^{12}\rm{C}}\rightarrow{^{11}\widetilde{\rm{C}}}+ n) \geq 2.0 \times 10^{31}$ y, $τ({^{12}\rm{C}}\rightarrow{^{12}\widetilde{\rm{N}}}+ e^- + \widetilde{ν_e}) \geq 6.4 \times 10^{30}$ y and $τ({^{12}\rm{C}}\rightarrow{^{12}\widetilde{\rm{B}}}+ e^+ + ν_e) \geq 6.6 \times 10^{30}$ y (90\% C.L.). The upper limits on the relative strengths for the non-Paulian electromagnetic, strong, and weak transitions have been obtained: $δ^2_γ\leq 1.0\times 10^{-57}$, $δ^2_{N}\leq 7.0\times 10^{-61}$ and $δ^2_β\leq 9.6\times 10^{-36}$, all at 90\% C.L..

</details>

# math.DG [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [A Conformally Invariant Dirac-type Equation on Compact Spin Manifolds: the Effect of the Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08738)
*Ali Maalaoui,Vittorio Martino*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了四维及以上闭黎曼Spin流形上的广义共形不变方程，证明了Aubin型不等式在非球面情形下总是严格的，从而为四维共形Dirac-Einstein问题提供了基态解的存在性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在研究闭黎曼Spin流形上的广义共形不变方程，该方程涉及具有卷积型非线性的Dirac算子。主要动机是探索四维共形Dirac-Einstein问题的解存在性，这是该领域的一个重要未解决问题。

Method: 研究方法基于分析闭黎曼Spin流形上的广义共形不变方程，该方程包含Dirac算子和卷积型非线性项。核心方法是证明对应的Aubin型不等式在流形非共形于标准球面时总是严格的。

Result: 主要结果表明，除非流形共形于标准球面（round sphere），否则对应的Aubin型不等式总是严格的。这一结果特别为四维共形Dirac-Einstein问题提供了基态解（ground state）的存在性证明。

Conclusion: 该研究首次为四维共形Dirac-Einstein方程提供了非微扰情形下的一般性存在性结果。除了某些微扰或特殊情况外，这是该领域第一个普遍适用的存在性定理，填补了四维情形下的理论空白。

Abstract: Given a closed Riemannian Spin manifold $(M,g)$ of dimension greater or equal than four, we consider a generalized conformally invariant equation involving the Dirac operator with a non-linearity of convolution type. We show that the Aubib-type inequality corresponding to the problem is always strict, unless $(M,g)$ is conformal to the round sphere. In particular, this result provides an existence result for a ground state to the conformal Dirac-Einstein problem in dimension four. We point out that aside from some perturbative or special cases, this presents the first general existence result for the conformal Dirac-Einstein equations in dimension four.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mes-hall'></div>

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Floquet Engineering of a Quasiequilibrium Superradiant Phase Transition in Landau Polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08635)
*Wen-Hua Wu,Fuyang Tay,Mengqian Che,Andrey Baydin,Junichiro Kono,David Hagenmüller*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了一种通过Floquet驱动在Landau极化子系统中实现超辐射相变（SRPT）的方法，绕过了平衡态下的禁戒定理，实现了光子凝聚和Landau能级极化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超辐射相变（superradiant phase transitions, SRPTs）在平衡态下因禁戒定理（no-go theorems）而被禁止。本研究旨在探索如何通过Floquet驱动来规避这一限制，实现光子凝聚和宏观物质极化。

Method: 采用Floquet驱动方法，在由二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas）与太赫兹腔（terahertz cavity）耦合组成的Landau极化子系统中施加直流磁场。通过非共振交流磁场调制回旋频率（cyclotron frequency）和光-物质耦合强度，同时保持抗磁项不变，产生额外的直流耦合贡献。

Result: 系统被驱动跨越临界阈值进入超辐射相（superradiant phase），其特征表现为Floquet哈密顿量基态中的光子凝聚（photon condensation）和Landau能级极化（Landau-level polarization）。

Conclusion: 这种准平衡（quasiequilibrium）方法为实现超辐射相变提供了一条与驱动-耗散方案（driven-dissipative schemes）不同的新途径，成功绕过了平衡态下的禁戒约束。

Abstract: Superradiant phase transitions (SRPTs), characterized by photon condensation and macroscopic matter polarization, are forbidden in equilibrium for homogeneous fields by no-go theorems. Here, we show that Floquet driving can circumvent this constraint in a Landau polariton system consisting of a two-dimensional electron gas coupled to a terahertz cavity in a DC magnetic field. An off-resonant AC magnetic field modulates the cyclotron frequency and light--matter coupling strength while leaving the diamagnetic term unchanged, generating an additional DC coupling contribution. This drives the system across a critical threshold into a superradiant phase, characterized by photon condensation and Landau-level polarization in the ground state of the Floquet Hamiltonian. This quasiequilibrium approach offers a route to SRPTs distinct from driven-dissipative schemes.

</details>


### [5] [Mesoscopic transport in a Chern mosaic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08654)
*Sayak Bhattacharjee,Julian May-Mann,Yves H. Kwan,Trithep Devakul,Aaron Sharpe*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析了Chern mosaic（陈数马赛克）中的介观电子输运，这是一种由具有不同局部陈数（local Chern numbers）的电子带域组成的规则图案。研究计算了零温度和零磁场下不同畴壁网络几何结构的线性响应电阻，发现简单畴配置可表现出零、整数或分数倍量子电阻的纵向和横向（霍尔）响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于分析Chern mosaic中的介观电子输运特性，这种结构可在莫尔异质结（moiré heterostructure）中实现，其中局部莫尔参数的变化会产生具有不同局部陈数的畴域。理解这类拓扑材料中的输运行为对实验研究具有重要意义。

Method: 采用简单的半经典分析（semi-classical analysis）方法，计算了零温度和零磁场下多种畴壁网络几何结构的线性响应电阻。该方法为二维拓扑材料（two-dimensional topological materials）的持续实验提供了有用的计算工具。

Result: 研究发现简单畴配置可表现出零、整数或分数倍量子电阻的纵向和横向（霍尔）响应。不同畴壁网络几何结构展现出多样化的电阻特性，为实验观测提供了比较基准。

Conclusion: 该半经典分析方法为二维拓扑材料的实验研究提供了有效的计算工具和比较目录。Chern mosaic中的介观输运展现出丰富的电阻行为，包括分数倍量子电阻现象，对拓扑材料实验具有指导意义。

Abstract: We analyze mesoscopic electronic transport in a Chern mosaic: a regular pattern of domains whose electronic bands carry differing local Chern numbers. An example platform where a Chern mosaic can arise is a moiré heterostructure, where variations in the local moiré parameters can produce such domains. We compute resistances at linear response for a variety of domain wall network geometries at zero temperature and magnetic field. Simple domain configurations can exhibit zero, integer, or fractional multiples of the quantum of resistance in both the longitudinal and transverse (Hall) responses. Our simple semi-classical analysis provides a useful computational method and comparative catalog for ongoing experiments in two-dimensional topological materials.

</details>


### [6] [Fluctuation engineering in cavity quantum materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08666)
*Hope M Bretscher,Lorenzo Graziotto,Marios H Michael,Angela Montanaro,I-Te Lu,Andrey Grankin,James W McIver,Jerome Faist,Daniele Fausti,Martin Eckstein,Michael Ruggenthaler,Angel Rubio,DN Basov,Mohammad Hafezi,Martin Claassen,Dante M Kennes,Michael A Sentef*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该综述论文从电磁涨落（electromagnetic fluctuations）调控的角度，系统梳理了腔量子材料（cavity quantum materials）领域，重点关注通过设计电磁涨落来控制和操纵关联量子物质（correlated quantum matter）的理论框架、实验进展及未来挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在通过结构化电磁涨落的频率、空间和模态分布，为控制关联量子物质提供新途径。通过新一代腔量子材料，真空和热涨落谱可以移动相边界，稳定或抑制有序相，从而实现对量子材料的调控。

Method: 采用以涨落为中心的视角组织该领域，综述了实用的设计工具箱和近期里程碑。重点分析了在现实、多模、超越长波长（beyond-long-wavelength）体系下的理论-实验挑战，并考察了光子可观测量。

Result: 论文系统梳理了腔量子材料领域的理论框架和实验进展，绘制了在超导、磁性、莫尔（moire）和拓扑平台中实现平衡态和驱动控制的机遇图谱。强调了通过设计电磁涨落调控量子材料相变和有序态的可能性。

Conclusion: 该综述为通过电磁涨落调控关联量子物质提供了系统性框架，指出了在现实多模体系中实现精确控制的理论与实验挑战，并展望了在多种量子平台中应用这一方法的广阔前景。

Abstract: Coupling tailored electromagnetic fluctuations to materials provides a resource for controlling correlated quantum matter. By structuring the frequency, spatial, and modal distribution of fluctuations through a new generation of cavity quantum materials, vacuum and thermal spectra can shift phase boundaries and stabilize or suppress orders. This review organizes the field around a fluctuation-focused perspective, surveying a practical design toolbox and recent milestones, and outlining theory-experiment challenges in realistic, multimode, beyond-long-wavelength regimes. We highlight photonic observables and map opportunities for equilibrium and driven control across superconducting, magnetic, moire, and topological platforms.

</details>


### [7] [Optical spin defect pairs in cubic boron nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08737)
*Josiah E. Hsi,Islay O. Robertson,Abhijit Biswas,Jishnu Murukeshan,Valery Khabashesku,Alexander J. Healey,Erin S. Grant,David A. Broadway,Mehran Kianina,Igor Aharonovich,Pulickel M. Ajayan,Jean-Philippe Tetienne*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在立方氮化硼（cBN）中观测到与六方氮化硼（hBN）相似的室温光学探测磁共振（ODMR）信号，验证了电荷转移机制在不同晶体相中的普适性，为量子传感应用拓展了材料选择范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前仅有少数材料能实现室温光学活性固态自旋缺陷（room-temperature optically active solid-state spin defects），限制了量子传感应用的材料选择。虽然六方氮化硼（hBN）中观测到的ODMR信号可用电荷转移机制解释，但需要验证该机制是否适用于其他晶体相。

Method: 研究测试了电荷转移机制在不同晶体相中的适用性，通过光学探测磁共振（ODMR）技术观测立方氮化硼（cBN）样品。实验考虑了不同尺寸的cBN样品，包括单个亚微米级cBN颗粒。

Result: 在立方氮化硼（cBN）中观测到了与六方氮化硼（hBN）完全相同的ODMR特征性质，包括自旋1/2特征信号。实验成功从单个亚微米cBN颗粒中检测到ODMR信号，验证了电荷转移机制在不同晶体相中的普适性。

Conclusion: 该工作证实了光学自旋缺陷对（optical spin defect pairs）在不同材料中的普遍存在性，建立了基于电荷转移机制的ODMR材料无关性方法，为探索更广泛材料的量子技术应用铺平了道路。

Abstract: Room-temperature optically active solid-state spin defects are widely known to be useful in quantum sensing applications, however, only a select range of materials have been found to host such systems. Recent measurements in the van der Waals material hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) have shown optically detected magnetic resonance (ODMR) with spin-1/2-like signatures can be explained by a charge transfer mechanism where charges move between adjacent defects forming weakly coupled spin pairs. Interestingly, these ODMR signatures have been reported in a variety of materials aside from hBN, suggesting the spin pair model provides a potentially material agnostic approach for enabling ODMR. Here, we test whether the charge transfer mechanism is supported in a different crystal phase, and report on ODMR signatures in cubic boron nitride (cBN), showing all the characteristic properties identified in hBN are preserved. We consider a selection of different cBN samples of varying size and observe ODMR from a single sub-micron cBN particle, paving the way towards sensing applications. This work further expands understanding of the ubiquity of optical spin defect pairs, and establishes the potential for exploring quantum technologies with a wider range of materials.

</details>


### [8] [Antitopological magnetic textures in an antiferromagnetically coupled bilayer with frustration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08845)
*Lewei Zhou,Jun Chen,Zhong Shen,Shuai Dong,Xiaoyan Yao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种无外磁场的双层斯格明子（bilayer skyrmion）模型，通过上下层拓扑电荷完全补偿（称为反拓扑结构）实现无斯格明子霍尔效应的直线运动，为拓扑磁结构的设计和应用提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统斯格明子（skyrmion）存在斯格明子霍尔效应（skyrmion Hall effect），限制了其直线运动能力。双层反拓扑斯格明子结构通过上下层紧密耦合且拓扑电荷完全补偿，有望实现无霍尔效应的直线运动，具有重要的实际应用价值。

Method: 研究建立了一个无外磁场的通用模型，用于分析受挫诱导的反拓扑双层磁结构（frustration-induced anti-topological bilayer magnetic textures）。该模型探讨了关键参数对能量势垒（energy barrier）和电流驱动动力学（current-driven dynamics）的调制作用。

Result: 研究发现层间耦合（interlayer coupling）在防止结构扭曲方面起关键作用，从而有助于实现更快的运动速度。该模型可在多种具有反铁磁耦合双层（antiferromagnetically coupled bilayer）的受挫磁性材料中实现。

Conclusion: 该通用模型为拓扑磁结构（topological magnetic textures）的材料设计和应用提供了有益指导，特别适用于需要实现无霍尔效应直线运动的实际应用场景。

Abstract: The bilayer skyrmion composed of upper and lower tightly coupled skyrmions on two layers with completely compensated topological charges (called as anti-topology here), has become one feasible improvement of conventional skyrmion to realize straight motion without skyrmion Hall effect, which has aroused great interest in practical applications. The present work investigates a general model (without external magnetic field) for the frustration-induced anti-topological bilayer magnetic textures with rich morphologies, and discusses the modulations of key parameters on the energy barrier and the current-driven dynamics. It is revealed that the interlayer coupling plays a key role in preventing distortion, and thus helps to reach a faster velocity. This model can be realized in various frustrated magnetic materials with antiferromagnetically coupled bilayer, providing a helpful guidance for the material design and application of topological magnetic textures.

</details>

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验验证了轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）及其互易过程——轨道泵浦（orbital pumping）和逆轨道霍尔效应（iOHE）在非磁体/铁磁体异质结构中的存在，建立了轨道输运现象的统一框架。

Method: 采用双端口散射参数测量方法，在Ru/Ni、Ru/Pt/CoFeB和Co/Cu/SiO2器件平台上直接探测轨道力矩驱动的磁化动力学和轨道泵浦现象。

Result: 实验观察到传输系数满足昂萨格互易性（Onsager reciprocity）要求的对称关系，证明了电荷、轨道和自旋角动量之间的互易转换。研究结果确立了轨道泵浦作为轨道力矩的互易对应过程。

Conclusion: 实验发现为轨道输运现象提供了统一框架，证实了轨道角动量在自旋轨道电子学中的重要作用及其与电荷、自旋角动量之间的互易转换机制。

Abstract: Orbital angular momentum has recently emerged as an important carrier of angular momentum in solids, offering new pathways for spin orbitronic functionality beyond conventional spin transport. Here, we investigate the orbital Hall effect which generates orbital torques and their reciprocal process viz orbital pumping and the inverse orbital Hall effect (iOHE) in non-magnet/ferromagnet heterostructures. Using two port scattering parameter measurements on Ru/Ni, Ru/Pt/CoFeB and Co/Cu/SiO2 devices, we directly probe both orbital torque driven magnetization dynamics and orbital pumping within the same device platform. We observe that the transmission coefficients satisfy the symmetry relations required by Onsager reciprocity, demonstrating reciprocal conversion between charge, orbital and spin angular momenta. Our results establish orbital pumping as the reciprocal counterpart of orbital torque. Our experimental findings provide a unified framework for orbital transport phenomena.

### [10] [Giant resonant nonlinear THz valley Hall effect in 2D Dirac semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08994)

Abstract: We predict a giant cyclotron resonance in the nonlinear valley Hall response of inversion-asymmetric two-dimensional semiconductors subjected to crossed terahertz electric and static magnetic fields. By employing a two-band Hamiltonian that incorporates both linear and quadratic in momentum terms, thereby capturing the essential orbital texture and broken inversion symmetry, we develop a kinetic theory that accounts for antisymmetric skew scattering from impurities. Solving the Boltzmann transport equation we uncover resonant photocurrents that exhibit a sharp, polarity-switching cyclotron peak and a nontrivial polarization response dictated by the underlying D3h crystal symmetry. Our results establish a universal mechanism for frequency-selective, phase-sensitive valley current control, directly accessible in monolayer transition metal dichalcogenides. This work provides a pathway for harnessing resonant nonlinear transport in valleytronic and terahertz optoelectronic devices.

### [11] [Topology-constrained spin-wave modes of asymmetric antibimerons and their clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09178)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Here we theoretically identify and characterize low-energy collective spin-wave excitations of isolated asymmetric antibimerons and their clusters in ultrathin ferromagnetic films. We demonstrate that an isolated asymmetric antibimeron supports a discrete spectrum of localized modes, reflecting its internal degrees of freedom. When multiple asymmetric antibimerons form a cluster, inter-texture coupling leads to the splitting of these modes into $N$-fold multiplets, where $N$ denotes the number of asymmetric antibimerons. To rationalize these findings, we introduce an effective coupled-oscillator model based on meron pairs that captures the essential collective dynamics of the system. This emergent classical mechanics description reveals that the motion of asymmetric antibimeron clusters can be understood in terms of well-defined normal modes governed by topology-constrained particle-like degrees of freedom. These results establish coupled asymmetric antibimerons as a tunable platform for spin-wave based nano-oscillators, whose normal-mode spectrum is controllable through cluster size, thus providing a programmable set of low-lying resonances for these nano-oscillators.

### [13] [Unidirectional information flow in a nanomagnetic metamaterial](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09420)
*Johannes H. Jensen,Ida Breivik,Arthur Penty,Anders Strømberg,Henrik Tidemann Kaarbø,Dheerendra S. Bhandari,Thea M. Dale,Michael Foerster,Miguel Angel Niño,Deepak Dagur,Magnus Själander,Gunnar Tufte,Erik Folven*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者开发了一个用于纳米磁体间非互易影响的框架，并基于此发现了一系列具有固有方向性的ASI几何结构。通过外部磁场协议驱动，这些定向ASI表现出单向畴生长和反转特性。研究重点分析该定向ASI家族中的一个成员，并实验验证了单向畴生长现象。

Result: 实验证实了定向ASI的单向畴生长特性，且生长方向可通过调节外部磁场强度进行重构。更重要的是，该系统的方向性在储层计算（reservoir computing）框架中显著提升了记忆能力，实现了首个具有固有方向性的ASI演示。

Abstract: Artificial spin ice (ASI) are metamaterials composed of interacting nanomagnets. Although ASI hold promise for low-power computing, the ability to transmit information through these two-dimensional systems has been limited. Inspired by non-reciprocal transport in nature, we develop a framework for non-reciprocal influence between nanomagnets. Using the framework we discover a family of ASI geometries with inherent directionality. Directional ASI have the property that, when driven by an external field protocol, domains grow and reverse in the same direction, illustrating an emergent non-reciprocity of the system. Combining growth and reversal results in unidirectional domain movement through the metamaterial. We focus on one member of the directional ASI family, and demonstrate unidirectional domain growth experimentally. Furthermore, we show that the direction of growth is reconfigurable by tuning the external field strengths. Finally, we demonstrate how the directionality of the system significantly improves memory capabilities in a reservoir computing framework. Our work is the first demonstration of an ASI with inherent directionality, offering a magnetic computing platform that combines memory and computation within a single neuromorphic substrate.

### [15] [Probing Electrostatic Disorder via g-Tensor Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09475)
*Edmondo Valvo,Christian Ventura-Meinersen,Michele Jakob,Stefano Bosco,Tereza Vakhtel,Maximilian Rimbach-Russ*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先分析量子比特对双能级涨落器的准静态响应，考虑g-张量（g-tensor）各向异性的影响。然后提出通过累积贝里相位（Berry phase）分离特定g-张量分量的读出协议。最后使用微观模拟计算量子费舍尔信息（quantum Fisher information, QFI）。

Result: 由于g-张量各向异性，量子比特响应取决于涨落器诱导的偶极扰动的几何构型。在提出的读出模型中，估计信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）约为1，总协议时间在数十微秒量级。通过QFI分析识别了量子比特对特定g-张量分量变化最敏感的磁场方向和约束区域。

Abstract: Low-frequency charge noise induced by fluctuating electrostatic disorder is a major limitation for semiconductor hole spin qubits. Here, we analyze the quasistatic response of a hole spin qubit to individual two-level fluctuators (TLFs). We show that, due to the anisotropy of the g-tensor, the qubit response depends on the geometry of the fluctuator-induced dipolar perturbation. We then propose a readout protocol that isolates selected g-tensor components through an accumulated Berry phase and estimate, within our readout model, an order-unity signal-to-noise ratio with a total protocol time in the tens of microseconds. Finally, using microscopic simulations, we compute the quantum Fisher information (QFI) to identify magnetic field directions and confinement regimes in which the qubit is most sensitive to disorder-induced variations of selected g-tensor components.

### [16] [Fundamental fields in the deformed $W$-algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09471)
*Hicham Assakaf*

Main category: math.QA

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Frenkel和Reshetikhin引入了变形W-代数$\mathbf{W}_{qt}(\mathfrak{g})$，但需要更明确的构造方法来研究其具体元素。本文旨在重新定义该代数并开发显式算法，以验证相关猜想并探索新的研究可能性。

Method: 在重新定义的框架下，本文提出了受Frenkel-Mukhin算法启发的显式算法，该算法从满足特定次数条件的主导单项式$m$出发，生成变形W-代数的元素。然后将该算法应用于具体构造$\mathbf{W}_{qt}(\mathfrak{g})$中的特定元素。

Result: 成功应用该算法证明了Frenkel和Reshetikhin在arXiv:q-alg/9708006中提出的猜想，覆盖了$B_\ell$型、$C_\ell$型李代数以及其他类型中的某些节点。该框架为显式研究变形W-代数中的场（fields）开辟了新途径。

Conclusion: 本文提出的重新定义框架和显式算法不仅验证了重要猜想，还为变形W-代数的显式研究提供了新工具和可能性，特别是在构造具体元素和探索代数结构方面具有重要价值。

Abstract: Let $\mathfrak{g}$ be a simple Lie algebra. Frenkel and Reshetikhin introduced the deformed $W$-algebra $\mathbf{W}_{qt}(\mathfrak{g})$. In this work, we propose a formal reformulation of this definition in a slightly different context. In this framework, we introduce an explicit algorithm inspired by the Frenkel-Mukhin algorithm (arXiv:math/9911112) that produces elements of the deformed $W$-algebra starting from a given dominant monomial $m$ satisfying some degree conditions. Then, we apply this algorithm to construct explicitly some specific elements of $\mathbf{W}_{qt}(\mathfrak{g})$. In particular, we apply this to prove a conjecture of Frenkel and Reshetikhin in arXiv:q-alg/9708006 in types $B_\ell$, $C_\ell$, and for some nodes in other types. This framework opens up new possibilities for studying explicitly fields in the deformed $W$-algebra $\WWqt$.

### [17] [Decoding coherent errors in toric codes on honeycomb and square lattices: duality to Majorana monitored dynamics and symmetry classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08650)
*Zhou Yang,Andreas W. W. Ludwig,Chao-Ming Jian*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究建立了拓扑稳定子码（toric codes）在相干错误（coherent errors）下的可解码性（decodability）与1+1D监控马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermions）动力学之间的对偶性（duality），揭示了可解码性相图（phase diagram）的普适结构由对偶马约拉纳动力学的Altland-Zirnbauer对称性类（symmetry class）决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑稳定子码（topological stabilizer codes）如环面码（toric codes）是容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computation）的主要候选方案。虽然其在随机噪声下的可解码性已被广泛研究，但涉及量子干涉的相干错误（coherent errors）的影响仍较少被探索。

Method: 建立了环面码在X型和Z型相干错误下的解码问题与1+1D监控非相互作用马约拉纳费米子（non-interacting Majorana fermions）动力学之间的对偶性。以六角晶格环面码（hTC）和方形晶格环面码（sTC）为代表性模型，引入了具有空间变化旋转角度的最小双参数相干错误模型，并采用解析和数值方法进行研究。

Result: 发现hTC的X型错误对偶于DIII类动力学，而hTC的Z型错误和sTC的两种错误类型对偶于D类动力学，关键区别源于时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。在DIII类中，可解码相（decodable phase）的转变对偶于面积律（area-law）和对数纠缠标度（logarithmic entanglement scaling）动力学相之间的测量诱导转变（measurement-induced transition）；在D类中，则对应两个拓扑不同的面积律相之间的转变。方形晶格环面码的可解码性对空间变化相干错误比均匀错误更脆弱。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了拓扑稳定子码在相干错误下的可解码性相图具有普适结构，由对偶马约拉纳动力学的对称性类决定。不同对称性类导致不同的相变特性，为理解相干错误对量子纠错的影响提供了新视角。

Abstract: Topological stabilizer codes, such as the toric and surface codes, are leading candidates for fault-tolerant quantum computation. While their decodability under stochastic noise has been extensively studied, the effects of coherent errors, which involve quantum interference, remain less explored. In this work, we study the decodability of toric codes on honeycomb and square lattices subject to $X$- and $Z$-type coherent errors generated by the $X$- and $Z$-rotations on each qubit. We establish a duality between these decoding problems and 1+1D monitored dynamics of non-interacting Majorana fermions. This duality shows that the Altland-Zirnbauer symmetry class of the dual Majorana dynamics governs the universal structure of the decodability phase diagram. We show that the honeycomb-lattice toric code (hTC) with $X$-type error is dual to class-DIII dynamics, while the hTC with $Z$-type error and the square-lattice toric code (sTC) with both error types are dual to class-D dynamics. The key distinction arises from time-reversal symmetry. In class DIII, the generic transition out of the decodable phase is dual to a measurement-induced transition between dynamical phases with area-law and logarithmic entanglement scaling. In contrast, in class D, the generic decodability transition corresponds to a transition between two topologically distinct area-law phases. To explore these transitions in microscopic models, we consider hTC and sTC with $X$-type errors as representatives and introduce a minimal two-parameter coherent error model with spatially varying rotation angles. Using analytical and numerical methods, we map out the decodability phase diagrams and characterize the universal behavior of the transitions. We find that the decodability of sTC is more vulnerable to spatially varying coherent errors than uniform ones.

</details>


### [18] [Path-Integral Formulation of Unavoidable Canonical Nonlinearity: Dynamic Discretization Cost over Variable Supports](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08784)
*Koretaka Yuge*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了路径积分不可避免的典型非线性（PUCN）方法，用于量化不同分布之间的累积信息几何成本，解决了现有方法无法分解整体典型非线性的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典离散系统的统计热力学中，从微观相互作用到热力学平衡构型的映射表现出复杂的典型非线性（canonical nonlinearity, CN）。虽然传统上使用Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度表征，但这种方法无法捕捉由连续高斯族离散化本身产生的内在非线性。现有不可避免的典型非线性（UCN）方法仅限于评估单个连续分布的离散化成本，无法处理不同支撑集状态之间的信息几何成本。

Method: 提出了路径积分不可避免的典型非线性（Path-Integral UCN, PUCN）方法，通过两个步骤量化累积信息几何成本：（1）通过基测度的e-混合（几何平均）保持典型分布为指数族，导致Fisher度量的算术混合作为CN标准；（2）通过其第二矩矩阵M的调和混合强制离散化单元的协变变化，反映统计流形上参数变化的不确定性。

Result: PUCN提供了任意状态之间几何成本的灵活度量，包括具有本质上不同支撑集的状态。该公式能够明确量化不同CDOS系统之间的CN，并将总CN自然分解为UCN和剩余贡献，这在现有方法中未能清晰分离。

Conclusion: PUCN方法解决了现有UCN框架的根本局限性，为量化不同分布之间的信息几何成本提供了灵活框架，实现了整体典型非线性的明确分解，填补了现有方法的空白。

Abstract: In the statistical thermodynamics of classical discrete systems, the map from microscopic interactions to thermodynamic equilibrium configurations generally exhibits complex nonlinearity, known as "canonical nonlinearity" (CN). While conventionally characterized by the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence, this approach inevitably misses intrinsic nonlinearities arising from the discretization of continuous Gaussian families themselves. This intrinsic effect of unavoidable CN (UCN), has recently been quantified within a transport-information-geometric framework. However, the UCN is fundamentally limited to evaluating the discretization-induced cost for a single continuous distribution. It therefore does not capture the information-geometric cost between a continuous Gaussian reference and an actual discrete distribution, nor between states with fundamentally different supports, making it conceptually unclear how to decompose the overall CN. To address this limitation, we propose the Path-Integral UCN (PUCN) quantifying the cumulative information-geometric cost between distinct distributions. The PUCN adopts a path by (i) retaining the canonical distribution as an exponential family via the $e$-mixture (geometric mean) of the base measure, leading to an arithmetic mixture of the Fisher metric as the CN standard, and (ii) enforcing covariant changes in the discretization cell through the harmonic mixture of its second-moment matrix $M$, reflecting the uncertainty in parameter variations on the statistical manifold. The resulting PUCN provides a flexible measure of the geometric cost between arbitrary states, including those with essentially different supports. This formulation enables an explicit quantification of CN between different CDOS systems and a natural decomposition of the total CN into the UCN and a residual contribution, which has not been clearly separated in existing approaches.

</details>


### [19] [Self-similar Dynamics in Percolation and Sandpile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08864)
*Mingzhong Lu,Ming Li,Youjin Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究发现了渗流（percolation）过程中的时间自相似性（temporal self-similarity），建立了动态标度指数（dynamic scaling exponents）与传统静态临界指数（static critical exponents）的定量关系，为理解临界动力学（critical dynamics）提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间自相似性（spatial self-similarity）是临界现象的标志性特征，但动态过程中的时间自相似性尚未被充分研究。本研究旨在探索渗流过程中的时间标度不变性（temporal scale invariance），并建立其与静态临界性质的联系。

Method: 通过追踪渗流过程中键（bond）添加时的间隙（gap）——即团簇（cluster）大小的增量——以及相应的合并团簇，研究在晶格和网络上的键渗流（bond percolation）与座渗流（site percolation）过程。该方法进一步扩展到爆炸渗流（explosive percolation）和刚性渗流（rigidity percolation）等其他系统。

Result: 在整个过程的很大部分中，间隙和合并团簇都显示出标度不变的时间模式，揭示了一种先前未报道的时间自相似性。研究建立了动态标度指数与传统静态临界指数的定量关系，使得无需事先知道临界点（critical point）即可确定临界行为（critical behavior）。

Conclusion: 时间自相似性在多种渗流系统中普遍存在，并且在Bak-Tang-Wiesenfeld沙堆模型（sandpile model）的初始非平衡演化中也发现了类似的时间标度行为，表明其动态临界行为与平衡态不同。这些结果为理解临界动力学提供了统一框架，并可能在广泛的复杂系统中得到应用。

Abstract: Spatial self-similarity is a hallmark of critical phenomena. We study the dynamic process of percolation, in which bonds are incrementally added to an initially empty lattice until the system becomes fully occupied. By tracking the gap -- the size increment of clusters upon bond addition -- and the corresponding merged cluster, we identify scale-invariant temporal patterns in both quantities throughout a large portion of the process. This reveals a form of temporal self-similarity that has not been reported before. We further establish quantitative relations between the dynamic scaling exponents and the conventional static critical exponents, which enable the determination of critical behavior without prior knowledge of the critical point. The same self-similar dynamics is observed in both bond and site percolation on lattices and networks, and extends to other systems such as explosive and rigidity percolation. Moreover, similar temporal scaling is found in the initial nonequilibrium evolution of the Bak-Tang-Wiesenfeld sandpile model, suggesting a dynamic critical behavior distinct from its equilibrium state. These results provide a unified framework for understanding critical dynamics and may find applications in a broad range of complex systems.

</details>


### [20] [Eigenstate entanglement entropy in Bose-Hubbard models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09180)
*G. Medoš,L. Vidmar*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究分析了玻色-哈伯德模型（Bose-Hubbard models）中谱中间本征态（mid-spectrum eigenstates）的纠缠熵（entanglement entropy），重点关注弱无序（weakly disordered）模型，对比了有/无粒子数守恒（particle-number conservation）以及平移不变（translationally-invariant）模型的情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管费米子系统的本征态纠缠熵已被广泛研究，但对玻色子系统的了解相对较少。本研究旨在探究玻色-哈伯德模型中谱中间本征态的纠缠熵特性，特别是弱无序模型与平移不变模型的对比。

Method: 通过将平均场方法（mean-field approach）推广到具有可调局域玻色截断（local bosonic cutoff）的多体系统，推导了纠缠熵的体积律系数（volume-law coefficient）。同时，通过谱中间本征态的平均值及其分布，分析了纠缠熵的体积律和O(1)次主导贡献。

Result: 研究发现，纠缠熵的体积律贡献在通过在位无序（on-site disorder）破坏平移不变性时保持不变。在粒子数守恒情况下，O(1)次主导贡献对粒子数密度和局域玻色截断表现出非平凡依赖；而在无粒子数守恒时，结果暗示存在超越随机纯态预测的普适O(1)贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了玻色-哈伯德模型本征态的纠缠熵结构，揭示了体积律贡献对平移不变性破坏的鲁棒性，以及次主导O(1)贡献在不同对称性条件下的不同行为特征。

Abstract: While the eigenstate entanglement entropy has been extensively studied for fermionic systems, much less is known about bosonic systems. Here, we study the entanglement entropy of mid-spectrum eigenstates of Bose-Hubbard models, focusing on weakly disordered models with and without particle-number conservation, and contrasting them with the translationally-invariant model. We analyze the volume-law and O(1) contributions to the entanglement entropy via the averages over mid-spectrum eigenstates and the corresponding distributions. We derive the volume-law coefficient of the entanglement entropy by generalizing the mean-field approach from [Phys. Rev. Lett. 119, 220603 (2017)] to many-body systems with a tunable local bosonic cutoff, which agrees with previous analytical and numerical results from [Phys. Rev. B 110, 235154 (2024)]. We show that the volume-law contribution to the entanglement entropy does not change upon breaking translational invariance via on-site disorder. We then numerically study the role of the subleading O(1) contribution to the entanglement entropy. We find that, in the particle-number conserving case, it exhibits a nontrivial dependence on the particle-number density and the local bosonic cutoff, while without particle-number conservation, results suggest the emergence of a universal O(1) contribution beyond the random pure state predictions.

</details>


### [21] [Steady-state phonon heat currents and differential thermal conductance across a junction of two harmonic phonon reservoirs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09390)
*Eduardo C. Cuansing,Juan Rafael K. Bautista*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过非平衡格林函数方法精确计算了两个谐振子库通过弹簧耦合的结中的声子输运，发现热流遵循傅里叶定律，且热导在声子谱匹配时出现峰值，但低温下峰值位置可能偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究两个谐振子库通过弹簧耦合的结中的声子输运特性，旨在为更复杂的分子结声子输运模型提供基础参考框架。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's functions）方法精确计算稳态热流和热导，分析弹簧耦合对声子输运的影响。

Result: 热流遵循傅里叶定律，热导在声子谱匹配时出现峰值；低温下由于高频声子被排除，热导最大值可能与谱匹配峰不重合；增加耦合弹簧常数会提高热导；稳态热流和热导大小与声子流动方向无关，即使在质量和弹簧常数不对称的情况下也是如此。

Conclusion: 该基本模型的特性可作为更复杂分子结声子输运设置的参考基准，揭示了声子谱匹配、温度效应和耦合强度对热输运的调控机制。

Abstract: We study phonon transport in junctions of two harmonic reservoirs coupled together by a spring. The exact steady-state heat currents and thermal conductance are calculated using nonequilibrium Green's functions. We find that the heat currents follow Fourier's law and the thermal conductance has a peak whenever the phonon spectra match. At lower temperatures, however, the thermal conductance maximum may not coincide with the spectra-matching peak due to the exclusion of higher-frequency phonons, whose spectra may match, from participating in the transport. Furthermore, we find that increasing the coupling spring constant increases the thermal conductance. Lastly, the magnitude of the steady-state heat currents and thermal conductance are the same whether the direction of phonon flow is from left to right or vice versa, even with mass and spring constant asymmetry. The properties of this basic model can serve as a reference for more complicated setups of phonon transport in molecular junctions.

</details>


### [22] [Complex paths for real stochastic processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09398)
*D. A. Baldwin,A. J. McKane,S. P. Fitzgerald*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究重新审视了随机过程路径积分表述中亚稳态衰变速率的计算，通过伊藤（Ito）表述中的极值解解决了先前推导中难以数学证明的步骤问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前在随机过程路径积分表述中计算亚稳态（metastable state）衰变速率的推导存在一个难以数学证明的步骤。本研究旨在解决这一理论困难，为衰变速率的计算提供更严格的数学基础。

Method: 采用伊藤（Ito）表述的路径积分方法，利用其中自然出现的极值解（extremal solution）来克服数学证明难题。为清晰展示分析过程，选择了一个简单的势能函数，其极值解可以用初等函数表示。

Result: 研究表明，通过伊藤表述路径积分中的极值解可以有效解决先前推导中的数学证明困难。虽然分析基于简单势能函数示例，但所识别的机制具有普适性，不限于特定示例。

Conclusion: 该研究为随机过程路径积分中亚稳态衰变速率的计算提供了更严格的数学框架，所提出的极值解方法解决了先前推导中的理论缺陷，且该机制具有一般适用性。

Abstract: The calculation of the decay rate of a metastable state in the path-integral formulation of stochastic processes is revisited. Previous derivations of this rate were achieved at the cost of a step that is difficult to justify mathematically. We show that this difficulty can be resolved by working with an extremal solution that arises naturally in the Ito formulation of the path integral. To make the analysis as transparent as possible, we choose a simple potential for which the extremal solution can be written in terms of elementary functions. The mechanism identified here, however, is not restricted to this example and holds more generally.

### [23] [Unifying hydrodynamic theory for motility-regulated active matter: from single particles to interacting polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09447)
*Alberto Dinelli,Pietro Luigi Muzzeddu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究推导了具有空间调控运动性（spatially-regulated motility）的标量活性物质（scalar active matter）的闭合流体动力学方程，建立了微观运动性与宏观集体行为之间的联系，揭示了一种新的"反运动诱导相分离（anti-MIPS）"现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解微观运动性如何塑造涌现的集体行为是活性物质（active matter）研究中的挑战，特别是当自推进（self-propulsion）受外部信号或群体感应（quorum-sensing）相互作用调控时。需要建立连接微观动力学与宏观现象的通用理论框架。

Method: 在粒子取向微观动力学的一般假设下，推导了具有空间调控运动性的标量活性物质的闭合流体动力学方程（closed hydrodynamics）。研究表明，在大尺度上，取向的贡献完全由其自相关张量（autocorrelation tensor）捕获。

Result: 建立了广泛类别的运动调控活性系统（从单粒子到活性聚合物）之间的宏观等价性（macroscopic equivalence）。理论揭示了群体感应活性聚合物中一种新的运动诱导相分离形式，称为"反-MIPS（anti-MIPS）"，其中致密相相对于稀薄区域表现出增强的活性。

Conclusion: 该理论表明，反-MIPS普遍出现在具有内部结构的运动调控活性剂中，揭示了多种不同的转变途径（transition pathways）的存在。这为理解活性物质的集体行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Understanding how microscopic motility shapes emergent collective behaviors is a challenging task in active matter, especially when self-propulsion is regulated by external cues or via quorum-sensing interactions. To address this problem, we derive a closed hydrodynamics for scalar active matter with spatially-regulated motility, under general hypotheses for the microscopic dynamics of the particles' orientations. We show that, at large scales, the contribution of the latter is entirely captured by the autocorrelation tensor of the orientations. This allows us to establish a macroscopic equivalence within a broad class of motility-regulated active systems, from single particles to active polymers. Our formalism allows us to reveal a new form of motility-induced phase separation for quorum-sensing active polymers, which we term anti-MIPS, where dense phases exhibit enhanced activity relative to dilute regions. Our theory shows that anti-MIPS generically arises for motility-regulated agents with internal structure, uncovering the existence of several distinct transition pathways.

### [24] [Multiscale perturbative approach to active matter with motility regulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09453)
*Alberto Dinelli,Pietro Luigi Muzzeddu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于具有运动性调控（motility regulation）的干性标量活性物质（dry scalar active matter）的粗粒化方法，该方法基于后向柯尔莫哥洛夫方程（backward Kolmogorov equation）的多尺度微扰展开，不依赖于粒子取向的特定微观动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种通用的粗粒化方法，能够处理具有运动性调控的干性标量活性物质，涵盖从空间依赖的自推进速度到趋化性（taxis）等不同调控形式，并扩展至一类非马尔可夫取向动力学（non-Markovian orientational dynamics）。

Method: 方法基于后向柯尔莫哥洛夫方程的多尺度微扰展开，不依赖于粒子取向的特定微观动力学模型。该理论框架能够识别确保有效大尺度平衡态存在的微观动力学条件，并在条件违反时定量捕捉大尺度粒子流的出现。

Result: 该方法成功应用于多种自推进剂（self-propelled agents）模型，从单粒子到活性聚合物（active polymers），并通过数值模拟验证了理论预测。理论还自然扩展到具有密度介导相互作用（density-mediated interactions）的活性物质，如群体感应（quorum sensing）。

Conclusion: 该粗粒化理论为具有运动性调控的干性标量活性物质提供了通用分析框架，能够处理多种调控形式和动力学特性，并在大尺度平衡态条件违反时定量描述非平衡现象，具有应用于自组织软材料（self-organizing soft materials）的潜力。

Abstract: We present a coarse-graining method applicable to dry scalar active matter with motility regulation. Our approach, based on a multiscale perturbative expansion of the backward Kolmogorov equation, does not rely on any specific microscopic dynamics for the particles' orientations. Its generality allows us to address different forms of motility regulation, from space-dependent self-propulsion speed to taxis, and to extend the analysis to a class of non-Markovian orientational dynamics. Furthermore, we identify general conditions on the microscopic dynamics that ensure the existence of an effective large-scale equilibrium regime. When the latter are violated, our theoretical framework is able to quantitatively capture the emergence of large-scale particle currents. We directly apply our coarse-grained theory to several models of self-propelled agents, ranging from single particles to active polymers, and test our analytical predictions with numerical simulations. Finally, we show that our theory naturally extends to active matter with density-mediated interactions, such as quorum sensing, with potential applications to self-organizing soft materials.

</details>

### [25] [Post-Jamming Mechanics of Feedback-Regulated Budding-Cell Packings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08942)
*Pawel Gniewek*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究建立了芽殖细胞堆积（budding-cell packings）在部分芽体未受约束情况下的平均场理论，揭示了后堵塞（post-jamming）状态由压力P和未约束芽体比例u共同决定，并预测了耗尽未约束芽体储库的交叉密度φ₂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 芽殖细胞堆积在全部芽体受到机械约束之前就会发生堵塞（jam），因此后堵塞状态同时取决于压力P和未受约束的芽体比例u，需要理论框架来描述这一特殊机制。

Method: 研究开发了平均场理论（mean-field theory），包括修正的麦克斯韦计数（modified Maxwell count）用于计算后堵塞协调数，未约束芽体的耗尽定律（depletion law）预测交叉密度φ₂，以及通量分配论证（flux-partition argument）分析生长反馈效应。

Result: 理论预测显示，强生长反馈（strong growth feedback）能显著增加系统刚性（rigidity）同时产生很小的内部压力，而未约束芽体储库在交叉密度φ₂处耗尽。

Conclusion: 该平均场理论成功描述了芽殖细胞堆积的后堵塞状态机制，揭示了压力与未约束芽体比例共同决定系统行为，并解释了生长反馈对刚性与压力关系的特殊影响。

Abstract: Budding-cell packings jam before all buds are mechanically constrained. The post-jamming state is therefore set by both the pressure $P$ and the fraction $u$ of buds that remain unconstrained. We develop a mean-field theory for this regime. A modified Maxwell count gives the post-jamming coordination, a depletion law for the unconstrained buds predicts the crossover density $φ_2$ at which that reservoir is exhausted, and a flux-partition argument explains why strong growth feedback can markedly increase rigidity while generating little internal pressure.

</details>


### [26] [Textiles: from twisted yarn to topology and mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09005)
*Elizabeth J. Dresselhaus,Sonia Mahmoudi,Lauren Niu,Samuel Poincloux,Vanessa Sanchez,Michael S. Dimitriyev*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该综述论文探讨了纺织材料作为复杂机械超材料（mechanical metamaterials）的对称性、拓扑和力学特性，将其视为凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）中一个独特但尚未充分探索的研究领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管纺织材料作为复杂机械超材料在人类历史中长期存在，但物理学界直到最近才开始关注纺织科学。本文旨在填补这一空白，将纺织材料纳入凝聚态物理的研究框架。

Method: 采用综述方法，首先分析纺纱（spun yarn）的基本构造和力学特性，特别是扭绞束结构（twisted bundle structures）。然后引入编织（woven）和针织（knitted）织物作为具有层对称性（layer symmetries）的材料，并对其进行拓扑表征，将其视为加厚环面（thickened torus）中的结和链环（knots and links）。

Result: 论文展示了纺织材料可以通过对称性、拓扑和力学特性进行系统性分析。编织和针织材料具有独特的层对称性，可以在拓扑上表征为加厚环面中的结和链环结构，这为理解其宏观性质提供了新的理论框架。

Conclusion: 纺织材料代表了凝聚态物理中一个独特的研究领域，其对称性、拓扑和力学特性值得进一步探索。通过纱线级几何（yarn-level geometry）、耗散机制（dissipation mechanisms）和缺陷结构（defect structures）的分析，可以深入理解织物的力学和几何特性。

Abstract: While textiles have existed throughout much of human history as complex mechanical metamaterials, textile science has largely been overlooked by the physics community until recently. In this review, we consider the symmetry, topology, and mechanics of woven and knitted materials, showing that they represent a unique, if under-explored, regime of condensed matter. We start with the basic construction and mechanics of spun yarn, reviewing recent developments twisted bundle structures. We then introduce woven and knitted fabrics as materials with layer symmetries that can be topologically characterized as knots and links in the thickened torus. We finally discuss fabric mechanics and geometry in terms of yarn-level geometry, dissipation mechanisms, and defect structures.

### [27] [DWS-based microrheology of triblock copolymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09273)
*René Tammen,Xiaoying Tang,Ren Liu,Iliya D. Stoev,Erika Eiser*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Pluronic三嵌段共聚物水溶液的热可逆相变及其织构已有深入研究，但其相应的流变性质，特别是高温行为，使用经典流变学方法难以表征。

Method: 采用基于扩散波谱（Diffusing Wave Spectroscopy, DWS）的微流变学技术，通过测量强度自相关函数来研究Pluronic F127溶液在5°C至80°C温度范围内的相变和粘弹性性质。

Result: 从强度自相关函数中提取了有效粘度，确定了临界胶束化温度和浓度。研究发现F127的高EO/PO（臂-核）比及其多分散性对高温再入液相的形成起关键作用，这是由于PEO溶解度降低和PPO核脱水共同导致的。

Conclusion: 微观粘弹性模量G'(ω)和G''(ω)有助于确定这些相变，并提供了固相中的力学性质，这些性质由于布朗运动受限而难以通过标准多粒子追踪技术获得。

Abstract: The thermally reversible phase transitions in aqueous solutions of the triblock copolymers known as Pluronic and their related textures are well-researched. However, their corresponding rheological properties are less studied. In particular, their high-temperature behavior is difficult to access with classical rheology. Here we demonstrated that Diffusing Wave Spectroscopy (DWS)-based microrheology allows us to study the phase transition and the associated viscoelastic properties of Pluronic F127 solutions for temperatures from 5 C to 80 C. From the measured intensity-autocorrelation functions we can extract effective viscosities and determine the critical micellization temperature and concentration. Moreover,the high EO/PO (arm-to-core) ratio of F127 and its polydispersity play a critical role in the high-temperature re-entrant liquid phase, due to decreasing solubility of PEO along with the dehydration of the PPO core. The microscopic viscoelastic moduli G'(ω) and G''(ω) help to determine these phase transitions and provide mechanical properties in the solid phase that are not readily accessible with standard multi-particle tracking techniques due to limited Brownian motion.

### [28] [Physical Properties of Dextran Solutions as Model Crowding Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09373)
*Giuliano Migliorini,Josipa Cecic Vidos,Josef Hamacek,Anand Yethiraj,Francesco Piazza*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究系统表征了葡聚糖（dextran）拥挤体系的密度、粘度、聚合物自扩散和水扩散行为，揭示了其遵循支化聚合物物理规律，并建立了考虑结合水的真实体积分数计算方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大分子拥挤（macromolecular crowding）在生命系统中作用显著，但体外模拟中常用的人工拥挤剂（artificial crowders）往往缺乏充分表征。本研究旨在深入分析葡聚糖拥挤体系的物理性质。

Method: 通过测量葡聚糖体系的密度、粘度、聚合物自扩散（polymer self-diffusion）和水扩散（water diffusion）行为，分析其浓度和尺寸依赖性，并应用聚合物物理概念进行解释。

Result: 葡聚糖粘度和自扩散遵循尺寸依赖性趋势，可用重叠浓度（overlap concentration）的普适函数描述，对应弗洛里指数（Flory exponent）为0.44，符合支化聚合物特征。粘度随浓度呈幂律增长，存在从稀溶液到半稀溶液的交叉行为。聚合物自扩散呈指数衰减，可用罗森菲尔德超额熵标度假说（Rosenfeld's excess entropy scaling hypothesis）解释。水自扩散系数和比容随浓度降低，但与聚合物尺寸无关。

Conclusion: 研究结果展示了如何构建考虑结合水（bound water）的拥挤剂真实体积分数，并证明了聚合物物理概念在体外大分子拥挤研究中的强大解释力。

Abstract: The role of macromolecular crowding in living systems is widely appreciated, but artificial crowders used to model these effects in vitro are often inadequately characterized. In this work, we examine density, viscosity, polymer self-diffusion and water diffusion in crowded dextran systems. Dextran viscosity and self-diffusion follow size-dependent trends, collectively described by universal functions of the overlap concentration corresponding to a Flory exponent of 0.44, characteristic of branched polymers. Viscosity increases with concentration as a power law, with a crossover from dilute to semi-dilute behaviors. Dextran self-diffusion decays exponentially: this can be interpreted in light of Rosenfeld's excess entropy scaling hypothesis. Water self-diffusivity and specific volume decrease with concentration, but show no dependence on polymer size. We show how these results can be used to construct the true volume fraction of crowders, which takes into account bound water. Overall, our findings showcase the power of polymer physics concepts in macromolecular crowding studies in vitro.

### [29] [A three-dimensional morphoelastic model for self-oscillations in polyelectrolyte hydrogel filaments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09486)
*Ariel Surya Boiardi,Roberto Marchello,Pietro Maria Santucci,Davide Riccobelli,Giovanni Noselli*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个三维聚电解质水凝胶细丝模型，在电场作用下于流体环境中工作。模型基于形态弹性框架，通过电场诱导自发曲率编码细丝活性，并采用局部斯托克斯流近似处理流体动力学相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在将先进的聚电解质水凝胶细丝模型扩展到三维空间，探索其在时不变外力作用下的丰富动力学行为。这种驱动机制在仿生纤毛和软体机器人系统设计中具有潜在应用价值。

Method: 采用基于不可拉伸且不可剪切杆的形态弹性框架（morphoelastic framework），将细丝活性编码为电场诱导的自发曲率。流体动力学相互作用通过斯托克斯流的局部近似（local approximation of Stokes flows）来捕捉。研究包括线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）和超临界状态下的数值模拟。

Result: 当恒定均匀电场与细丝轴线对齐时，超过临界场强后细丝会发生颤振不稳定性（flutter instability）。根据模型参数，不稳定性表现为二维或三维自持振荡。数值模拟显示，颤振可能发展为大幅平面振荡或通过次级分岔（secondary bifurcation）形成更复杂的三维运动。

Conclusion: 尽管这是将聚电解质水凝胶细丝模型扩展到三维的第一步，但在时不变外力作用下实现的丰富动力学行为突显了所提出驱动机制在仿生纤毛和软体机器人系统设计中的潜力。

Abstract: We introduce a three-dimensional model for polyelectrolyte hydrogel filaments operating in a fluid environment under an electric field. The formulation builds on a morphoelastic framework for inextensible and unshearable rods, such that the filament's activity is encoded in electric-field-induced spontaneous curvatures, while hydrodynamic interactions are captured via a local approximation of Stokes flows. We employ this framework to investigate the prototypical case of a filament with elliptic cross-section clamped at its base. Under a constant and uniform electric field aligned with its axis, the filament undergoes flutter instability beyond a critical field strength, as revealed by a linear stability analysis. Depending on the model parameters, the instability is characterized by either two- or three-dimensional self-sustained oscillations. We further examine this behaviour through numerical simulations in the post-critical regime, showing that flutter may develop into large amplitude planar oscillations or more complex three-dimensional motions, through a secondary bifurcation. Although the study represents a first step towards extending state-of-the-art models for polyelectrolyte hydrogel filaments to three dimensions, the richness of the resulting dynamics achievable under time-independent forcing underscores the potential of the proposed actuation mechanism for the design of biomimetic cilia and soft robotic systems.

</details>


### [30] [Field-mediated active dynamical bonds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09506)
*Yuanmei Li,Rahil Valani*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过共享场（shared field）介导的相互作用，实现了活性物质（active matter）系统在结构稳定性和动力学自由度之间的连续调控，克服了传统系统的权衡限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统活性物质系统通常面临结构鲁棒性（structural robustness）与动力学自由度（dynamical freedom）之间的权衡，限制了结构和运动的独立控制。本研究旨在克服这一约束，探索实现可编程活性物质（programmable active matter）的新途径。

Method: 使用振动流体浴（vibrated fluid bath）上的液滴作为最小实现系统，通过共享场（shared field）介导的相互作用实现集体自稳定（collective self-stabilization）。场介导的动力学键（field-mediated dynamical bonds）由波场干涉（wavefield interference）产生，形成持久、自修复的连接。

Result: 液滴尺寸决定了相互作用的对称性：相同尺寸液滴形成刚性σ类框架（σ-like frameworks），强制三角堆积（triangular packing）；较小液滴则支持π类协调（π-like coordination），实现更高阶对称性。组装体同时展现稳定性和持续集体动力学，包括自发旋转（spontaneous rotation）和受控迁移（controlled migration）。

Conclusion: 这项工作建立了实现可编程活性物质（programmable active matter）的通用途径，其中共享场（shared fields）调和了结构鲁棒性与动力学自由度之间的矛盾，为独立控制结构和运动提供了新框架。

Abstract: Active matter systems typically exhibit a trade-off between structural robustness and dynamical freedom, limiting independent control over structure and motion. Here, we show that encoding interactions in a shared field overcomes this constraint, enabling continuous tuning between stable architectures and dynamically active states. Using droplets on a vibrated fluid bath as a minimal realization, we demonstrate that individually unstable units can collectively self-stabilize through field-mediated dynamical bonds. Arising from wavefield interference, these bonds form persistent, self-healing connections that preserve architecture while sustaining motion. Droplet size sets the symmetry of the interactions, with identical droplets forming rigid $σ$-like frameworks that enforce triangular packing, while smaller droplets enable $π$-like coordination that supports higher-order symmetries. The resulting assemblies exhibit both stability and sustained collective dynamics, including spontaneous rotation and controlled migration. This work establishes a general route to programmable active matter in which shared fields reconcile structural robustness with dynamical freedom.

</details>

### [31] [A Levinson's theorem for particle form factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09207)
*Francesco Rosini,Simone Pacetti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并论证了专门用于描述形状因子（form factor）相位渐近行为的列文森定理（Levinson's theorem）版本，建立了相位渐近值与强子电磁相互作用动力学性质之间的明确关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于解析性要求，形状因子作为四动量平方的复变函数，在正实轴割线（cut）上方的类时区域（time-like region）相位趋于π的整数倍，需要建立这种渐近行为与动力学性质之间的理论联系。

Method: 提出并论证专门针对形状因子相位渐近行为的列文森定理版本，该定理基于形状因子作为复平面中具有正实轴割线的多值复变函数的解析性质。

Result: 证明了形状因子在类时区域上边缘的相位渐近地趋于π的整数倍，且列文森定理建立了这些整数倍与强子电磁相互作用动力学相关形状因子性质之间的唯一对应关系。

Conclusion: 该版本的列文森定理为理解形状因子相位渐近行为与强子电磁相互作用动力学之间的深刻联系提供了理论基础，建立了相位渐近值与相关物理性质之间的明确数学关系。

Abstract: We present and demonstrate a version of Levinson's theorem especially dedicated to the asymptotic behavior of form factor phases. Indeed, as required by analyticity, form factors are multi-valued complex functions of a square four-momentum defined in the complex plane with a cut along the positive real axis. Their phases evaluated on the upper edge of this cut, i.e., on the time-like region, tend asymptotically to integer multiples of $π$ radians. The Levinson's theorem establishes a univocal relation between such multiples and properties of form factors related to the dynamics of the electromagnetic interaction of the corresponding hadrons.

### [32] [Probing Higgs and Top Interactions through the Muon Lens at multi-TeV Muon Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08688)
*Tisa Biswas,Anindya Datta,Barbara Mele*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了未来10 TeV μ子对撞机对标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中六维算符的灵敏度，重点关注希格斯玻色子和顶夸克产生过程，发现其对μ子-希格斯-规范玻色子和μ子-顶夸克相互作用的约束可比现有极限提升一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中的六维算符在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上仅受到弱约束或难以探测，这主要是由于灵敏度有限和标准模型背景较大。研究旨在评估未来10 TeV μ子对撞机对这些算符的探测潜力。

Method: 研究分析了μ⁺μ⁻ → Zh、μ⁺μ⁻ → μ⁺μ⁻h、μ⁺μ⁻ → t\bar{t}和μ⁺μ⁻ → t\bar{t}h等过程，利用μ子对撞机可达的多TeV能量尺度上SMEFT效应的能量增强特性。方法包括结合微分信息和角分布的详细模拟。

Result: 研究发现，10 TeV μ子对撞机可将μ子-希格斯-规范玻色子和μ子-顶夸克相互作用的现有极限提升最多一个数量级，甚至超过未来环形对撞机（FCC-ee）的预期。研究还推导了相关威尔逊系数（Wilson coefficients）的预期界限。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，μ子对撞机在探测超出LHC能标的新物理方面具有显著潜力，特别是在矢量样轻子（vector-like lepton）和标量轻夸克（scalar leptoquarks）等代表性紫外完成（UV）模型中，能够探索远超LHC探测范围的新物理能标。

Abstract: We investigate the sensitivity of a future 10 TeV muon collider to dimension-6 operators in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT), focusing on Higgs and top quark production processes. The analysis includes two-fermion and four-fermion operators that induce electroweak vector and axial-vector interactions, as well as dipole, scalar, and tensor interactions involving muons. Many of these operators are only weakly constrained or difficult to probe at the LHC due to limited sensitivity and large SM backgrounds. We study the processes $μ^+μ^- \to Zh$, $μ^+μ^- \to μ^+μ^-h$, $μ^+μ^- \to t\bar t$, and $μ^+μ^- \to t\bar t h$, exploiting the energy-enhanced SMEFT effects at multi-TeV scales accessible to a muon collider. Using detailed simulations that incorporate differential information and angular distributions, we derive projected bounds on the relevant Wilson coefficients. We find that a 10 TeV muon collider can strengthen existing limits on muon-Higgs-gauge and muon-top interactions by up to an order of magnitude, surpassing even FCC-ee projections. Finally, we interpret these bounds in the context of representative UV scenarios, including models with vector-like lepton and scalar leptoquarks, highlighting the potential of a muon collider to probe new physics at scales well beyond the LHC reach.

### [33] [Probing Solar Symmetrons with Direct Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09283)
*Hannah Banks,Anne-Christine Davis,Luca Visinelli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次研究了太阳产生的对称子（symmetrons）及其在地下直接探测实验中的吸收。对称子是一类具有密度依赖耦合的屏蔽标量场，通过太阳转速层（tachocline）磁场中的光子转换产生。研究计算了对称子通量，并利用太阳光度约束和XENONnT数据获得了新的参数空间限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在首次研究太阳产生的对称子（symmetrons）及其在地下直接探测实验中的吸收。对称子是一类具有良好物理动机的屏蔽标量场（screened scalar fields），其与标准模型（Standard Model）的耦合具有密度依赖性。研究太阳作为对称子来源的可行性，填补了该参数空间此前未被探索的区域。

Method: 方法包括计算太阳转速层（tachocline）磁场中通过光子转换产生的对称子通量（flux）。通过约束对称子产生的光度不超过观测太阳输出的3%，获得天体物理限制。同时推导了对称子在液氙探测器（liquid xenon detectors）中的吸收信号，其中对称子通过共形耦合（conformal couplings）和非共形耦合（disformal couplings）与电子相互作用。

Result: 研究结果显示，即使在保守假设下（仅转速层产生），太阳光度约束对对称子参数空间产生了稳健的天体物理限制，并预测了地球上的keV尺度对称子能谱。利用XENONnT的分箱数据（binned data）获得了新的直接探测限制，这些限制与太阳光度约束互补，进一步压缩了可行的对称子参数空间。

Conclusion: 结论表明太阳提供了一个可测试且此前未被利用的对称子来源。天体物理搜索与实验室探测的相互作用为探测屏蔽标量理论（screened scalar theories）提供了强有力的策略，凸显了这种多方法结合的重要性。

Abstract: We provide the first investigation of the solar production of symmetrons, a well-motivated class of screened scalar fields with density dependent couplings to the Standard Model, and their subsequent absorption in underground direct detection experiments. We compute the flux of symmetrons produced through photon conversion in the magnetic field of the solar tachocline, and constrain the resulting luminosity to not exceed 3% of the observed solar output. Even under the conservative assumption that production occurs only in the tachocline, this criterion yields robust astrophysical bounds on previously uncharted regions of symmetron parameter space, and predicts a keV-scale symmetron spectrum at Earth. We then derive the corresponding absorption signal in liquid xenon detectors, where symmetrons can interact with electrons through both conformal and disformal couplings. Using binned data from XENONnT, we obtain new direct-detection limits that are complementary to the solar luminosity constraint, further tightening the viable symmetron parameter space. Our results demonstrate that the Sun provides a testable, previously unexploited, source of symmetrons, and highlight that the interplay of astrophysical and laboratory searches offers a powerful strategy for probing screened scalar theories.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate the axion quality problem in warped extra-dimensional models in which the QCD axion arises as the Wilson-line mode of a five-dimensional $U(1)$ gauge field compactified on an $S^1/\mathbb{Z}_2$ orbifold. We systematically compute these contributions and examine how both the warped geometry and the orbifold fixed points (branes) affect the resulting axion quality. *Ling-Xiao Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有粒子物理模型中的选择规则（selection rules）常由交换非可逆融合代数描述，需要系统化的方法来追踪耦合常数（coupling constants）在任意粒子散射过程中的行为，特别是在树图和圈图阶（tree and loop orders）。

Method: 构建了一个适用于包含非自共轭（non-self-conjugate）非可逆基元的融合代数的spurion分析框架，该框架不要求融合代数的忠实实现（faithful realization），也不假设动力学粒子具有其他量子数。

Result: 该框架能够系统追踪任意粒子散射过程中的耦合常数，统一并简化了先前对近群融合代数和$\mathbb{Z}_M/\mathbb{Z}_2$融合代数的分析，支持非可逆选择规则常可通过提升阿贝尔群（lifted Abelian groups）和结构化显性破缺项（structured set of explicit breaking terms）进行辅助描述的观点。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有交换非可逆融合代数的粒子物理模型提供了通用的spurion分析框架，揭示了非可逆选择规则常可通过提升阿贝尔群和结构化破缺项来描述，为相关理论研究提供了系统化工具。

Abstract: We formulate a general prescription for spurion analysis in particle-physics models whose selection rules are described by commutative non-invertible fusion algebras. The construction applies to fusion algebras containing non-invertible basis elements that need not be self-conjugate, thereby allowing us to systematically track coupling constants in arbitrary particle scattering processes at tree and loop orders, but without assuming faithful realization of the fusion algebra, or no other quantum numbers for dynamical particles. This unifies and streamlines the previous analysis of near-group fusion algebras and of the $\mathbb{Z}_M/\mathbb{Z}_2$ fusion algebras, and supports the broader viewpoint that the non-invertible selection rules often admit auxiliary descriptions using lifted Abelian groups with a structured set of explicit breaking terms.

Since the production is sensitive to the spin of the produced particle, we perform a concrete analysis for two representative cases: scalar dark Higgs DR and vector dark photons DR.Using the Planck 2018 observations, we find constraints on the reheating temperature ($T_{\rm RH}$) and background equation of state ($w_Φ$) during reheating in such scenarios featuring dark Higgs and dark photon. ### [37] [The four-loop non-singlet splitting functions in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09534)

Method: 研究采用微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）方法计算了四圈分裂函数。该方法涉及对夸克非单态分布演化相关的所有非单态贡献（non-singlet contributions）进行完全解析计算。

Abstract: The scale evolution of parton distributions is governed by splitting functions. We confirm previous partial results and obtain, for the first time, fully analytic expressions for all non-singlet contributions at this order. ### [38] [An Algorithm for Fast Assembling Large-Scale Defect-Free Atom Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08669)
*Tao Zhang,Xiaodi Li,Hui Zhai,Linghui Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一框架，通过两个创新模块解决大规模原子阵列组装中的算法挑战：基于图神经网络和监督学习的路径规划模块，以及相位和轮廓感知的加权Gerchberg-Saxton算法，实现了在原子真空寿命内组装10^4量子比特阵列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建实用量子计算机需要数万物理量子比特，光学镊子形成的原子阵列因其优异可扩展性和移动性成为理想平台。然而，组装无缺陷的~10^4量子比特阵列面临算法挑战，包括计算困难的路径规划问题和空间光调制器生成足够平滑轨迹的耗时问题。

Method: 提出统一框架包含两个创新组件：(1) 路径规划模块采用监督学习方法，结合图神经网络（graph neural network）和改进的拍卖解码器（modified auction decoder）；(2) 势场生成模块称为相位和轮廓感知的加权Gerchberg-Saxton算法（phase and profile-aware Weighted Gerchberg-Saxton algorithm）。

Result: 第一模块推理时间接近尺寸无关的常数开销~5毫秒，第二模块生成势场帧约0.5毫秒，短于当前商业空间光调制器刷新时间。整体算法能够在远短于囚禁原子典型真空寿命的时间尺度内组装10^4量子比特原子阵列。

Conclusion: 该统一框架完全解决了大规模原子阵列组装中的算法挑战，为实现实用量子计算机所需的大规模原子阵列提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: It is widely believed that tens of thousands of physical qubits are needed to build a practically useful quantum computer. Atom arrays formed by optical tweezers are among the most promising platforms for achieving this goal, owing to the excellent scalability and mobility of atomic qubits. However, assembling a defect-free atom array with ~ 10^4 qubits remains algorithmically challenging, alongside other hardware limitations. This is due to the computationally hard path-planning problems and the time-consuming generation of suffciently smooth trajectories for optical tweezer potentials by spatial light modulators (SLM). Here, we present a unified framework comprising two innovative components to fully address these algorithmic challenges: (1) a path-planning module that employs a supervised learning approach using a graph neural network combined with a modified auction decoder, and (2) a potential-generation module called the phase and profile-aware Weighted Gerchberg-Saxton algorithm. The inference time for the first module is nearly a size-independent constant overhead of ~ 5 ms, and the second module generates a potential frame with about 0.5 ms, a timescale shorter than the current commercial SLM refresh time. Altogether, our algorithm enables the assembly of an atom array with 10^4 qubits on a timescale much shorter than the typical vacuum lifetime of the trapped atoms.

### [39] [Immiscible to miscible quenching instabilities in two-dimensional binary Bose-Einstein condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08714)
*Lauro Tomio,S. Sabari,Arnaldo Gammal,R. K. Kumar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索均匀玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中不相容到相容淬火转变（IMQT）的动力学行为，特别关注非线性动力学在演化过程中的关键作用。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，研究$^{85}$Rb和$^{87}$Rb同位素在二维（2D）圆盒约束下的系统，考虑两种不同的初始配置，通过突然减小两体种间散射长度$a_{12}$触发IMQT不稳定性。

Result: 数值模拟表明，不稳定性动力学主要由大涡旋（large vortices）产生和声波（phonons）传播驱动，长期演化中声波激发占主导。动能谱的可压缩与不可压缩部分在波数$k$上呈现经典Kolmogorov标度$k^{-5/3}$，但在小尺度紫外耗散区前出现瓶颈效应（bottleneck effect）。在渐近相容区域，涡度和声波产生保持稳定，且相容性参数与初始IMQT配置呈线性关系。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了IMQT过程中非线性动力学的关键作用，发现了与经典湍流标度行为的偏离（瓶颈效应），并在渐近相容区域建立了相容性参数与初始配置的线性关系，为理解多组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的相变动力学提供了新见解。

Abstract: Immiscible to miscible quenching transitions (IMQT) in homogeneous Bose-Einstein condensate are investigated, considering rubidium isotopes $^{85}$Rb and $^{87}$Rb confined in a two-dimensional (2D) circular box, under two different initial configurations. These IMQT instabilities, triggered by sudden reductions in the two-body interspecies scattering length $a_{12}$, are explored under two distinct initialconditions, highlighting the critical role of nonlinear dynamics in their evolution. The numerical simulations indicate that the instability dynamics are primarily driven by the production of large vortices and the propagation of sound waves (phonons), with sound wave excitations prevailing in the long-term evolution. The compressible and incompressible parts of the kinetic energy spectra, in terms of the wave number $k$, are confronted with the classical Kolmogorov scaling, $k^{-5/3}$ for turbulence, which is observed in the onset of instabilities. Before reaching the ultraviolet dissipation region at small scales, the IMQT spectra exhibit a bottleneck effect, indicating a clear departure from classical scaling behavior. In the time asymptotic miscible regime, it is observed that the vorticity and sound-wave production remain practically stable. In this regime, for both cases investigated, a linear relation is also recognized between the miscibility parameter and the initial IMQT configuration.

### [40] [Ultrafast All-Optical Switching via a Supersolid Phase Transition of Light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09097)
*J. L. Figueiredo,J. T. Mendonça,H. Terças*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种超快全光开关方案，利用驱动耗散微腔中空间均匀光子超流体与自发有序超固态之间的双稳态特性，通过可调谐非局域光子-光子相互作用实现高达120 dB的开关对比度，并可在亚阈值驱动下保持双稳态记忆功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发高性能全光开关，克服现有开关在对比度和可重构性方面的限制。通过利用微腔中的双稳态现象，实现超快、低能耗的光学开关操作。

Method: 方法基于在微腔内嵌入高迁移率二维电子气（2DEG）来工程化可调谐非局域光子-光子相互作用。漂移电流使费米盘位移，在有限波矢处赋予林哈德（Lindhard）相互作用核负值区域，从而触发旋子（roton）不稳定性。

Result: 研究实现了双稳态S曲线，支持写入-保持-擦除协议，短光脉冲可在不同分支间切换，开关对比度达120 dB。在写入脉冲移除后，滞后ON态可在恒定亚阈值驱动下持续存在，实现了全光双稳态存储器。

Conclusion: 该平台在超快、亚飞焦耳（sub-fJ）工作状态下，在对比度和可重构性方面优于大多数现有全光开关。通过堆叠具有不同漂移角度的量子阱层，可工程化具有高阶对称性的旋子轮廓，实现非二进制开关的推广。

Abstract: We propose ultrafast all-optical switching exploiting the bistability between a spatially uniform photon superfluid and a spontaneously ordered supersolid in a driven-dissipative microcavity. The key ingredient is a tunable nonlocal photon--photon interaction engineered by embedding a high-mobility two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG) inside the cavity. A drift current displaces the Fermi disk, imparting a negative region to the Lindhard interaction kernel at finite wavevectors and triggering a roton instability. The resulting bistable $S$-curve supports a write--hold--erase protocol in which short optical pulses toggle the system between branches with a switching contrast of order 120~dB. The hysteretic ON state persists under a constant sub-threshold drive after the write pulse is removed, realizing an all-optical bistable memory. Since the photon field couples additively to each embedded quantum well, stacking layers with distinct drift angles allows the roton profile to be engineered with higher-order symmetries, imprinting richer spatial order on the supersolid and enabling nonbinary generalizations of the switch. Operating in the ultrafast, sub-fJ regime, this platform outperforms most existing all-optical switches in contrast and reconfigurability.

### [41] [Many-body dynamical localization in Fock space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09224)
*Nathan Dupont,Bruno Peaudecerf,David Guéry-Odelin,Gabriel Lemarié,Bertrand Georgeot,Christian Miniatura,Nathan Goldman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索周期性驱动相互作用玻色系统中多体动力学局域化的涌现机制，特别关注福克空间中的输运抑制现象，并与无序晶格中的安德森局域化进行类比。

Method: 通过将相互作用双模玻色系统映射到经典踢陀螺模型（kicked-top model），分析经典混沌扩散与量子干涉效应的相互作用，并表征局域化长度及其随粒子数和驱动参数的标度行为。

Result: 研究发现，尽管平均场（经典）动力学在布居数不平衡轴上表现出有界遍历扩散，但量子动力学在福克空间中显示出强烈的输运抑制，类似于无序晶格中的安德森局域化。研究揭示了局域化长度随粒子数和驱动参数的标度关系，以及多体系综局域化时谱统计从随机矩阵到泊松统计的交叉。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了多体动力学局域化与离散时间晶体之间的联系，为研究福克空间中的安德森相变提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of many-body dynamical localization (MBDL) in the Fock space of an interacting two-mode bosonic system subject to periodic driving. Using a mapping to the paradigmatic kicked-top model, we analyze the interplay between classical chaotic diffusion and quantum interference effects. While the mean-field (classical) dynamics exhibits bounded ergodic diffusion along the population imbalance axis, the quantum dynamics reveals strong suppression of transport in Fock space, in close analogy with Anderson localization in disordered lattices. We characterize the localization length, its scaling with particle number and driving parameters, and reveal the spectral crossover from random-matrix to Poisson statistics as the many-body ensemble localizes. We highlight the connection between MBDL and discrete time crystals. Our findings offer a promising avenue to study the Anderson transition in Fock space.

### [42] [Machine Learning Phase Field Reconstruction in a Bose-Einstein Condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09528)
*Jackson Lee,Andrew J Millis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合深度学习模型与经典计算机视觉后处理的方法，从玻色超流体的密度场中重建相位场并识别拓扑缺陷（如涡旋与反涡旋）。该方法利用U-Net架构从密度场推断相位梯度绝对值，再通过机器学习模型定位涡旋核心，最终通过图形分析确定每个涡旋的量子化电荷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验物理中的基本挑战是提取与未直接测量变量相关的信息，这在量子系统中尤为严峻。玻色超流体（Boson superfluids）的标准原位成像仅提供空间分辨的密度场，而相位场——对于识别拓扑缺陷（如涡旋）和确认超流性至关重要——被间接编码。先前研究仅能检测相位场中涡旋的位置，但未能完全重建相位或识别电荷（涡旋vs.反涡旋）。

Method: 采用深度学习（deep machine learning, ML）模型与经典计算机视觉后处理步骤相结合的方法。使用从投影Gross-Pitaevskii方程模拟获得的合成数据，训练基于U-Net的架构从观测密度场推断相位场梯度的绝对值；然后使用单独的ML模型定位涡旋核心位置，并通过后处理图形分析确定相位场。

Result: 该方法能够高精度地重建相位场，包括确定每个涡旋的量子化电荷（quantized charge）。研究展示了从二维玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）在谐振势阱中热态的逼真快照中提取相位信息的能力。

Conclusion: 结合深度学习与经典计算机视觉后处理的方法能够有效解决从玻色超流体密度场中提取完整相位信息的问题，包括涡旋位置的检测、相位场的重建以及涡旋电荷的识别，为实验物理中未直接测量变量的信息提取提供了新途径。

Abstract: A basic challenge in experimental physics is the extraction of information related to variables that are not directly measured. The challenge is particularly severe in quantum systems where one may be interested in correlations of operators that are not diagonal in the measurement basis. In this paper we take a step towards addressing this issue in the context of Boson superfluids, where standard in-situ imaging yields only the spatially resolved density, leaving the phase field - crucial for identifying topological defects such as vortices and confirming superfluidity - indirectly encoded. Previous work has shown that the location of vortices in the phase field may be detected, but has not solved the problems of fully reconstructing the phase or identifying the charge (vortex vs. antivortex). This paper shows that a combination of a deep machine learning (ML) model and classical computer vision post-processing steps can address this gap. We use realistic snapshots of the thermal state of a two-dimensional BEC in a harmonic trap using synthetic data obtained from projected Gross-Pitaevskii equation simulations to train a U-Net-based architecture to infer the absolute values of the phase field gradients from an observed density field, and then employ a separate ML model to locate the positions of the vortex cores and a post-processing graphical analysis to determine with high accuracy the phase field, including the quantized charge of each vortex.

</details>

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [43] [A scalable platform for nanometer-scale quantum confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08957)
*Christina M. Spaegele,Mehdi Rezaee,Thomas Werkmeister,Soon Wei Daniel Lim,Kailyn Vaillancourt,Joon-Suh Park,Paul Chevalier,Ido Kaminer,Philip Kim,Federico Capasso,Michele Tamagnone*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一种可扩展的纳米制造平台，能够实现低至1.75纳米的面内特征尺寸，突破了当前自上而下纳米制造技术的限制，为探索纳米尺度光-物质相互作用的新领域铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服当前纳米制造技术的局限性以实现纳米级特征尺寸，对于在极端频率和长度尺度上实现光-物质相互作用（light-matter interactions）的新领域至关重要。现有技术难以实现大规模、可重复的亚10纳米周期性结构制造。

Method: 通过精确控制原子层沉积（atomic layer deposition, ALD）的厚度，并利用宽间距氧化物纳米鳍（oxide nanofins），将传统ALD转化为表面结构化方法，在大面积上制备具有亚10纳米周期性的纳米层压结构（nanolaminates）。

Result: 该平台实现了低至1.75纳米的面内特征尺寸，并将该结构与石墨烯（graphene）集成进行电子输运测量。在纳米层压结构形成的栅极阵列（gate array）作用下，观察到与能带结构调制（band-structure modulation）一致的卫星狄拉克峰（satellite Dirac peaks），表明存在量子限制效应（quantum-confinement effects）。

Conclusion: 该纳米制造平台为探索先前无法触及的纳米尺度光-物质相互作用领域铺平了道路，在短波长光学、电子学和极化子学（polaritonics）应用中具有重要前景。

Abstract: Overcoming the limitations of current nanofabrication techniques to achieve nanoscale feature sizes is essential for achieving new regimes of light-matter interactions at extreme frequencies and length scales. Here, we demonstrate a scalable nanofabrication platform capable of producing in-plane feature sizes down to 1.75 nm, pushing the boundaries of current top-down nanofabrication techniques. Using precise thickness control of atomic layer deposition (ALD) and employing widely spaced oxide nanofins, we transform conventional ALD into a surface structuring method that produces nanolaminates with sub-10 nm periodicities over large areas. The resulting nanostructures can be used as a one-dimensional gate array to control charge carriers in two-dimensional materials. As an initial demonstration, we integrate the platform with graphene and perform electron transport measurements. In the presence of the gate array enabled by the nanolaminate, we observe satellite Dirac peaks consistent with band-structure modulation, suggestive of quantum-confinement effects. Our platform paves the way for exploring previously inaccessible regimes of nanoscale light-matter interactions, holding significant promise for applications in short wavelength optics, electronics, and polaritonics.

</details>


### [44] [Local control and lateral nanofocusing of hyperbolic phonon polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08996)
*Jacob T. Heiden,Haozhe Tong,Yongjun Lim,Heerin Noh,Pablo Alonso-González,Alexey. Y. Nikitin,Seungwoo Lee,Sergey G. Menabde,Min Seok Jang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究通过正弦波纹金表面实现了对六方氮化硼中声子极化激元波长的连续局部调控，展示了通过基底几何结构实现极化激元横向纳米聚焦的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基底纳米图案化方法（substrate nanopatterning）是二元的且调控能力有限，需要开发更精细的极化激元（polariton）波长控制技术。基底工程（substrate engineering）虽然有效，但需要更灵活的方法来实现连续可调的局部控制。

Method: 采用正弦波纹金表面（sinusoidally corrugated gold surface）来平滑变化范德华晶体（van der Waals crystal）与金属基底之间的间隙，从而实现对六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride）中声子极化激元（phonon polaritons）波长的局部控制。通过近场光学显微镜（near-field optical microscopy）进行验证。

Result: 非均匀间隙在整个结构上实现了极化激元波长的连续且近三倍的局部变化。该平台进一步实现了横向纳米聚焦（lateral nanofocusing），通过基底几何结构将传播极化激元的波长逐渐压缩和解压缩约2.5倍，与局部控制实验和理论计算一致。

Conclusion: 该研究突破了基底工程的边界，展示了一种精确局部定制极化激元模式（polaritonic modes）的强大方法，为极化激元调控提供了新途径。

Abstract: Phonon polaritons in van der Waals crystals enable exceptional light confinement and control over low-loss nanolight propagation. The polariton wavelength can be controlled by the crystal geometry, isotopic composition, or surrounding environment -- for which substrate engineering is particularly effective. However, existing approaches of substrate nanopatterning are binary and offer limited leverage. Here, we demonstrate local control over the wavelength of phonon polaritons in hexagonal boron nitride by employing a sinusoidally corrugated gold surface to smoothly vary the gap between the van der Waals crystal and metallic substrate. The nonuniform gap provides a continuous and nearly threefold local variation of the polariton wavelength across the structure, verified by near-field optical microscopy. Our platform further enables lateral nanofocusing by gradually compressing and decompressing the wavelength of propagating polaritons by a factor of around 2.5 achieved solely through substrate geometry, consistent with our local control experiments and theoretical calculations. Our results push the boundaries of substrate engineering and showcase a powerful method for precise and local tailoring of polaritonic modes.

</details>
