Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Y. Z. Zhang,Z. Zhang,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文在LHCb实验中测试了B^0→K^{*0}ℓ^+ℓ^-衰变中的μ子-电子普适性（muon-electron universality），测量了分支比比值R_{K^{*0}}，在14.0 GeV^2/c^4以上的双轻子不变质量区域得到与标准模型一致的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是测试B^0→K^{*0}ℓ^+ℓ^-衰变中的μ子-电子普适性，特别是在ψ(2S)共振以上的双轻子不变质量区域。这有助于检验标准模型（Standard Model）的预测，并为寻找新物理（new physics）提供重要线索。

Method: 分析方法基于LHCb探测器记录的质子-质子碰撞数据，质心能量分别为7、8和13 TeV，对应积分亮度为9 fb^{-1}。测量了μ子道和电子道之间的分支比比值R_{K^{*0}}，重点关注双轻子不变质量平方在14.0 GeV^2/c^4以上的区域。

Result: 测量得到R_{K^{*0}} = 1.08^{+0.14}_{-0.12}(stat) ± 0.07(syst)，与标准模型预测一致。这是该区域最精确的R_{K^{*0}}测量结果，也是首次在强子对撞机（hadron collider）上进行的此类测量。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在ψ(2S)共振以上的双轻子不变质量区域，B^0→K^{*0}ℓ^+ℓ^-衰变中的μ子-电子普适性与标准模型预测相符。该精确测量为相关物理研究提供了重要基准。

Abstract: Muon-electron universality is tested in $B^0 \to K^{*0} \ \ell^+ \ell^-$ decays, in the dilepton-invariant-mass region above the $ψ(2S)$ resonance. The analysis uses beauty mesons produced in proton-proton collisions recorded by the LHCb detector at center-of-mass energies of 7, 8, and 13 $\text{TeV}$, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9 $\text{fb}^{-1}$. The ratio of branching fractions between the muon and electron channels, $R_{K^{*0}}$, is measured to be $1.08\,^{+0.14}_{-0.12}\text{(stat)} \ \pm 0.07\text{(syst)}$ for a dilepton-invariant-mass squared above 14.0 $\text{GeV}^{2}/\text{c}^{4}$, consistent with the Standard Model prediction. This result represents the most precise measurement of $R_{K^{*0}}$ in this region and the first such measurement performed at a hadron collider.

</details>


### [46] [New physics searches at NA62](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08954)
*Elizabeth Long*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: NA62实验利用2016-2022年和2017-2024年收集的数据，分别对K⁺→π⁺X和π⁺→e⁺N衰变进行搜索，为暗光子、标量粒子、轴子耦合以及重中性轻子混合矩阵元素设定了严格的实验上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过搜索K⁺和π⁺的稀有衰变过程，探索超出标准模型的新物理场景，特别是通过四种门户模型（portal model）来约束暗物质候选粒子及其相互作用。

Method: 利用欧洲核子研究中心（CERN）NA62实验在2016-2018年Run 1和2021年开始的Run 2期间收集的飞行中K⁺和π⁺衰变数据，分别使用2016-2022年和2017-2024年的数据集对K⁺→π⁺X和π⁺→e⁺N衰变进行搜索。

Result: 对K⁺→π⁺X衰变的分支比设定了10⁻¹¹量级的上限，约束了暗光子（dark photon）、标量粒子和轴子（ALP）的耦合；对π⁺→e⁺N衰变中重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton）的产生，在质量范围95-126 MeV/c²内，为扩展的中微子混合矩阵元素|Uₑ₄|²设定了10⁻⁸量级的上限。

Conclusion: NA62实验通过高精度测量为多种新物理场景提供了严格的实验约束，这些结果覆盖了所有四种门户模型场景，对暗物质候选粒子和重中性轻子的参数空间设定了重要限制。

Abstract: The NA62 experiment at CERN has collected a large sample of $K^+$ and $π^+$ decays in flight during Run 1 in 2016--2018 and the ongoing Run 2 which started in 2021. Searches for the decays $K^+\rightarrowπ^+X$ and $π^+\rightarrow e^+N$ are presented using NA62 data collected in 2016--2022 and 2017--2024, respectively. Results are interpreted to constrain a range of new physics scenarios covering all four portal model scenarios. Upper limits on the $K^+\rightarrowπ^+X$ branching ratio are established at the $10^{-11}$ level, providing constraints on dark photon, scalar and ALP couplings. From the search for heavy neutral lepton production in $π^+\rightarrow e^+N$ decays of beam pions, upper limits of the extended neutrino mixing matrix element $|U_{e4}|^2$ are established at the $10^{-8}$ level over the heavy neutral lepton mass range 95--126~MeV/$c^2$.

</details>

### [47] [New Deep Learning Data Analysis Method for PROSPECT using GAPE: Genetic Algorithm Powered Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08814)
*M. Adriamirado,A. B. Balantekin,C. Bass,O. Benevides Rodrigues,E. P. Bernard,N. S. Bowden,C. D. Bryan,T. Classen,A. J. Conant,N. Craft,A. Delgado,G. Deichert,M. J. Dolinski,A. Erickson,M. Fuller,A. Galindo-Uribarri,S. Ghosh,S. Gokhale,C. Grant,S. Hans,A. B. Hansell,T. E. Haugen,K. M. Heeger,B. Heffron,A. Irani,J. Koblanski,C. E. Lane,B. R. Littlejohn,A. Lozano Sanchez,J. Maricic,F. Machado,M. P. Mendenhall,A. M. Meyer,R. Milincic,P. E. Mueller,H. P. Mumm,R. Neilson,C. Roca,R. Rosero,D. Venegas-Vargas,J. Wilhelmi,M. Yeh,X. Zhang*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于遗传算法的进化方法（GAPE），用于为PROSPECT实验中的反应堆反中微子相互作用创建深度学习解决方案，包括能量和位置估计以及信号-背景分类。该方法在某些情况下优于传统分析模型，分类器可将信噪比提高近2.8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为PROSPECT实验中的反应堆反中微子相互作用开发更优的深度学习解决方案，包括能量和位置估计，以及区分反贝塔衰变（IBD）相互作用与常见背景类型。该方法也可推广至其他粒子物理机器学习应用。

Method: 提出遗传算法驱动的进化方法（GAPE）来创建深度学习模型。该方法应用于PROSPECT实验环境，针对反应堆反中微子相互作用进行能量和位置估计，并构建分类模型以区分IBD信号与背景。

Result: GAPE选择的模型在某些情况下优于PROSPECT数据分析中使用的传统模型。与使用相同基础信息的传统PROSPECT中微子识别路径相比，分类器有望将信噪比提高近2.8倍。通过特定数据周期的训练方案有效缓解了初始IBD分类器验证中发现的性能偏差。

Conclusion: GAPE方法为PROSPECT实验提供了有效的深度学习解决方案，在信号-背景分类方面展现出显著优势。通过特定训练方案解决数据偏差问题，为未来反应堆中微子数据集实现无偏IBD信号分类器提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We propose a genetic algorithm powered evolution (GAPE) method to create deep learning solutions for energy and position estimation for reactor antineutrino interactions in the Precision Reactor Oscillation and Spectrum Experiment (PROSPECT) at the highly enriched High Flux Isotope Reactor (HFIR) at Oak Ridge National Laboratory. We also apply GAPE to create classification models to distinguish signatures of inverse beta decay (IBD) interactions of reactor antineutrinos from common background types. The GAPE method can also be adopted for optimization of other types of problems that utilize machine learning (ML) models for particle physics applications. When applied in the PROSPECT context, we find that the models selected by GAPE can, in some cases, outperform the traditional models previously used for PROSPECT data analysis. In particular, when benchmarked against conventional PROSPECT neutrino identification pathways using the same underlying information, the classifier offers the promise of improving the signal-to-background ratio by nearly 2.8 times. Performance biases uncovered during initial IBD classifier validation were primarily caused by differences in time-dependent response between background and signal training datasets. Biases were effectively mitigated through a data-period-specific training regimen, offering a pathway towards realizing an unbiased IBD signal classifier for future reactor neutrino datasets.

### [48] [Periodicity in Ergodic Quantum Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09422)
*Owen Ekblad,Jeffrey Schenker*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了从满足不可约条件的遍历随机过程中采样的量子通道序列的周期性特性，建立了这些特性与量子通道序列全局谱数据之间的联系，并证明了一个广义的Perron-Frobenius型定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于探索量子通道序列的周期性特性，这些序列采样自满足不可约条件的遍历随机过程。该研究旨在建立这些周期性特性与量子通道序列全局谱数据之间的理论联系。

Method: 研究方法包括分析从满足不可约条件的遍历随机过程中采样的量子通道序列，建立这些序列的周期性特性与其全局谱数据之间的数学关系。通过证明一个广义的Perron-Frobenius型定理来建立理论框架。

Result: 主要结果包括建立了量子通道序列周期性特性与其全局谱数据之间的明确关系，并证明了一个广义的Perron-Frobenius型定理。研究还提供了激励理论的示例，并提出了若干开放问题和猜想。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了量子通道序列周期性特性与全局谱数据之间的理论联系，为理解量子通道序列的动力学行为提供了新的数学框架。研究最后提出了开放问题和未来研究方向。

Abstract: We study the periodic properties of sequences of quantum channels sampled from an ergodic stochastic process satisfying a natural irreducibility condition. We relate these periodic properties to certain global spectral data defined by the sequence of quantum channels, proving a general Perron-Frobenius-type theorem. We give examples to motivate the theory and conclude with some open problems and conjectures.

</details>


### [49] [Heat and thermal travelling wave solutions of a nonlinear Maxwell-Cattaneo-Vernotte equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09432)
*Munafò Carmelo Filippo,Rogolino Patrizia,Sciacca Michele*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 研究非线性麦克斯韦-卡塔内奥-韦尔诺特方程中热和热信号以行波形式的传播，通过将热导率和弛豫时间表达为温度的多项式函数来推导精确波解，识别产生孤子解的非线性度，并通过参数选择展示精确解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究非线性麦克斯韦-卡塔内奥-韦尔诺特方程（nonlinear Maxwell-Cattaneo-Vernotte equation）中热和热信号以行波（travelling waves）形式的传播特性，探索该方程在非线性条件下的精确解析解。

Method: 通过将热导率（thermal conductivity）和弛豫时间（relaxation time）表达为温度的多项式函数，推导非线性麦克斯韦-卡塔内奥-韦尔诺特方程的精确波解，并识别能够产生孤子解（soliton solutions）的合适非线性度。

Result: 成功推导出非线性麦克斯韦-卡塔内奥-韦尔诺特方程的精确行波解，识别了能够产生孤子解的非线性度，并通过参数选择展示了这些精确解的图形表示。

Conclusion: 该方法能够有效处理非线性热传导方程，获得精确的波解并识别孤子解条件，为非线性热传导现象的研究提供了新的解析工具。

Abstract: The propagation of heat and thermal signals in the form of travelling waves is investigated for a nonlinear Maxwell-Cattaneo-Vernotte equation. The exact wave solutions are derived by expressing the thermal conductivity and the relaxation time as polynomial functions of the temperature. This approach enables the identification of suitable degrees of nonlinearity that give rise to soliton solutions. Finally, exact solutions are shown through plots for the values of the selected parameters.

### [50] [Picard-Fuchs Equations of Twisted Differential forms associated to Feynman Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09129)
*Pierre Vanhove*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种扩展的Griffiths-Dwork极点约化算法，用于从Feynman积分推导作用于扭曲微分形式的D-模（D-module）微分算子，并展示了该算法在超几何、椭圆和Calabi-Yau微分动机中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 维度或解析正规化的Feynman积分（dimensionally or analytically regulated Feynman integrals）导致相对扭曲周期积分（relative twisted period integrals）。需要发展有效方法来处理这些积分对应的微分算子。

Method: 本文提出了Griffiths-Dwork极点约化算法（Griffiths-Dwork pole reduction algorithm）的扩展版本，用于推导作用于Feynman积分产生的扭曲微分形式（twisted differential forms）的D-模（D-module）微分算子。

Result: 通过该算法，作者为来自Feynman积分族的超几何（hypergeometric）、椭圆（elliptic）和Calabi-Yau微分动机（Calabi-Yau differential motives）提供了扭曲Picard-Fuchs算子（twisted Picard-Fuchs operators）。

Conclusion: 扩展的Griffiths-Dwork算法能够有效处理Feynman积分产生的扭曲微分形式，为相关微分动机的微分算子计算提供了系统方法。

Abstract: Dimensionally or analytically regulated Feynman integrals lead to relative twisted period integrals. We present a recent extension of the Griffiths-Dwork pole reduction algorithm for deriving the D-module of differential operators acting on the twisted differential forms from Feynman integrals.
  We illustrate the application of this algorithm by providing twisted Picard-Fuchs operators for hypergeometric, elliptic and Calabi-Yau differential motives arising from families of Feynman integrals.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [51] [Does Gravity Render Probability Quasilocal?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08611)
*Oem Trivedi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出在弯曲时空中，量子理论中的概率（probability）像广义相对论中的能量一样获得准局域（quasilocal）特性。引力边界和视界将全局概率守恒转化为通量平衡定律，导致受限观测者感受到有效非厄米性（non-Hermiticity），同时保持全局幺正性（unitarity）。作者在施瓦西（Schwarzschild）、克尔（Kerr）和FLRW时空进行了具体演示，并识别了黑洞铃荡（ringdown）中的观测印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文动机源于探索量子理论中的概率概念在弯曲时空背景下的本质变化。作者注意到概率与能量在广义相对论中的相似性，旨在研究引力边界和视界如何改变概率守恒的全局特性，从而揭示量子场论在弯曲背景下的几何约束特征。

Method: 方法包括将厄米性（Hermiticity）解释为与内积守恒相关的对称性，并展示引力边界和视界如何将全局概率守恒转化为通量平衡定律。作者在施瓦西（Schwarzschild）、克尔（Kerr）和FLRW时空进行了具体计算和演示，以验证准局域概率概念的有效性。

Result: 结果表明，引力效应导致概率获得准局域（quasilocal）特性，这自然诱导了受限观测者的有效非厄米性（non-Hermiticity），同时保持全局幺正性（unitarity）。作者在黑洞铃荡（ringdown）中识别了观测印记，证实了概率守恒在弯曲时空中的几何条件性。

Conclusion: 结论指出，在弯曲背景上的量子场论中，概率守恒与能量本身一样受到几何条件的约束。这一发现揭示了量子理论与广义相对论在基本概念层面的深刻联系，为准局域量子现象的研究提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We propose that probability in quantum theory, like energy in general relativity, acquires a fundamentally quasilocal character in curved spacetime. Interpreting Hermiticity as the symmetry associated with inner-product conservation, we show that gravitational boundaries and horizons convert global probability conservation into a flux balance law. The resulting quasilocal probability naturally induces effective non-Hermiticity for restricted observers while preserving global unitarity. We demonstrate this explicitly in Schwarzschild, Kerr and FLRW spacetimes and after this, we identify observational imprints in black hole ringdowns. Our results suggest that in quantum field theory on curved backgrounds, probability conservation is as geometrically conditioned as energy itself.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括从κ-形变牛顿势（κ-deformed Newtonian potential）构建有效的κ-形变Schwarzschild-AdS度规，在扩展相空间中将κ-形变参数作为额外热力学变量处理，并推导修正的第一定律和相应的Smarr关系。

Result: 结果显示κ-形变能在不带电的Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞中诱导临界行为和相变，临界比值P_c v_c/T_c ≈ 0.370独立于形变参数且接近范德瓦尔斯值；G-T曲线呈现独特的双环结构，偏离标准的一级相变燕尾行为。

Conclusion: 结论表明κ-形变非交换几何对黑洞热力学有显著影响，能诱导相变并产生独特的双环结构，临界比值具有普适性特征，为黑洞热力学研究提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics of the Schwarzschild-AdS black hole in the framework of \(κ\)-deformed non-commutative geometry by constructing an effective \(κ\)-deformed Schwarzschild-AdS metric from the \(κ\)-deformed Newtonian potential. In the extended phase space, we derive a modified first law and the corresponding Smarr relation by treating the \(κ\)-deformation parameter as an additional thermodynamic variable and identifying its conjugate potential. Our analysis shows that \(κ\)-deformation induces critical behaviour and phase transitions in an uncharged Schwarzschild-AdS black hole, with a critical ratio \(P_c v_c/T_c \simeq 0.370\) that is independent of the deformation parameter and close to the Van der Waals value. Interestingly, the \(G - T\) curve exhibits a peculiar double-loop structure, deviating from the standard swallow-tail behaviour associated with a first-order phase transition.

### [53] [Love numbers of black holes and compact objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08653)
*María J. Rodríguez,Luca Santoni,Adam R. Solomon*

TL;DR: 该综述系统阐述了引力体潮汐形变响应系数（Love numbers）的理论基础，重点回顾了黑洞和中子星潮汐效应的最新进展，特别关注了静态黑洞Love numbers消失现象及其背后的隐藏对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Love numbers作为编码引力体潮汐形变能力的响应系数，在致密双星系统中会出现在旋近阶段的引力波形中，即将被新一代引力波天文台测量。因此需要全面理解其理论基础并综述最新研究进展。

Method: 采用有效场论（effective field theory）和后牛顿（post-Newtonian）框架稳健定义广义相对论中的潮汐响应；综述了在静态、动态和非线性潮汐响应等多种设置下，Kerr黑洞和中子星Love numbers及耗散响应系数的计算方法。

Result: 综述涵盖了黑洞和中子星潮汐响应的广泛计算，并扩展到带电黑洞、高维黑洞、反德西特黑洞、超引力黑洞以及超越广义相对论的理论等"新物理"场景，特别揭示了为解释静态黑洞Love numbers消失现象而发现的一系列隐藏对称性。

Conclusion: 该综述提供了Love numbers理论基础的全面教学性阐述，系统总结了致密天体潮汐效应研究的最新进展，特别强调了在解释静态黑洞Love numbers消失过程中发现的广义相对论隐藏对称性，为未来引力波观测提供了重要理论支持。

Abstract: The Love numbers of a gravitating body are response coefficients encoding its tidal deformability. In compact binary systems, they appear in the gravitational waveform during the inspiral phase and will be measurable by upcoming gravitational-wave observatories. This review provides a comprehensive and pedagogical account of the theoretical foundations of Love numbers and surveys the most recent advances in the study of tidal effects in compact objects, with particular emphasis on black holes and neutron stars.
  We begin with a gentle introduction to tidal effects in Newtonian gravity, leading into a discussion of how to robustly define tidal responses in general relativity using the effective field theory and post-Newtonian frameworks. After an overview of the perturbation theory of black holes and neutron stars, we review the computation of Love numbers and dissipative response coefficients in a wide range of settings, including the static, dynamical, and nonlinear tidal responses of Kerr black holes and neutron stars in four-dimensional general relativity. We further discuss the extension of these results to charged black holes and a number of "new physics" scenarios, including higher-dimensional black holes and other black objects, (anti-) de Sitter black holes, supergravity black holes, and theories beyond general relativity. Finally we provide an overview of the tantalizing zoo of hidden symmetries of general relativity that have been uncovered in the attempt to explain the famous vanishing of static black hole Love numbers.

### [54] [Minimum mass, maximum charge and hyperbolicity in scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08668)
*Dario Rossi,Leonardo Gualtieri,Thomas P. Sotiriou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究标量高斯-博内引力（scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity）中黑洞解的微扰方程双曲性（hyperbolicity）的丧失。发现当黑洞质量低于最小值时，微扰方程变为椭圆型，这对应有效场论（effective field theory）的失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究标量高斯-博内引力中黑洞解微扰方程的双曲性丧失问题。当黑洞质量低于特定最小值时，微扰方程变为椭圆型，这可能导致有效场论失效，需要分析这种最小质量对理论参数的依赖性。

Method: 考虑一类允许任意小质量静态黑洞解的耦合函数（coupling functions）。分析微扰方程从双曲型变为椭圆型的临界条件，研究最小质量对理论参数的依赖关系，特别关注耦合函数的适当选择。

Result: 发现通过适当选择耦合函数，最小质量可以任意小。然而，这并不对应广义相对论（general relativity）的更大偏离，因为可观测量如黑洞标量荷（scalar charge）存在上界。

Conclusion: 标量高斯-博内引力中黑洞微扰方程的双曲性丧失定义了有效场论的适用范围。虽然最小质量可通过耦合函数调整至任意小，但可观测效应仍受限于标量荷的上界，表明与广义相对论的偏离有限。

Abstract: We study the loss of hyperbolicity of perturbation equations for black hole solutions of scalar Gauss-Bonnet gravity. We consider a class of coupling functions allowing for static black hole solutions with arbitrary small masses. For masses below a minimum value, such solutions become unphysical, because the perturbation equations become elliptic; this arguably corresponds to the loss of validity of the effective field theory. We analyse the dependence of this minimum mass on the parameters of the theory, finding that with an appropriate choice of the coupling function, such mass can be chosen arbitrarily small. However, this does not correspond to larger deviations from general relativity, since observable quantities like the black hole scalar charge are bounded by above.

*Valentin Pomakov,Stefano Liberati*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在浅水盆地表面重力波（surface-gravity waves）的模拟引力（analogue-gravity）平台上，如何模拟规则黑洞（regular black holes）和无视界黑洞模拟物（horizonless black-hole mimickers）的时空结构及其不稳定性，并评估了实验可行性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究基于浅水盆地表面重力波的模拟引力平台，通过识别所需的流场剖面（flow profiles）和边界条件来复制相关有效几何。具体展示了非旋转中心排水配置（non-rotating central-drainage configuration）可模拟内核度量，并提出了分级排水剖面（graded-drainage profile）将其连接到渐近平坦外部区域。

Result: 分析表明，虽然所需实验设置原则上可实现，但使用玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）等替代介质可能为忠实捕捉目标物理特征提供更实用的途径。研究评估了利用现有技术研究上述不稳定性的实验可行性。

Conclusion: 模拟引力平台为实验研究规则黑洞和无视界黑洞模拟物的不稳定性提供了可行路径，但需要进一步优化实验介质和配置以更有效地再现目标物理现象。

Abstract: Recent advances in the observation of black-hole candidates have renewed interest in probing their near-horizon structure and in searching for departures from the standard singular solutions of general relativity. In this context, significant effort has been devoted to regular black holes and to horizonless black-hole mimickers, motivated primarily by quantum-gravitational effects. Depending on the value of the regularization parameter relative to the object mass, typical spherically symmetric solutions can describe either of these two scenarios. Regular black-hole configurations generically feature an outer and an inner horizon surrounding a maximally symmetric core; the inner horizon in turn triggers mass inflation and semiclassical instabilities. The horizonless branch of the same solutions, by contrast, supports stable inner light rings when sufficiently compact, yet is itself subject to instabilities associated with long-lived quasinormal modes. Here we investigate how to emulate these spacetimes in an analogue-gravity platform based on surface-gravity waves in a shallow-water basin, with the aim of reproducing these instabilities experimentally. We begin by identifying the flow profiles and boundary conditions required to replicate the relevant effective geometries. In particular, we show that the inner-core metrics can be simulated with a non-rotating central-drainage configuration, and we propose a graded-drainage profile to connect them to an asymptotically flat exterior region. We then assess the experimental feasibility of studying the instabilities mentioned above with current technology. Our conclusion is that, while the required setup is realizable in principle, alternative media, such as Bose-Einstein condensates, may offer a more practical route to faithfully capturing the targeted physical features.

### [56] [Tidal Response of Compact Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08679)

Abstract: The tidal response of compact objects provides a powerful probe of their internal structure and of the surrounding gravitational field. We provide a comprehensive and unified overview of tidal effects in black holes, neutron stars, and exotic compact objects, with emphasis on both static and dynamical responses to external fields, encoded in Love numbers and dissipation numbers. We discuss the vanishing of static bosonic Love numbers for black holes in vacuum General Relativity, their modifications in alternative theories, in non-standard models of compact objects, and in the presence of matter, as well as their role in testing deviations from Einstein's theory and environmental effects. A fundamental distinction between bosonic and fermionic perturbations is highlighted, as the latter yield nonzero static Love numbers even for black holes in General Relativity. For neutron stars, we overview the dependence of tidal Love numbers on the equation of state, the emergence of quasi-universal relations, and the impact of rotation, nonlinearities, and dynamical effects. Exotic compact objects typically feature nonvanishing static tidal Love numbers -- a striking observational signature that differentiates them from black holes. We further review how tidal effects influence the gravitational-wave signals from binary inspirals, and explore their implications for gravitational-wave astronomy. In particular, we stress their significance for current and future detectors as tools to test General Relativity, constrain the nuclear equation of state, and probe the fundamental nature of compact objects and their environments.

### [57] [Prompt Response from Plunging Sources in Schwarzschild Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08680)
*Sizheng Ma*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中引力波（gravitational waves）的瞬态响应（prompt response）成分，将其与准正则模（quasinormal modes）和尾部（tail）贡献结合，实现了时域波形的高精度重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波由史瓦西时空中的运动源产生，可分解为三个主要成分：准正则模、尾部和瞬态响应。前两者已被广泛研究，但对瞬态响应的系统精确处理相对较少受到关注。

Method: 基于近期在阐明Regge-Wheeler方程格林函数（Green's function）结构方面的进展，本研究为瞬态响应建立了坚实的理论基础，并研究了源在史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）中旋进（inspiraling）和坠入（plunging）时的形态。

Result: 在旋进阶段，瞬态响应比准正则模的动态激发强约1.2倍，两者都受到瞬时轨道运动的调制。在波形峰值附近，瞬态响应迅速衰减，而准正则模过渡到铃荡（ringdown）区域。通过结合瞬态响应、准正则模和尾部贡献，实现了时域旋进-合并-铃荡（inspiral-merger-ringdown）波形的99%精度重构。

Conclusion: 这些结果为从旋进到合并和铃荡的过渡提供了新的见解，并通过高精度波形重构强有力地支持了这种分解方法的准确性。

Abstract: Gravitational waves generated by moving sources in Schwarzschild spacetime can be decomposed into three principal components: quasinormal modes, tail, and prompt response. While the first two have been extensively studied, a systematic and exact treatment of the prompt response has received comparatively little attention. In this work, building on recent progress in elucidating the structure of the Green's function of the Regge-Wheeler equation, we place the prompt response on a firm theoretical footing and investigate its morphology for sources inspiraling and plunging into a Schwarzschild black hole. We find that during the inspiral phase, the prompt response is stronger than the dynamical excitation of quasinormal modes by a factor of ~1.2, with both contributions modulated by the instantaneous orbital motion. Near the waveform peak, the prompt response rapidly decays, while the quasinormal modes transition into the ringdown regime. By combining the prompt response, quasinormal modes, and tail contributions, we achieve an accurate reconstruction of the full time-domain inspiral-merger-ringdown waveform at the 99$\%$ level, thereby providing strong support for the accuracy of this decomposition. These results offer new insight into the transition from inspiral to merger and ringdown.

Abstract: Gravitational-wave detectors are affected by short-duration non-Gaussian noise transients, commonly referred to as glitches, which can obscure astrophysical signals and complicate downstream analyses. While recent work has demonstrated the effectiveness of deep learning models for glitch classification using image-based time-frequency representations, comparatively less attention has been given to systematic evaluations of machine-learning architectures operating directly on tabular glitch metadata. In this work, we present a comprehensive benchmark of classical and deep learning models for multiclass glitch classification using numerical features derived from the Gravity Spy dataset. We compare gradient-boosted decision trees with a diverse set of neural architectures, including multilayer perceptrons, attention-based models, and neural decision ensembles, and evaluate them in terms of classification performance, inference efficiency, parameter efficiency, data-scaling behavior, and cross-model interpretability alignment. We find that while tree-based methods remain strong baselines for tabular data, several deep learning models achieve competitive performance with substantially fewer parameters and exhibit distinct inductive biases and scaling behavior. A cross-model attribution analysis further reveals partially consistent feature-importance hierarchies across architectures, providing new insight into interpretability structure in tabular models. These results clarify trade-offs between performance, complexity, data efficiency, and interpretability in tabular gravitational-wave analyses and provide practical guidance for deploying machine-learning models in detector characterization pipelines.

### [59] [Oppenheimer-Snyder Collapse in f(R) Gravity : Stalemate or Resolution?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08806)
*Soumya Chakrabarti,Apratim Ganguly,Radouane Gannouji,Chiranjeeb Singha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了度量f(R)引力中的Oppenheimer-Snyder塌缩问题，通过将均匀尘埃FLRW内部与广义Vaidya外部在类时超曲面上匹配。研究发现，在限制的广义Vaidya物质形式下，塌缩问题仍然未解决，可接受的解分支受到高度约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究度量f(R)引力理论中的Oppenheimer-Snyder塌缩问题，探讨在修正引力框架下恒星塌缩的物理可解性。该研究旨在理解f(R)引力中额外的匹配条件如何影响塌缩过程的描述。

Method: 通过将均匀尘埃Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker内部与广义Vaidya外部在类时超曲面上进行匹配。在度量f(R)引力中，正则匹配要求诱导度规、外曲率、Ricci标量及其法向导数的连续性。

Result: 对于无限制的广义Vaidya外部，匹配条件固定边界数据但不唯一确定体扩展。当外部物质内容限制为广义Vaidya形式时，场方程施加强约束，迫使f,R线性依赖于面半径。对于一般可行的f(R)模型，A(v)≠0的分支不允许具有有限渐近曲率的全局扩展，而A(v)=0的分支将内部置于常曲率区域。

Conclusion: 广义Vaidya外部在形式层面上重新开启了塌缩问题，但在本文考虑的限制物质区域内，Oppenheimer-Snyder尘埃塌缩问题仍然未解决。物理可接受的分支受到高度约束，排除了非平凡尘埃塌缩的可能性，尽管不排除具有常迹的更一般内部物质的塌缩。

Abstract: We study the Oppenheimer--Snyder (OS) collapse problem in metric $f(R)$ gravity by matching a homogeneous dust Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker (FLRW) interior to a generalized Vaidya exterior across a timelike hypersurface. In metric $f(R)$ gravity, regular matching requires the continuity not only of the induced metric and extrinsic curvature, but also of the Ricci scalar and its normal derivative. These additional conditions generically exclude the usual Ricci-flat exteriors, such as the Schwarzschild solution. We show that, for an unrestricted generalized Vaidya exterior, the matching conditions fix the boundary data but do not uniquely determine the bulk extension, leaving open the possibility of a physical resolution of the collapse problem. However, once the exterior matter content is restricted to the generalized Vaidya form, the field equations impose a strong constraint, forcing $f_{,R}$ to be linear in the areal radius, $f_{,R}=A(v)\,r+B(v)$. For locally invertible $f_{,R}$ with $f_{,RR}\neq 0$, this sharply reduces the admissible class of exteriors, so that the matching data uniquely determine the exterior solution on each interval where the boundary map is locally invertible. We further show that, for generic viable $f(R)$ models, the branch with $A(v)\neq 0$ does not admit a global extension with finite asymptotic curvature, while the branch $A(v)=0$ places the interior on a constant-curvature sector. This excludes nontrivial dust collapse, although it does not rule out collapse for more general interior matter with constant trace. Thus, generalized Vaidya exteriors reopen the collapse problem at a formal level, but within the restricted matter sector considered here, the OS dust collapse problem remains unresolved and the physically acceptable branch is highly constrained.

</details>


### [60] [labrador: A domain-optimized machine-learning tool for gravitational wave inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08897)
*Javier Roulet,Marco Crisostomi,Lucy M. Thomas,Katerina Chatziioannou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为labrador的改进型神经后验估计方法，通过整合物理领域知识（如异差压缩、坐标变换和参数空间折叠）来增强引力波源参数推断的效率与可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速可靠的引力波源参数推断对于分析规模达数百次探测的大型目录以及识别短寿命电磁对应体至关重要。神经后验估计（neural posterior estimation）虽能实现快速推断，但训练成本高昂且模型可解释性有限。

Method: 该方法在模型架构中整合了领域特定的物理洞见与方法：通过近似似然最大化选择参考波形进行异差（heterodyning）以压缩数据；采用定制坐标系消除参数简并性；通过折叠参数空间消除已知的多模态性。这些改进使网络对源参数变化具有近似等变性（equivariance）。

Result: 实现的labrador系统可在约1天时间尺度上完成端到端训练（使用约10²个CPU核心和V100 GPU），在宽质量范围（啁啾质量chirp mass ℳ∈1-50 M⊙，质量比q>0.1）的四极、对齐自旋信号上达到1%的中位数重要性采样效率。该方法是首个能够广泛覆盖次质量m₂<10 M⊙的长时信号的神经推断代码。

Conclusion: 通过整合物理领域知识，labrador显著降低了训练成本并提升了模型可解释性。其创新贡献包括一种数值稳定的程序，使得在模拟先验与推断先验不同时仍能进行神经后验估计。

Abstract: Fast and reliable inference of gravitational-wave source parameters is crucial for analyzing large catalogs that are reaching the size of hundreds of detections, and for identifying short-lived electromagnetic counterparts. Neural posterior estimation has emerged as a powerful inference method, where the model is trained on simulated gravitational-wave data at considerable computational cost, but thereafter enables extremely fast and inexpensive inference at test time. Here, we extend this approach by incorporating domain-specific physical insights and methods in the model architecture. These include compressing the data by heterodyning against a reference waveform chosen via approximate likelihood maximization, removing parameter degeneracies through tailored coordinate systems, and eliminating known multimodalities by folding the parameter space. As a result, the network is approximately equivariant to changes in the source parameters, and achieves a reduced training cost and improved model interpretability. Our implementation, called labrador, can be trained end-to-end on a 1-day timescale on $\sim 10^2$ CPU cores and a V100 GPU, achieving a median importance-sampling efficiency of 1% on quadrupolar, aligned-spin signals in a broad mass range (chirp mass $\mathcal M \in 1\text{-}50\,\mathrm{M}_\odot$, mass ratio $q > 0.1$). labrador is the first neural inference code to achieve extensive coverage of long-duration signals with secondary masses $m_2 < 10\,\mathrm{M}_\odot$, rendered possible by its equivariance property. Among our novel contributions is a numerically stable procedure that enables neural posterior estimation when the simulation and inference priors differ.

</details>

Abstract: In arXiv:2603.18175, the authors argue, based on numerical studies of particular cases, that the quantum damping of cosmological shear in a modified loop quantum cosmological model (mLQC-I) that was recently found in arXiv:2510.14021 is not generic and that the universe never becomes truly classical. In this brief Note, we revisit these claims by carefully examining the underlying assumptions and the class of initial conditions considered. Restricting to physically relevant initial conditions corresponding to genuine three-dimensional contraction, we find that the quantum damping of cosmological shear is a robust dynamical feature. This conclusion is supported by both numerical and perturbative analyses, which demonstrate that the post-bounce evolution admits an isotropic attractor, with anisotropies decaying exponentially and independently of the matter content, provided that the weak energy condition is satisfied. ### [63] [Finite Hilbert space and maximum mass of Schwarzschild black holes from a Generalized Uncertainty Principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08953)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过在史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）的约化相空间（reduced phase space）上直接实现广义不确定性原理（generalized uncertainty principle, GUP），得到了有限且离散的质量谱、严格的质量上限、有界的熵以及完全正则化的霍金温度（Hawking temperature）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索在同时具有最小长度（minimal length）和最大动量（maximal momentum）的广义不确定性原理框架下，黑洞物理性质的修正效应，特别是对质量谱、熵和温度等关键物理量的影响。

Method: 方法包括：1）在史瓦西黑洞的约化相空间上直接实现GUP；2）构造GUP变形的流逝函数（lapse function），该函数保持ADM质量和视界半径不变，同时通过表面引力精确再现GUP温度；3）利用观测到的超大质量黑洞数据约束GUP参数。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）获得有限且离散的黑洞质量谱；2）发现黑洞质量的严格上限；3）得到有界的熵；4）实现完全正则化的霍金温度；5）利用观测数据推导出GUP参数约束β≲10⁻⁹⁸。

Conclusion: 结论表明，当前的天体物理观测数据已经对最小长度量子引力（minimal length quantum gravity）施加了强有力的约束，GUP框架能够显著修正黑洞的热力学性质，包括质量谱的离散化和物理量的有限性。

Abstract: We show that implementing a generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) with both minimal length and maximal momentum directly on the reduced phase space of the Schwarzschild black hole (BH) leads to a finite and discrete mass spectrum, a strict upper bound on the BH mass, a bounded entropy, and a fully regulated Hawking temperature. We further construct a GUP-deformed lapse function that preserves the ADM mass and horizon radius while exactly reproducing the GUP temperature through the surface gravity. Using the most massive observed supermassive BHs, we derive the constraint on the GUP parameter, $β\lesssim 10^{-98}$, showing that present astrophysical data already impose robust bounds on minimal length quantum gravity.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过完全解析推导激光干涉空间天线对运动学偶极的响应函数，构建最优检测器，并利用费希尔预报评估不同探测器配置下的检测灵敏度。

Result: 研究发现偶极响应由单一频率依赖函数决定，对于尺度不变背景，基准LISA需要$h^2Ω_{\rm GW} \gtrsim 5\times 10^{-8}$才能检测，而仪器噪声降低一个数量级的探测器仅需$h^2Ω_{\rm GW} \gtrsim 5\times 10^{-10}$。

Abstract: The motion of the Solar System with respect to the cosmic rest frame induces a kinematic dipole in the stochastic gravitational-wave background (GWB). Detecting this signal with space-based interferometers would provide an independent measurement of our peculiar velocity and a GW probe of cosmic anisotropies. We present a fully analytic derivation of the response of the \emph{Laser Interferometer Space Antenna} (LISA) to a kinematic dipole, and construct an optimal estimator for its detection. We show that the dipolar response is governed by a single frequency-dependent function fixed by symmetry, and we compute its behaviour across the LISA band. Using Fisher forecasts, we find that for a scale-invariant background detectability requires $h^2Ω_{\rm GW} \gtrsim 5\times 10^{-8}$ for \emph{fiducial} LISA, and $h^2Ω_{\rm GW} \gtrsim 5\times 10^{-10}$ for a detector with characteristic instrumental-noise amplitudes improved by an order of magnitude. Prospects are more favorable for signals with richer frequency profile. We also explore the potential of the kinematic dipole to break degeneracies, particularly in the presence of strong galactic foregrounds or noise features that closely mimic the primordial signal.

Abstract: With the Event Horizon Telescope and future Very Long Baseline Interferometry arrays poised to image supermassive black holes, there is an urgent need to understand dynamic aspects of small-scale structure near the supermassive black hole. In this study, we introduce the relative magnification factor to characterize point sources distributed on the surface of the accretion disk near a black hole. We investigate the influence of source motion on this factor, comparing static sources with those corotating with the disk. In contrast to the static case, which can be well-understood in the standard framework of gravitational lensing, corotating sources exhibit significant distortions in the distribution of the magnification factor on both the image and source planes, indicating that the caustic structure is substantially modulated by source motion. This magnification factor pattern encodes signatures of the kinematics of accretion flow when the time-delayed images are incorporated. This potentially offers a novel probe for investigating the interplay between spacetime geometry and properties of accretion flow.

### [67] [Gravitational Memory from Hairy Binary Black Hole Mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09350)
*Silvia Gasparotto,Jann Zosso,Llibert Aresté Saló,Daniela D. Doneva,Stoytcho S. Yazadjiev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究首次在广义相对论之外的理论中计算了引力波记忆效应，聚焦于标量-高斯-博内引力理论，发现记忆效应可为第三代探测器提供测试引力的补充信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波记忆（gravitational-wave memory）是辐射场的低频非振荡分量，为强场引力提供了潜在强大但尚未被探测的探针。本研究旨在超越广义相对论（general relativity），在标量-高斯-博内引力（scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）这一理论动机充分且数值可处理的扩展理论中，首次计算全旋近-并合-铃坠波形产生的引力波记忆。

Method: 从霍恩德斯基引力（Horndeski gravity）中的一般记忆公式出发，推导了标量-高斯-博内理论中张量零记忆（tensor null memory）的显式自旋权重球谐表达式。利用现有数值相对论波形，对对称平移和动态标量化双黑洞并合两种情况进行了评估。

Result: 研究发现主导效应是通过非线性并合动力学的改变间接修正张量记忆，而标量对张量记忆的直接贡献在本研究考虑的系统中仍被压制数个数量级。对于数据集中最大的偏差，最终记忆振幅与相应广义相对论预测相差几个百分点，在探测器导向分析中与最小化波形失配的广义相对论模板相比差异可达约4%。

Conclusion: 包含记忆效应使广义相对论与标量-高斯-博内波形之间的失配增加一个数量级以上，表明记忆效应可为第三代探测器测试引力提供补充信息，尤其对低质量双星系统。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave memory is a low-frequency, non-oscillatory component of the radiation field that provides a potentially powerful but as yet undetected probe of strong-field gravity. We present the first calculation of gravitational memory from full inspiral--merger--ringdown waveforms in a theory beyond general relativity, focusing on scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity as a theoretically well-motivated and numerically accessible extension of GR. Starting from the general memory formulas in Horndeski gravity, we derive explicit spin-weighted spherical-harmonic expressions for the tensor null memory in scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory and evaluate them on existing numerical-relativity waveforms for both shift-symmetric and dynamically scalarizing binary black hole mergers. We find that the dominant effect is an indirect modification of the tensor memory through changes in the nonlinear merger dynamics, while the direct scalar contribution to the tensor memory remains suppressed by orders of magnitude for the systems considered in this work. For the largest deviations in our dataset, the final memory amplitude differs from the corresponding GR prediction by a few percent and by up to $\sim 4\%$ when compared to the GR template that minimizes the waveform mismatch in a detector-oriented analysis. We further show that including memory increases the mismatch between GR and scalar-Gauss-Bonnet waveforms by more than an order of magnitude, indicating that memory can provide complementary information for testing gravity with third-generation detectors, especially for low-mass binaries.

</details>


### [68] [New Exact Vacuum Solutions in Extended Bumblebee Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09464)
*Jie Zhu,Hao Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义bumblebee引力模型中静态球对称真空解，该模型以非最小耦合$B^2 R$和$B^μB^νR_{μν}$为特征。研究发现作用量变分与真空期望值约束施加不可交换，导致比先前探索更丰富的解空间，获得了包括裸奇点、黑洞和虫洞在内的多种解，并呈现多达十个精确解。

Method: 采用广义bumblebee引力模型，分析静态球对称真空解。通过研究作用量变分与真空期望值约束的非交换性，系统求解场方程。该方法考虑了非最小耦合项$B^2 R$和$B^μB^νR_{μν}$的完整影响。

Conclusion: 如果这种非最小耦合的矢量-张量引力（vector-tensor gravity）为宇宙提供了基本描述，那么最好由bumblebee型理论来描述，其中矢量场获得真空期望值（VEV）。研究强调了非交换性在扩展解空间中的重要作用。

Abstract: We investigate the static spherically symmetric vacuum solutions in a generalized bumblebee gravity model characterized by non-minimal couplings $B^2 R$ and $B^μB^νR_{μν}$. We demonstrate that the variation of the action and the imposition of the vacuum expectation value constraint are non-commutative, leading to a richer solution space than previously explored. A diverse set of solutions, including naked singularities, black holes, and wormholes, is obtained, and as many as ten exact solutions are presented. The thermodynamic properties of the new black hole solutions are also analyzed, and a subset of these solutions is found to have zero entropy. We argue that if such a non-minimally coupled vector-tensor gravity provides a fundamental description of the universe, it is best described by a Bumblebee-type theory, where the vector field acquires a VEV.

### [69] [Black Hole Dynamics at Fifth Post-Newtonian Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09545)
*Rafael A. Porto,Massimiliano M. Riva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究基于世界线作用量推导了第五阶后牛顿（5PN）近似下的总偶速度冲量、散射角和时间延迟，包括辐射反作用和遗传贡献。通过引入类各向同性描述，建立了从散射数据确定系统演化的框架，并利用费曼i0⁺处方分离了保守分量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立基于散射可观测量来明确表征双体动力学的框架。通过推导高阶后牛顿近似下的散射可观测量，为理解引力双体系统的完整动力学提供新途径。

Method: 采用世界线作用量（worldline action）方法，推导第五阶后牛顿（5PN）近似下的总偶速度冲量、散射角和时延。引入类各向同性描述（isotropic-like description），并利用费曼i0⁺处方（Feynman's i0⁺ prescription）分离保守分量。

Result: 获得了5PN阶的保守（各向同性）哈密顿量的普遍贡献，并确定了有效单体（Effective One Body）系数{bar d₅loc, a₆loc}。发现费曼处方与γ-3处方在重叠有效区域完全一致，但在O(G⁵ν²)阶的局部记忆类贡献符号相反。

Conclusion: 该框架为仅基于散射可观测量明确表征基础双体动力学开辟了道路。费曼处方保持了所有π²项仅来自势能区域的预期，而γ-3重路由在O(G⁶ν²)阶与此预期不相容。

Abstract: Using the worldline action in [2409.05860], we derive the total even-in-velocity (relative) impulse, scattering angle, and time delay at fifth post-Newtonian (5PN) order, including radiation-reaction and hereditary contributions at ${\cal O}(G^5ν^2)$ and ${\cal O}(G^6ν^2)$. We introduce an isotropic-like description which, together with the associated losses of energy and angular momentum, fixes the evolution of the system from scattering data. This framework opens the door to an unambiguous characterization of the underlying two-body dynamics solely in terms of scattering observables. Following [2409.05860], we isolate a conservative component using Feynman's $i0^+$ prescription. This sector contains both "tail-like" and "memory-like" contributions, the latter being nonlocal in time and described by a double Principal-Value integral. Owing to the local-in-time character of the corresponding (in-in) action, we establish a systematic procedure that is consistent with Feynman's prescription while preserving the complete local dynamics. This provides a universal contribution to the conservative (isotropic) Hamiltonian at 5PN order and, as a byproduct, also fixes the value of the Effective One Body coefficients $\{{\bar d}_{5{\rm loc}}, a_{6{\rm loc}}\}$ consistently with the Tutti-Frutti framework. For completeness, we analyse the "$γ\text{-}3$" prescription introduced in recent post-Minkowskian computations. When implemented in our formalism, we find exact agreement over the overlapping regime of validity. In contrast, Feynman's prescription yields a (local) memory-like contribution with the opposite sign at ${\cal O}(G^5ν^2)$. We also find that an analogous $γ\text{-}3$ rerouting at ${\cal O}(G^6ν^2)$ would be incompatible with the conjecture that all $π^2$ terms arise solely from the potential region, while Feynman's formulation preserves this expectation.

### [70] [Sharp description of local minima in the loss landscape of high-dimensional two-layer ReLU neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09412)
*Jie Huang,Bruno Loureiro,Stefano Sarao Mannelli*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该研究分析了两层ReLU网络在可实现的师生设置（teacher-student setting）中的总体损失景观（population loss landscape），揭示了局部极小值（local minima）具有精确的低维统计量表示，并与单次SGD（one-pass SGD）动力学建立了直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解两层ReLU网络在可实现师生设置中的损失景观特性，特别是针对常见简化假设的内在局限性，这些假设即使在最小神经网络模型中也可能忽略损失景观的本质特征。

Method: 采用可实现师生设置（realisable teacher-student setting）和高斯协变量（Gaussian covariates），研究两层ReLU网络形式为$\sum_{k=1}^K \mathrm{ReLU}(w_k^\top x)$的总体损失景观，通过统计量空间（summary statistics space）分析局部极小值的表示。

Result: 局部极小值可以通过统计量进行精确的低维表示，并与单次SGD动力学形成直接联系：局部极小值对应统计量空间中动力学的吸引不动点（attractive fixed points）。极小值呈现层次结构：在良好指定（well-specified）机制中通常孤立，但随着网络宽度增加会通过平坦方向（flat directions）连接。

Conclusion: 在过参数化（overparameterised）机制中，全局极小值（global minima）变得更容易接近，吸引动力学并减少收敛到伪解（spurious solutions）的可能性，这揭示了常见简化假设的内在局限性。

Abstract: We study the population loss landscape of two-layer ReLU networks of the form $\sum_{k=1}^K \mathrm{ReLU}(w_k^\top x)$ in a realisable teacher-student setting with Gaussian covariates. We show that local minima admit an exact low-dimensional representation in terms of summary statistics, yielding a sharp and interpretable characterisation of the landscape. We further establish a direct link with one-pass SGD: local minima correspond to attractive fixed points of the dynamics in summary statistics space. This perspective reveals a hierarchical structure of minima: they are typically isolated in the well-specified regime, but become connected by flat directions as network width increases. In this overparameterised regime, global minima become increasingly accessible, attracting the dynamics and reducing convergence to spurious solutions. Overall, our results reveal intrinsic limitations of common simplifying assumptions, which may miss essential features of the loss landscape even in minimal neural network models.

Method: 采用主动学习策略，整合密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算、热化学建模、消息传递神经网络（message-passing neural networks）和贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization），构建高通量工作流程，通过平衡化学空间探索与高性能候选物开发的方式迭代扩展训练数据集。

Result: 从超过700亿个初始候选物中建立了最大的公开CHNO炸药数据库，开发了能够准确预测爆轰性能的通用代理模型（R² > 0.98）。特征重要性分析显示氧平衡（oxygen balance）是爆轰性能的主要驱动因素，辅以局部电子结构、密度和特定官能团的贡献。

Conclusion: 该代理模型、数据库和化学见解为高通量筛选和定向发现新型含能材料提供了有价值的基础，能够探索化学空间中多样且先前未开发的区域，化学信息学分析揭示了具有相似性能指标的含能材料倾向于聚集在特定的化学空间中。

Abstract: The discovery of new energetic materials is critical for advancing technologies from defense to private industry. However, experimental approaches remain slow and expensive while computational alternatives require accurate material property inputs that are often costly to obtain, limiting their ability to efficiently predict detonation performance across a vast chemical space. We address this challenge through an active learning strategy that integrates density functional theory calculations, thermochemical modeling, message-passing neural networks, and Bayesian optimization. The resulting high-throughput workflow iteratively expands the training dataset by selecting new molecules in a targeted manner that balances the exploration of broad chemical space with the exploitation of promising high-performing candidates. This approach yields the largest publicly available database of potential CHNO explosives drawn from an initial pool of more than 70 billion candidates and a generalizable surrogate model capable of accurately predicting detonation performance (R$^2$ > 0.98). Feature importance analysis on this largest-to-date dataset reveals that oxygen balance is the dominant driver of detonation performance, complemented by contributions from local electronic structure, density, and the presence of specific functional groups. Cheminformatics analysis highlights how energetic materials with similar performance metrics tend to cluster in distinct chemical spaces offering a clearer direction for future synthesis studies. Together, the surrogate model, database, and resulting chemical insights provide a valuable foundation for high-throughput screening and targeted discovery of new energetic materials spanning diverse and previously unexplored regions of chemical space.

### [73] [Cryogenic hydrogen embrittlement of 316plus (EN 1.4420) stainless steel at 77 K and 20 K](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08751)
*W. Li,A. Zafra,L. Armendariz,Z. Wang,W. Bailey,E. Martinez-Pañeda*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在首次实验表征316plus（EN 1.4420）这种新型奥氏体不锈钢在液氢（LH2）储存中的氢-温度耦合效应。该研究填补了该材料在极端低温氢环境下性能数据的空白。

Method: 研究方法包括在室温（RT）、77K和20K下对未充氢和预充氢试样进行单轴拉伸试验。同时辅以断口分析和基于电子背散射衍射（EBSD）的应变诱发马氏体（SIM）定量分析。

Result: 316plus在77K和20K下通过增强的应变诱发马氏体（SIM）形成表现出低温强化效应。氢在室温或77K下不影响强度，但在20K时导致适度降低（约10%），仍保持在316L低温强度的上限。氢在所有温度下均导致延展性显著降低，在77K和20K时最为严重（约40-50%）。氢在20K时抑制了SIM形成，但SIM分数与延展性降低无相关性。

Conclusion: 尽管存在温度和氢的耦合效应，316plus仍保持了显著的延展性（断面收缩率约30%）。该材料在液氢储存应用中表现出良好的综合性能，特别是在极端低温氢环境下仍保持较好的塑性。

Abstract: This paper presents the first experimental characterisation of combined hydrogen-temperature effects in 316plus (EN 1.4420), a new austenitic stainless steel for liquid hydrogen (LH2) storage. Uniaxial tensile tests were conducted at room temperature (RT), 77 K and 20 K on uncharged and hydrogen-precharged specimens, complemented by fractography and EBSD-based quantification of strain-induced martensite (SIM). 316plus exhibited cryogenic strengthening at 77 K and 20 K by enhanced SIM formation. Hydrogen did not influence strength at RT or 77 K and caused a modest decrease (~10%) at 20 K, keeping 316plus at the upper bound of cryogenic strength for 316L. The presence of hydrogen resulted in significant reductions in ductility at all temperatures, being most severe at 77 and 20K (~40-50%). Hydrogen suppressed SIM at 20 K, but SIM fraction did not correlate with ductility reduction. Despite the combined effect of temperature and hydrogen, 316plus retained notable ductility (reduction in area ~30%).

### [74] [Nucleation of Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev Clusters in One Spatial Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08662)
*Hrant Topchyan,Tigran A. Sedrakyan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）相互作用如何从有效一维系统中的局域化单粒子态产生，展示了当每个局域化体积被分解为多个微观片段时，耦合分布如何趋近于标准SYK形式，并构建了SYK团簇形成的实空间唯象理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解SYK相互作用如何从具有局域化单粒子态的实际物理系统中涌现。标准SYK模型假设完全随机的全对全相互作用，但实际系统中相互作用通常具有空间结构，需要探究这种结构如何影响SYK物理的实现。

Method: 方法包括将局域相互作用投影到粗粒化的局域轨道上，然后将每个局域化体积分解为M个具有随机相位的微观片段。通过将相互作用张量映射到配对空间中的图结构，使用连通分量和团/单纯形计数来表征SYK团簇的形成、合并和增长过程。

Result: 结果显示，当M增加时，非零耦合的分布向复高斯SYK形式移动。大M极限下形成稀疏但渐近规范的SYK网络：非零耦合创建SYK团簇，而缺失或极弱耦合的模式仍由局域轨道的实空间重叠决定。

Conclusion: 该研究构建了SYK团簇形成的最小实空间唯象理论，为实验提供了清晰的标准。结果表明，通过适当分解局域化体积，即使从具有几何约束的相互作用出发，也能实现渐近的SYK物理。

Abstract: We study how Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) interactions can arise from localized single-particle states on a system that is effectively one dimensional. If a local interaction is projected onto coarse localized orbitals, the resulting couplings do not immediately follow the standard SYK distribution. Instead, they have a finite probability of being exactly zero, a broad non-Gaussian distribution for the nonzero values, and strong correlations coming from the geometry of the localized states. We then show that this changes when each localization volume is resolved into $M>1$ smaller microscopic pieces with random phases. As $M$ increases, the distribution of the nonzero couplings moves toward the complex-Gaussian SYK form. At the same time, the large-$M$ limit is a sparse but asymptotically canonical SYK network: the nonzero couplings create SYK clusters, while the pattern of missing or very weak couplings is still determined by the real-space overlap of the localized orbitals. Finally, we map the interaction tensor to a graph in pair space. This makes it possible to follow the formation, merger, and growth of SYK clusters, which we characterize using connected components and clique/simplex counts. The result is a minimal real-space phenomenological theory of SYK-cluster formation, providing clear experimental criteria.

</details>

*Haoxiang Chen,Yubing Qian,Weiluo Ren,Xiang Li,Ji Chen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文引入了一种基于模拟电荷泵浦过程的稳健方法，通过监测通量插入时极化响应的变化来确定拓扑不变量。该方法可应用于神经网络波函数框架。

Result: 应用该方法准确提取了阿贝尔分数陈绝缘体的陈数（Chern numbers），并首次基于神经网络波函数识别了反常复合费米液体态（anomalous composite Fermi liquid states）。

Abstract: Many-body topological quantum states host exotic quantum phenomena and lie at the forefront of developing next-generation quantum technologies. Recently emerged neural network wavefunction methods have established themselves as a powerful computational framework for accessing these states, enabling the variational machine learning calculation of the system's ground state wavefunction. However, reliable computation of topological invariants remains an open challenge when the whole deterministic energy spectrum is not available. In this work, we introduce a robust approach to determining topological invariant based on simulating the charge pumping process, by monitoring the response of polarization upon flux insertion. By applying this method, we accurately extract the Chern numbers for Abelian fractional Chern insulators. Our approach also enables the first neural-network-wavefunction-based identification of anomalous composite Fermi liquid states. Our work resolves a key bottleneck in applying neural network wavefunctions to correlated topological matter, and the method proposed is also generally applicable to other many-body approaches, thereby opening up new avenues for future research in this field.

### [76] [Evolution of crystal field and intraionic interactions in the ilmenite $A$IrO$_3$ ($A$ = Mg, Zn, Cd) and hyperhoneycomb $β$-ZnIrO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08934)
*Yuya Haraguchi,Hiroko Aruga Katori,Kenji Ishii,Hakuto Suzuki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）分析铱酸盐材料的局域电子结构，揭示了A位离子取代对晶体场和离子内相互作用参数的系统性影响，为理解Kitaev候选材料中局域晶体场畸变如何控制磁哈密顿量提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有$t_{2g}^5$电子构型的自旋轨道莫特绝缘体是Kitaev自旋液体的有前景平台，但需要精细调控其晶体结构以抑制非Kitaev相互作用。研究旨在通过分析ilmenite铱酸盐$A\mathrm{IrO}_3$和hyperhoneycomb $β\text{-}\mathrm{ZnIrO}_3$的局域电子结构，理解化学取代对材料性质的影响。

Method: 采用Ir $L_3$-边共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic x-ray scattering, RIXS）技术研究材料的局域电子结构。通过多重态分析（multiplet analysis）RIXS光谱，系统分析晶体场和离子内相互作用参数随A位化学取代的变化规律。

Result: 研究发现三角畸变（trigonal distortion）随A位离子半径增大而增强，这为$\mathrm{CdIrO}_3$中偏离理想$J=1/2$态和反铁磁相互作用提供了微观解释。ilmenite $\mathrm{ZnIrO}_3$和hyperhoneycomb $β\text{-}\mathrm{ZnIrO}_3$的局域多重态参数几乎相同，表明它们不同的磁基态主要受晶格结构差异而非单离子性质控制。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解Kitaev候选材料中局域晶体场畸变如何控制磁哈密顿量（magnetic Hamiltonian）建立了坚实基础，强调了晶格结构在决定材料磁性质中的关键作用。

Abstract: Spin-orbit Mott insulators with the $t_{2g}^5$ electron configuration are promising platforms for the Kitaev spin liquid, yet fine-tuning of their crystal structures is essential to suppress non-Kitaev interactions. Here, we investigate the local electronic structures of the ilmenite iridates $A\mathrm{IrO}_3$ ($A = \mathrm{Mg}, \mathrm{Zn}, \mathrm{Cd}$) and the hyperhoneycomb $β\text{-}\mathrm{ZnIrO}_3$ using Ir $L_3$-edge resonant inelastic x-ray scattering (RIXS). Multiplet analysis of the RIXS spectra reveals a systematic evolution of the crystal field and intraionic interaction parameters upon chemical substitution at the $A$-site. We observe an enhancement of the trigonal distortion with increasing $A$-site ionic radius. This provides a microscopic explanation for the deviation from the ideal $J=1/2$ state and the antiferromagnetic interactions identified in $\mathrm{CdIrO}_3$. Furthermore, the local multiplet parameters of ilmenite $\mathrm{ZnIrO}_3$ and hyperhoneycomb $β\text{-}\mathrm{ZnIrO}_3$ are found to be nearly identical, demonstrating that their different magnetic ground states are primarily governed by their distinct lattice structures rather than the single-ion properties. These findings establish a solid foundation for understanding how local crystal-field distortions control the magnetic Hamiltonian in Kitaev candidate materials.

</details>


### [77] [Superconductivity and competing orders in honeycomb $t$-$J$ model: interplay of lattice geometry and next-nearest-neighbor hopping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08937)
*Zhi Xu,Hong-Chen Jiang,Yi-Fan Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）和slave-boson平均场理论（SBMFT）方法，系统研究了蜂窝晶格上扩展的t-J模型中次近邻（NNN）电子跃迁t'和超交换耦合J'对电荷和超导（SC）性质的影响，揭示了多种竞争相的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索蜂窝晶格上扩展的t-J模型中次近邻（next-nearest-neighbor, NNN）相互作用参数t'对系统基态性质的影响，特别是对电荷有序和超导（superconducting, SC）相竞争关系的理解。

Method: 研究方法结合了大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）模拟和slave-boson平均场理论（slave-boson mean-field theory, SBMFT）。通过系统改变t'参数和圆柱几何构型（YC4-0和XC圆柱），分析不同边界条件对相稳定性的影响。

Result: DMRG结果显示：在YC4-0圆柱上，掺杂模型的基态在广泛的t'范围内表现出显著的准长程d波超导（d-wave SC），并共存着扶手椅取向的条纹相（armchair-oriented stripes, a-stripe）。超导Luttinger指数对t'呈非单调依赖，最佳t'_op∼0.4时超导最显著。相反，在XC圆柱上，t'>0.5时存在竞争的长程之字形条纹相而无超导。SBMFT分析表明a-stripe在大部分相图中是稳定构型，在δ=1/8掺杂和大t'时转变为均匀向列d波超导。

Conclusion: 结论指出两种互补方法的结果共同表明，在蜂窝晶格上掺杂的扩展t-J模型中存在一个由t'诱导的稳健超导相，该相可能在二维极限下保持稳定。边界几何构型在稳定不同竞争相中起着关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the extended $t$-$J$ model on honeycomb lattices with next-nearest-neighbor (NNN) electron hopping $t'$ and superexchange coupling $J'=(t'/t)^2 J$ using large-scale density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) simulations and slave-boson mean-field theory (SBMFT). By systematically varying $t'$ and cylinder geometries, our DMRG results reveal several competing phases with distinct charge and superconducting (SC) properties. On YC4-0 cylinders possessing bonds lying along $\vec{e}_y$ direction, the ground state of doped models exhibits pronounced quasi-long-range $d$-wave SC with coexisting armchair-oriented stripes (a-stripe) across a broad range of $t'$. Notably, the SC Luttinger exponent has a non-monotonic dependence on $t'$, showing an optimal $t'_{op}\sim0.4$ for dominant SC. Conversely, XC cylinders host a competing long-range zigzag stripes phase without SC for $t'>0.5$, highlighting the role of boundary geometry in stabilizing distinct competing phases in DMRG. To elucidate the stability of all these competing phases in 2D limit, we employ SBMFT and identify the a-stripe as the stable configuration across most of phase diagram, with a transition to uniform nematic $d$-wave SC at large $t'$ for $δ=1/8$. The combined results from two complementary approaches suggest a robust $t'$-induced SC phase that might remain stable in doped extended $t$-$J$ model on the honeycomb lattice.

</details>


### [78] [$\mathrm{U}(2)$ Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau Theory of Fractional Quantum Hall Hierarchies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09542)
*Taegon Lee,Gil Young Cho,Donghae Seo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究构建了用于描述阿贝尔（Abelian）和非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall）层级结构的有效U(2) Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau理论，统一了先前仅通过范畴数据或试探波函数描述的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论仅通过范畴数据（categorical data）或试探波函数（trial wavefunctions）描述某些分数量子霍尔层级态，缺乏统一的场论框架。本研究旨在构建一个能够同时涵盖阿贝尔和非阿贝尔层级结构的有效理论。

Method: 构建了有效的U(2) Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau理论框架，该框架能够描述基于半填充Pfaffian型母态的阿贝尔层级态，以及从阿贝尔态中涌现的非阿贝尔层级结构。

Result: 该理论框架重现了从波函数和范畴构造获得的所有填充分数（filling fractions），并唯一确定了相应的拓扑序（topological orders）。同时发现了一个有趣的粒子-空穴对称性（particle-hole symmetry），该对称性关联了两个层级序列。

Conclusion: 所构建的U(2) Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau理论为分数量子霍尔层级态提供了统一的场论描述，揭示了粒子-空穴对称性在连接不同层级序列中的关键作用，深化了对拓扑序结构的理解。

Abstract: We construct effective $\mathrm{U}(2)$ Chern-Simons-Ginzburg-Landau theories for Abelian and non-Abelian fractional quantum Hall hierarchies for those which had previously been described only through categorical data or trial wavefunctions. Our framework captures both Abelian hierarchy states built on half-filled Pfaffian-type parents and non-Abelian hierarchies emerging from Abelian states. It reproduces all filling fractions obtained from wavefunction and categorical constructions and, moreover, uniquely determines the corresponding topological orders. We also identify an intriguing particle-hole symmetry relating two hierarchy sequences, one built on a trivial insulator and the other on the $ν=1$ integer quantum Hall state, which respectively generate the Read-Rezayi sequences and their particle-hole conjugates under the same hierarchy construction.

### [79] [Exact SL(2,Z)-Structure of Lattice Maxwell Theory with $θ$-term in Modified Villain Formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08736)
*Shoto Aoki,Yoshio Kikukawa,Toshinari Takemoto*

Main category: hep-lat

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究格点Maxwell理论在修正Villain表述下的对偶性，特别关注含theta项的局域作用量的对偶变换性质，旨在解决传统方法中出现的非局域性问题。

Method: 采用修正Villain表述的格点Maxwell理论，使用含theta项的局域作用量，通过将非局域变换程序整合到S-变换定义中，消除Poisson重求和导致的非局域性。

Result: 在无磁单极子条件下，含theta项的局域作用量展现出精确的SL(2,Z)-对偶性；Wilson圈在变换中产生源于磁Wilson圈非平凡自链的非平凡相位因子，其SL(2,Z)-结构与无自旋Maxwell理论相似。

Conclusion: 通过将非局域变换程序纳入S-变换定义，成功实现了修正Villain表述下格点Maxwell理论的精确SL(2,Z)-对偶性，揭示了磁Wilson圈自链效应导致的相位因子结构。

Abstract: We study the duality of lattice Maxwell theory in a modified Villain formulation and employ an ultra-local action with a theta term. Although this action is known to become non-local under Poisson resummation, we show that this non-locality can be removed in the absence of monopoles by incorporating a non-local transformation procedure into the definition of the S-transformation. As a result, the ultra-local action with a theta term exhibits an exact SL(2,Z)-duality. We further analyze the SL(2,Z)-structure of Wilson loops, demonstrating that they transform properly up to a nontrivial phase factor arising from the nontrivial self-linking of magnetic Wilson loops. This effect originates from the non-local transformation procedure in the S-transformation. Remarkably, the resulting SL(2,Z)-structure closely resembles that of non-spin Maxwell theory.

### [80] [How does Chain of Thought decompose complex tasks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08872)
*Amrut Nadgir,Vijay Balasubramanian,Pratik Chaudhari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了语言模型分类错误随类别数量呈幂律增长，提出通过树状分解将任务拆分为多个小分类问题可显著降低错误率，并确定了思维深度的临界阈值和最优深度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多语言任务可建模为分类问题，其中大型语言模型（LLM）接收提示并从多个可能答案中选择。研究发现分类错误随类别数量呈幂律增长，这促使探索如何通过任务分解来降低错误率。

Method: 采用树状分解方法，将整体任务拆分为一系列具有相同类别数量（"度"）的较小分类问题，模拟思维链（chain-of-thought, CoT）过程。通过分析不同度值和深度下的错误率变化，识别临界阈值和最优深度。

Result: 研究发现存在一个度的临界阈值：低于该阈值时增加思维深度反而有害，高于该阈值时存在一个最小化错误的最优深度。超过该最优深度后，继续增加思维深度无法进一步降低错误率。

Conclusion: 通过树状分解将复杂分类任务拆分为多个小分类问题可显著降低预测错误，但存在度的临界阈值和最优思维深度。这一发现为优化思维链方法提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Many language tasks can be modeled as classification problems where a large language model (LLM) is given a prompt and selects one among many possible answers. We show that the classification error in such problems scales as a power law in the number of classes. This has a dramatic consequence: the prediction error can be reduced substantially by splitting the overall task into a sequence of smaller classification problems, each with the same number of classes ("degree"). This tree-structured decomposition models chain-of-thought (CoT). It has been observed that CoT-based predictors perform better when they "think'", i.e., when they develop a deeper tree, thus decomposing the problem into a larger number of steps. We identify a critical threshold for the degree, below which thinking is detrimental, and above which there exists an optimal depth that minimizes the error. It is impossible to surpass this minimal error by increasing the depth of thinking.

</details>

### [81] [Bulk-dissociated topological bands without spin-orbit coupling in hetero-dimensional superconducting metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08675)
*Joseph J. Cuozzo,Sayed A. A. Ghorashi,Dale Huber,Wei Pan,François Léonard*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该理论研究了一种由自旋极化磁性吸附原子装饰的方形超导网络，发现即使没有自旋轨道相互作用，磁性吸附原子处的局域Yu-Shiba-Rusinov束缚态也能集体形成弱拓扑超导相，并通过调节费米能实现从弱拓扑超导相到体解离拓扑超导相的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导混合异质结构中的拓扑超导体（TSCs）被深入研究以寻找用于容错量子计算的非阿贝尔任意子。然而，控制杂化是一个挑战，通常需要在增强超导邻近效应与抑制理想电子特性（如强自旋轨道相互作用）之间取得平衡。因此，探索通过材料几何设计控制拓扑性质而不依赖自旋轨道相互作用的混合超导系统具有重要意义。

Method: 本研究从理论上研究了一种由自旋极化磁性吸附原子（spin-polarized magnetic adatoms）装饰的方形超导网络（square superconducting network）。通过分析磁性吸附原子处局域化的Yu-Shiba-Rusinov束缚态（Yu-Shiba-Rusinov bound states）的集体行为，探索了在没有自旋轨道相互作用情况下的拓扑性质。

Result: 研究发现，尽管缺乏自旋轨道相互作用，磁性吸附原子处的局域Yu-Shiba-Rusinov束缚态能够集体形成弱拓扑超导相（weak topological superconducting phase）。通过调节网络的费米能量（Fermi energy），系统可以从弱拓扑超导相转变为体解离拓扑超导相（bulk-dissociated TSC phase），其中边缘态能带与体态分离，产生节点线（nodal lines）以及共存的体解离边缘和角模式（bulk-dissociated edge and corner modes）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了异维超导超材料（hetero-dimensional superconducting metamaterials）可以作为控制不同维度电子自由度耦合与解离的有用模板，为不依赖自旋轨道相互作用的拓扑超导系统设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: Topological superconductors (TSCs) in superconducting hybrid heterostructures, which integrate superconducting and non-superconducting materials, have been intensely investigated with the hope of discovering exotic non-Abelian anyons for fault-tolerant quantum computing. In this effort, a challenge for hybrid superconducting systems is controlling hybridization, which is often a balance between enhancing the superconducting proximity effect at the cost of suppressing desirable electronic properties such as strong spin-orbit interactions. Hence, discovering hybrid superconducting systems with topological properties controlled and enhanced by material geometry design without spin-orbit interactions would be intriguing to explore. In this work, we theoretically study a square superconducting network decorated with spin-polarized magnetic adatoms. We find that localized Yu-Shiba-Rusinov bound states at magnetic adatom sites collectively form a weak topological superconducting phase despite the absence of spin-orbit interactions. We then demonstrate that by tuning the Fermi energy of the network, the system can transition from a weak TSC phase to a bulk-dissociated TSC phase where the edge state bands separate from the bulk, giving rise to unexpected features such as nodal lines and co-existing bulk-dissociated edge and corner modes. Moreover, our findings highlight how hetero-dimensional superconducting metamaterials can serve as a useful template for controlling the coupling and dissociation between electronic degrees of freedom of different dimensionalities.

</details>


### [82] [Annealing-induced grain coarsening and voltage kinks in superconducting NbRe films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08735)
*Zahra Makhdoumi Kakhaki,Anton O. Pokusinskyi,Francesco Avitabile,Abhishek Kumar,Francesco Colangelo,Carla Cirillo,Carmine Attanasio,Oleksandr V. Dobrovolskiy*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比退火前后的20nm厚NbRe薄膜，发现退火处理使晶粒尺寸从2nm增至8nm，导致涡旋动力学行为发生显著变化：退火薄膜在I-V曲线中呈现多个电压拐点，这归因于正常畴的成核与生长，形成了沿晶界的涡旋通道网络。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: NbRe作为一种非中心对称超导体（non-centrosymmetric superconductor），具有高达9K的转变温度（transition temperature）和强反对称自旋轨道耦合（antisymmetric spin-orbit coupling），适用于单光子探测。虽然块体和多晶薄膜已被广泛研究，但薄膜中晶粒尺寸增大如何影响超导性和涡旋动力学（vortex dynamics）仍不清楚。

Method: 研究采用20nm厚的NbRe薄膜，对比生长态（as-grown）和退火态（annealed）样品，其中退火使平均晶粒尺寸从约2nm增加至8nm。通过在大范围温度和磁场下进行电流-电压（I-V）测量来研究涡旋动力学，并辅以时间相关的金兹堡-朗道模拟（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau simulations）进行验证。

Result: 生长态薄膜的低阻态因磁通流不稳定性（flux-flow instability）而崩溃，而退火薄膜在I-V曲线中表现出多个电压拐点（voltage kinks）。这些拐点被归因于正常畴（normal domains）的成核与生长。退火薄膜形成了沿晶界（grain boundaries）的涡旋通道路径的超导网络。

Conclusion: 退火处理改变了NbRe薄膜的微观结构，形成了具有涡旋通道的超导网络。这种结构中的局域加热和电压拐点现象可被用于离散电阻切换（discrete-resistance switching）和传感应用。

Abstract: NbRe, a non-centrosymmetric superconductor with a transition temperature $T_\mathrm{c}$ up to 9\,K, attracts interest for its strong antisymmetric spin-orbit coupling and suitability for single-photon detection. While bulk and thin-film polycrystalline NbRe are well studied, how superconductivity and vortex dynamics evolve with increasing grain size in thin films is largely unknown. Here, we investigate as-grown and annealed 20\,nm-thick NbRe films, where annealing increases the average crystallite size from approximately $2$\,nm to $8$\,nm, and study vortex dynamics via current-voltage ($I$-$V$) measurements over a broad temperature and magnetic field range. In contrast to as-grown films, where the low-resistive state breaks down due to flux-flow instability, annealed films exhibit multiple voltage kinks in the $I$-$V$ curves. We attribute these kinks to the nucleation and growth of normal domains, as further suggested by time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau simulations. Overall, the annealed films form superconducting networks with vortex-channeling paths along the grain boundaries, while localized heating and voltage kinks could be harnessed for discrete-resistance switching and sensing.

</details>


### [83] [Nonmonotonic Evolution of the Superconducting Transition Temperature and Robust Multigap Extended s-wave + s-wave Pairing in Zn-Substituted FeSe Single Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09172)
*Han-Shu Xu,Changhao Ding,Guanyin Gao,Xin Zhang,Xinyu Yin,Xucai Kan,Jiaping Hu,Wen Xie,Wensen Wei,Yuxiao Hou,Keyu An,Haoxiang Li,Kaibin Tang,Yu-Yan Han*

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了Zn掺杂FeSe单晶的超导特性，发现Tc随Zn掺杂呈非单调变化，证实了双能隙超导的鲁棒性，排除了简单杂质对破坏机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究Zn掺杂对FeSe超导体的影响，特别是掺杂浓度对超导转变温度Tc的演化机制，以及多能隙超导特性的稳定性。

Method: 通过合成宽范围Zn掺杂（x=0-0.023）的Fe1-xZnxSe单晶，采用磁化、输运和低温比热测量，分析超导转变和能隙结构。

Result: Tc随Zn掺杂呈非单调变化，低温比热数据支持由各向同性s波能隙和各向异性扩展s波能隙组成的双能隙模型，Zn替代引起的带间散射较弱。

Conclusion: 研究证实了FeSe中多能隙超导的鲁棒性，对候选配对机制施加了严格约束，强调了多带电子结构和各向异性能隙形成的重要作用。

Abstract: We report a systematic study of superconductivity on Fe1-xZnxSe single crystals synthesized over a broad Zn doping range (x = 0-0.023). High-quality single crystals across all compositions range exhibit superconducting transitions, while the transition temperature Tc shows a pronounced nonmonotonic dependence on Zn doping concentration, indicating that the underlying mechanism govering Tc its evolution cannot be explained solely by simple impurity pair breaking alone. Magnetization and transport measurements confirm the bulk behavior of superconductivity and reveal enhanced scattering effects with Zn doping. Low-temperature specific heat is consistently described by a two-gap scenario composed of an isotropic s-wave gap and an anisotropic extended s-wave gap, whereas single-gap and alternative pairing symmetries fail to describe the data. The nearly unchanged relative weights of the two gap components suggest the weak interband scattering induced by Zn substitution, thereby preserving multiband superconductivity. These results demonstrate the robustness of multigap superconductivity in FeSe and impose stringent constraints on candidate pairing mechanisms, highlighting the role of multiband electronic structure and anisotropic gap formation.

</details>


### [84] [Realistic Pearl vortices in thin film superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09440)
*Aurélien Balzli,Louk Rademaker,Giulia Venditti*

TL;DR: 该研究重新分析了薄膜超导体中涡旋的磁场分布，发现对于特定Ginzburg-Landau参数κ=1/√2的足够薄薄膜，涡旋核心周围的磁场屏蔽既非体材料中的指数衰减，也非Pearl预测的幂律衰减，而是出现随样品厚度变化的普适曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究分析了薄膜超导体中涡旋的磁场分布，特别关注具有实际Ginzburg-Landau参数κ=1/√2的足够薄薄膜，通过理论分析建立了磁场变化与样品厚度的标度关系。

Result: 发现薄膜超导体中涡旋周围的磁场屏蔽呈现普适曲线，其标度行为与样品厚度相关，厚度依赖性符合经典的Pearl长度，表明二维超导体中磁场屏蔽的减弱。研究还量化了从体材料到薄膜超导体的转变过程。

Conclusion: 研究确立了不同的屏蔽长度尺度，这些尺度对于实验数据分析至关重要，为薄膜超导体中涡旋磁场分布的实验研究提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We analyze magnetic field profiles of vortices in thin-film superconductors, shedding new light on this old and presumed settled problem. In sufficiently thin films with realistic Ginzburg-Landau parameter $κ= 1/\sqrt{2}$, the magnetic screening around a vortex core is neither exponential -- as is expected in bulk -- nor the power-law that was predicted by Pearl. Instead, a universal curve for the magnetic field variation appears that scales with the sample thickness. The thickness dependence is consistent with the seminal Pearl length, and serves as an indication of the reduced magnetic field screening present in two-dimensional superconductor. Finally, we quantify the crossover from bulk-like to thin superconductors, and establish different screening length-scales relevant for the analysis of experimental data.

### [85] [Pressure-Induced Superconducting-like Transition in the $\it d$-wave Altermagnet Candidate CsV$_2$Se$_2$O](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09457)
*Yuanzhe Li,Yilin Han,Liu Yang,Wanli He,Pengda Ye,Wencheng Huang,Jiabin Qiao,Yuemei Li,Xiaodong Sun,Tingli He,Jiayi Han,Yuxiang Chen,Ruifeng Tian,Hao Sun,Yuwei Liu,Feng Wu,Baoshan Song,Zhengtai Liu,Mao Ye,Yaobo Huang,Kenichi Ozawa,Ji Dai,Massimo Tallarida,Shengtao Cui,Jie Chen,Meiling Jin,Wayne Zheng,Chaoyu Chen,Zhiwei Wang,Zhi-Ming Yu,Xiang Li,Yugui Yao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁性（altermagnetism）产生交换型自旋劈裂而无净磁化，其d波形式与非常规d波超导的角对称性相似。这种对应关系是否直接影响真实关联材料中的超导不稳定性仍待探究。

Method: 通过实验与理论相结合的方法研究CVSO的晶格结构、电子结构和输运性质，包括常压和高压下的测量、室温X射线衍射以及磁阻演化分析。

Result: 常压下CVSO为弱绝缘母态，在约100K处存在类密度波异常，其体性质最符合G型补偿反铁磁背景。压力下类密度波特征被抑制，磁阻从负为主转为正，约3K以下出现类超导电阻下降，该异常可重复且被磁场抑制。

Conclusion: CVSO揭示了压力调控的相图，其中重构的弱绝缘母态让位于类奇异金属输运和类超导行为，呼应了包括铜酸盐和镍酸盐在内的非常规超导体的更广泛现象学。

Abstract: Altermagnetism generates exchange-type spin splitting without net magnetization and, in its $\it d$-wave form, resembles the angular symmetry of unconventional $\it d$-wave superconductivity. Whether this correspondence bears directly on superconducting instabilities in real correlated materials remains open. Here we study the quasi-two-dimensional vanadium oxychalcogenide CsV$_2$Se$_2$O (CVSO), a square-net $\it d$-wave altermagnet candidate, through combined experimental and theoretical investigation of its lattice structure, electronic structure and transport properties. At ambient pressure, CVSO is a weakly insulating parent state with a density-wave-like anomaly near 100 K, and its bulk properties are most consistent with a G-type compensated antiferromagnetic background. Under compression, the density-wave-like feature is suppressed, the magnetoresistance evolves from predominantly negative to positive, and a superconducting-like resistive downturn emerges below about 3 K. This low-temperature anomaly is reproducible across samples and pressure media, and is suppressed by magnetic field. Room-temperature X-ray diffraction reveals no symmetry lowering, whereas does show a pronounced compressibility anomaly over the same pressure range. CVSO thus reveals a pressure-tuned phase diagram in which a reconstructed weakly insulating parent state gives way to strange-metal-like transport and superconducting-like behavior, echoing broader phenomenology associated with unconventional superconductors, including cuprates and nickelates.

### [86] [Superconducting orbital diode effect in SN bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09504)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究界面电阻对超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect, SDE）的影响。此前Levichev等人的工作展示了理想界面下的SDE实现，本研究旨在分析非理想界面（具有有限电阻）如何影响该效应。

Method: 采用解析方法研究扩散超导体-正常金属（SN）双层结构在面内磁场中的行为。研究聚焦于弱层内不均匀性对应的极限情况，分析超电流沿层流动且垂直于磁场方向的配置。

Result: 研究发现SDE强度随界面电阻呈非单调依赖关系，特别是在双层厚度小于相干长度（coherence length）时。值得注意的是，非理想界面可能比理想情况更能增强SDE效应。

Conclusion: 界面电阻对超导二极管效应具有显著影响，非理想界面条件可能优化SDE性能，这为调控超导二极管器件提供了新的设计思路。

Abstract: We study the superconducting diode effect (SDE) in a diffusive superconductor - normal metal (SN) bilayer subjected to an in-plane magnetic field. The supercurrent flows along the layers, perpendicular to the field. The SDE, manifested as an asymmetry in the critical (depairing) currents and kinetic inductance for opposite current directions, arises from an orbital mechanism due to the inhomogeneous distribution of the Meissner currents caused by a spatially varying superfluid density. Recently, Levichev et al. [Phys. Rev. B 108, 094517 (2023)] demonstrated the realization of this effect in such a structure, supporting numerical calculations for an ideal interface with an experiment. In this work, we investigate the influence of a nonideal interface with finite resistance on the SDE. Employing an analytical approach, we focus on limiting cases corresponding to weak intralayer inhomogeneities. We find that the strength of the SDE depends nonmonotonically on the interface resistance when the bilayer thickness is small compared to the coherence length. Remarkably, a nonideal interface can enhance the SDE compared to the ideal case.

### [87] [High-temperature superconductivity in Nd$_{0.85}$Sr$_{0.15}$NiO$_2$ membranes under pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09525)
*Yonghun Lee,Mengnan Wang,Xin Wei,Yijun Yu,Wendy L. Mao,Yu Lin,Harold Y. Hwang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶格压缩已成为调控镍酸盐超导性的基本参数，但传统方法受限于外延稳定性极限或薄膜高压测量挑战。本研究旨在克服这些限制，探索无限层镍酸盐在更高压力下的超导行为。

Method: 开发了一种新技术，将独立式无限层（freestanding infinite-layer）Nd₀.₈₅Sr₀.₁₅NiO₂薄膜集成到金刚石压砧（diamond anvil cell）中，实现了高达~90 GPa的高压测量环境。

Result: 观察到超导转变温度（Tc）随压力显著增加，最高测量压力下在液氮温度附近出现超导下降趋势。Tc以0.65 K GPa⁻¹的速率线性增强，且无饱和迹象。

Conclusion: 无限层镍酸盐中的配对强度可通过高压提升至异常高的尺度，且该方法可广泛应用于多种二维材料，为探索高压下超导性提供了新平台。

Abstract: Lattice compression has emerged as a fundamental tuning parameter for nickelate superconductivity. Pressure acts as a trigger to induce superconductivity in bulk Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates. For infinite-layer nickelate thin films, compressive epitaxial strain and rare-earth ion chemical pressure have been used to substantially enhance the superconducting transition temperature ($T_c$). Efforts to go further have been constrained by the limits of epitaxial stability or the challenges of measuring thin films in high-pressure environments. Here, we overcome this limitation by developing a technique to incorporate freestanding infinite-layer $\mathrm{Nd_{0.85}Sr_{0.15}NiO_2}$ membranes into a diamond anvil cell. Using this platform, we observe a strong increase in $T_c$ up to our highest measurement pressure of $\sim$90 GPa, where a superconducting downturn can be observed near liquid nitrogen temperatures. Strikingly, we find a simple linear enhancement of $T_c$ at a rate of 0.65 K GPa$^{-1}$, with no signs of saturation. This suggests that the pairing strength in infinite-layer nickelates can be raised to a surprisingly high scale, using an approach that can be broadly applied to many two-dimensional materials.

### [88] [Equivariant localization for higher derivative supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08656)
*Pietro Benetti Genolini,Florian Gaar,Jerome P. Gauntlett,James Sparks*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文展示了四维N=2共形超引力（conformal supergravity）理论中存在等变闭形式（equivariantly closed forms），可用于计算具有高阶导数耦合的超引力理论中的超对称可观测量，无需求解运动方程，并在全息对偶（holography）中有应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形超引力（conformal supergravity）为研究高阶导数作用量提供了有效的离壳（off-shell）形式体系。论文旨在利用该框架计算超引力理论中的超对称可观测量（supersymmetric observables），避免求解复杂的运动方程。

Method: 论文证明四维（D=4）N=2共形超引力理论中存在等变闭形式（equivariantly closed forms）。这些形式可用于计算具有高阶导数耦合的一般超引力理论中超对称观测量的闭式表达式（closed-form expressions）。

Result: 该方法能够无需求解运动方程即可计算超对称可观测量。在全息对偶（holography）应用中，论文给出了壳上作用量（on-shell actions）的结果，这些结果推测在微扰1/N展开（perturbative 1/N expansion）中对所有阶都有效。

Conclusion: 共形超引力中的等变闭形式为计算高阶导数超引力理论中的超对称可观测量提供了强大工具，在全息对偶中具有重要应用价值，能够获得在微扰展开中全阶有效的结果。

Abstract: Conformal supergravity provides an effective off-shell formalism to study higher derivative actions. We show that the $D=4$, $\mathcal{N}=2$ theory admits equivariantly closed forms. These may be used to compute closed-form expressions for supersymmetric observables in a general class of supergravity theories with higher derivative couplings, without any need to solve equations of motion. We discuss applications to holography, presenting results for on-shell actions that are conjecturally valid to all orders in the perturbative $1/N$ expansion.

### [89] [Differential Equations for Massive Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08658)
*Daniel Baumann,Austin Joyce,Hayden Lee,Kamran Salehi Vaziri*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解德西特空间中具有通用质量的标量场波函数系数所满足微分方程的深层结构，揭示宇宙学关联函数的解析特性与组合数据之间的内在联系。

Method: 利用大质量模式函数的积分表示，将宇宙学关联函数的基础费曼积分表达为有理函数的扭积分（twisted integrals），并采用时间积分表示高效推导一阶微分方程组。

Result: 发现这些微分方程可通过图管（graph tubings）进行简单图形描述，编码基函数间的耦合和奇异性演化，从而提供推导微分方程的高效算法和边界中心视角。

Conclusion: 该组合结构为理解大质量宇宙学关联函数的解析结构提供了新视角，并在小质量和大质量极限下成功求解了微分方程组。

Abstract: We uncover a combinatorial structure governing the differential equations satisfied by wavefunction coefficients of scalar fields with generic masses in de Sitter space. Using an integral representation of the massive mode functions, we express the Feynman integrals underlying cosmological correlators as twisted integrals of rational functions. In this formulation, the integrals belong to a finite set of master integrals obeying a first-order system of differential equations, which can be derived efficiently in the time-integral representation. We show that these equations admit a simple graphical description in terms of graph tubings, which encode the couplings among basis functions and the evolution of singularities. This structure provides an efficient algorithm to derive the differential equations, and a boundary-centric perspective on massive cosmological correlators in which their analytic structure emerges from underlying combinatorial data. As an illustration, we solve the system in the limits of small and large masses.
