### [90] [A Lapse in the Cosmological Constant Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08659)
*Justin Khoury,Benjamin Muntz,Antonio Padilla*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出一种基于高维引力理论中lap函数全局约束的新机制，用于解决宇宙学常数问题。该机制在红外极限下产生类似真空能量隔离的全局约束，能够消除标准模型真空能量的所有阶辐射贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决宇宙学常数问题（cosmological constant problem），该问题涉及观测到的宇宙学常数与量子场论预测的巨大差异。受Horava-Lifshitz引力启发，通过高维时空中的全局约束机制来应对这一挑战。

Method: 采用具有各向异性标度（anisotropic scaling）的五维时空，其中额外维度紧致化，同时保持四维洛伦兹不变性（Lorentz invariance）。在深度红外极限下，通过对lap函数（lapse function）的变分产生对四维几何的全局约束，这一机制类似于真空能量隔离（vacuum energy sequestering）。

Result: 尽管所得有效引力方程与标准隔离机制不同，但标准模型（Standard Model）真空能量的所有阶辐射贡献均被消除。该机制成功实现了对量子修正的抵消，为解决宇宙学常数问题提供了新途径。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于高维引力理论中lap函数全局约束的新机制，能够有效解决宇宙学常数问题。该机制在保持四维洛伦兹不变性的同时，通过各向异性标度的额外维度实现了对真空能量辐射贡献的完全消除。

Abstract: We present a new mechanism for addressing the cosmological constant problem based on global constraints arising from a lapse function in a higher-dimensional gravitational theory. Inspired by Horava-Lifshitz gravity, we consider a 5d spacetime with anisotropic scaling along a compact extra dimension, while preserving Lorentz invariance in four dimensions. In the deep infrared limit, variation with respect to the lapse generates a global constraint on the 4d geometry, closely analogous to that of vacuum energy sequestering. Although the resulting effective gravitational equations differ from standard sequestering, radiative contributions to the Standard Model vacuum energy are nevertheless cancelled at all orders.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为具有守恒诺特荷的初始态的量子隧穿过程提供完整的第一性原理讨论，解决现有方法中假设不透明和特设性推广的问题。

Method: 结合直接方法和稳态子（steadyon）框架评估实时路径积分，提出了简单明确的欧几里得时间处方（Euclidean-time prescription），并推广到多维度和任意守恒诺特荷的情况。

Result: 建立了计算此类系统隧穿率的清晰框架，解释了复鞍点（complex saddle points）的出现机制，验证了先前技术假设，并首次给出了同时具有守恒荷和非平凡能量初始态的结果。

Conclusion: 该研究为有限密度和电荷不对称系统中的隧穿率计算提供了可靠基础，方法具有透明性和普适性，适用于复杂标量场等物理系统。

Abstract: We provide a complete first-principles based discussion of quantum tunnelling out of initial states carrying a conserved Noether charge. Our main result is a simple, unambiguous Euclidean-time prescription for the calculation of tunnelling rates out of such states. By relying on a combination of the direct approach and the steadyon framework for the evaluation of real-time path integrals, our derivation offers full transparency of its underlying assumptions, and is independent of any ad-hoc generalisations. This strategy also offers a simple explanation for the emergence of complex saddle points for such systems, justifying techniques postulated by earlier works. Our analysis furthermore offers the first results for initial states with both a conserved Noether charge and a non-trivial energy.
  We first illustrate the main conceptual points of our analysis for the simple example of a point particle in two spatial dimensions carrying a conserved angular momentum. Then, we generalise our results to the case of multiple dimensions and an arbitrary conserved Noether charge, providing an easy-to-implement prescription for the calculation of the tunnelling rate. We furthermore apply our results to the example of a complex scalar field subject to a global U(1)-symmetry with associated charge. These results provide a reliable foundation for the calculation of tunnelling rates in applications in finite-density and charge-asymmetric systems.

### [92] [Effective strings and particles interacting in 3D: the Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08670)
*J. M. Viana Parente Lopes,José Matos,Joao Penedones*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了三维空间中涨落畴壁（fluctuating domain wall）如何影响带隙相（gapped phase）中的体观测量（bulk observables），建立了畴壁与最轻体质量模（lightest bulk massive mode）间的有效相互作用，并在特定运动学区域（kinematic regime）验证了其普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解三维涨落畴壁对带隙相中体观测量的修正机制，特别是畴壁与体激发态（bulk excitations）之间的相互作用如何影响系统的物理性质。

Method: 方法包括引入畴壁与最轻体质量模间的有效相互作用描述，识别该描述受控的运动学区域：沿壁方向动量（momentum along the wall）较小、接近壳上（nearly on-shell）的体交换过程。通过重整化群（renormalization group）分析确定普适耦合常数λ。

Result: 结果表明，在特定运动学区域下，畴壁自由能（wall free energy）的大L_z修正和存在畴壁时两点函数（two-point functions）的大|x_⊥|尾部均由重整化无量纲耦合λ控制。而单点函数（one-point functions）和近邻区域两点函数仍保留对算符数据（operator data）和体谱密度（bulk spectral density）的非普适依赖。

Conclusion: 结论证实了畴壁涨落的普适运动学效应，包括粗糙壁展宽（rough-wall broadening）和近邻高斯行为（nearby Gaussian behavior），这些预测在具有反周期边界条件（anti-periodic boundary conditions）的三维伊辛模型（3D Ising model）蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）中得到良好验证。

Abstract: We study how a fluctuating domain wall in three dimensions modifies bulk observables in a gapped phase. We introduce an effective interaction between the wall and the lightest bulk massive mode, and identify the regime in which this description is controlled: nearly on-shell bulk exchange with small momentum along the wall. In this regime, several observables are controlled by a renormalized dimensionless coupling $λ$, including the large-$L_z$ correction to the wall free energy and the large-$|x_\perp|$ tail of two-point functions in the presence of the wall. Other observables, such as one-point functions and two-point functions in the nearby-regime, retain non-universal dependence on operator data and on the bulk spectral density. We test the universal kinematic consequences of wall fluctuations, and find good agreement with the predicted rough-wall broadening and nearby Gaussian behavior in Monte Carlo simulations of the 3D Ising model with anti-periodic boundary conditions.

</details>


### [93] [Classification of 2D Fermionic Systems with a $\mathbb Z_2$ Flavor Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09503)
*Chi-Ming Chang,Jin Chen,Fengjun Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文对描述二维费米子系统（具有通用费米子宇称对称性和额外Z₂味道对称性）的超融合范畴（superfusion categories）进行了分类，得到16个一致的超融合范畴，并用三个Z₈异常类不变量进行标记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在分类描述二维费米子系统的超融合范畴，这些系统具有由拓扑缺陷线（TDL）Z实现的通用费米子宇称对称性，以及由W TDL生成的额外Z₂味道对称性。

Method: 根据W是m型还是q型，其融合规则（fusion rules）分为三个不同类别，通过求解超五边形方程（super-pentagon equations）获得一致的超融合范畴。

Result: 研究得到了16个一致的超融合范畴，用不变量(ν_W,ν_Z,ν_{WZ})标记，这些不变量决定了由W、Z和WZ生成的对称性的Z₈异常类（anomaly classes）。

Conclusion: 研究提供了使用多个马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermions）的明确实现，并讨论了其对费米子共形场论（fermionic CFTs）和能隙相（gapped phases）的影响。

Abstract: We classify superfusion categories describing two-dimensional fermionic systems equipped with the universal fermion-parity symmetry, implemented by a topological defect line (TDL) $Z$, and an additional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ flavor symmetry generated by a $W$ TDL. Depending on whether $W$ is m-type or q-type, its fusion rules lead to three distinct classes, and solving the super-pentagon equations yields 16 consistent superfusion categories. These are labeled by invariants $(ν_W,ν_Z,ν_{WZ})$, which determine the $\mathbb{Z}_8$ anomaly classes of the symmetries generated by $W$, $Z$, and $WZ$. We also provide explicit realizations using multiple Majorana fermions and comment on implications for fermionic CFTs and gapped phases.

### [94] [Reduced superblocks at next-to-next-to-extremality for all half-maximally supersymmetric CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08673)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用arXiv:hep-th/0405180中引入的超共形Ward恒等式（superconformal Ward identity）解基。通过该方法，将混合关联函数中的动力学数据编码到更简单的"约化关联函数"（reduced correlator）中，这些约化函数允许块展开（block expansion）。

Result: 证明了极值性E=2的混合关联函数动力学数据可编码在约化关联函数中。这些约化块（reduced blocks）涉及具有移动运动学的普通块，在4d中重现已知结果，推广了6d中的已知例子，并在3d和5d中提供了新结果。

Conclusion: 约化关联函数方法成功统一了不同维度超共形场论中混合关联函数的分析，与arXiv:2601.15407中最大超对称CFTs的结果类似。该方法为3d和5d理论提供了新的解析工具。

Abstract: We consider mixed four-point correlators of 1/2-BPS operators $φ_{k}$ in SCFTs with eight real Poincaré supercharges, namely the 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$, 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$, 5d $\mathcal{N}=1$, and 6d $\mathcal{N}=(1,0)$ theories. Using the basis of solutions to the superconformal Ward identity introduced in arXiv:hep-th/0405180, we demonstrate that the dynamical data in mixed correlators of extremality $\mathcal{E}=2$ is encoded in certain simpler ``reduced correlator" functions that admit a block expansion, in close analogy to the recent result for maximally supersymmetric CFTs in arXiv:2601.15407. These reduced blocks similarly involve ordinary blocks with shifted kinematics and reproduce what is known in 4d, generalize a known example in 6d, and offer novel results in 3d and 5d.

### [95] [Harmonic Analysis of the Instanton Prepotential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08725)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究卡拉比-丘模空间离散对称性（由同构翻转生成）对4D N=2 Type IIA预势瞬子展开的约束作用，探索预势展开的数学结构与物理意义。

Method: 构建基于Coxeter不变对称双线性形式的拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子，证明预势组织成的Coxeter不变函数是该算子的本征函数。对于二面体Coxeter群（dihedral Coxeter groups），通过本征值方程的变量分离解释特殊函数出现的原因。

Result: Gromov-Witten展开可解释为在模空间Coxeter商上传播的波的叠加，其重求和（resummation）对应谱分解（spectral decomposition）。对于二面体群，根据Coxeter旋转作用类型（双曲、椭圆、抛物），分别出现修正贝塞尔函数（modified Bessel functions）、普通贝塞尔函数和雅可比θ函数（Jacobi theta functions）。

Conclusion: 所得谱表示在模空间内部高效收敛，补充了标准大体积瞬子展开，为理解预势的数学结构提供了新视角，建立了瞬子展开与谱理论之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: Discrete symmetries of Calabi-Yau moduli spaces, generated by isomorphic flops, constrain the instanton expansion of the 4D $\mathcal{N}=2$ Type~IIA prepotential. We show that the Coxeter-invariant functions into which the prepotential organizes are eigenfunctions of a Laplace-Beltrami operator built from the Coxeter-invariant symmetric bilinear form on the moduli space. This means that the Gromov-Witten expansion can be interpreted as a superposition of waves propagating on the Coxeter quotient of the moduli space, and its resummation is the corresponding spectral decomposition. For the dihedral Coxeter groups, separation of variables in the eigenvalue equation explains from first principles why special modified Bessel functions, ordinary Bessel functions and Jacobi theta functions appear as the natural building blocks of the prepotential, depending on whether the Coxeter rotation acts hyperbolically, elliptically, or parabolically. The resulting spectral representations converge efficiently in the interior of the moduli space, complementing the standard large-volume instanton expansion.

Conclusion: 研究证实了通过规范连续对称性获得的奇异拓扑界面在离散化后仍然存在，并揭示了非紧致边缘模与连续缺陷谱、无限量子维度之间的关联。在有理半径情况下，通过适当修改可以实现边缘模的紧致化，获得具有有限量子维度的标准缺陷结构。

Abstract: We analyze non-invertible topological interfaces and defects in the two-dimensional compact boson, focusing on the more exotic ones obtained by gauging continuous symmetries with flat connections on a half-space. These include interfaces between mutually irrational radii and T-duality symmetries at arbitrary boson radius. Using the modified Villain discretization on both a Euclidean two-dimensional square lattice and a quantum one-dimensional chain, we show that all these topological interfaces survive discretization and give rise to non-compact edge modes localized at the defect sites. Such non-compact edge modes imply a continuous defect spectrum and an infinite quantum dimension. In the special case of rational radii, we show how the defect action or Hamiltonian can be modified in order to compactify the edge modes and produce more standard defects with finite quantum dimension.

Abstract: This paper is an extension of the results presented in \cite{Guarino:2024gke}. We show that this construction is key to building pure supergravities around a supersymmetric AdS$_D$ solution. We illustrate this construction by building a consistent $\mathcal{N}=4$ subsector of the $D=4$ $\mathcal{N}=8$ $[\mathrm{SO}(6)\times \mathrm{SO}(1,1)]\ltimes \mathbb{R}^{12}$ gauged supergravity. We use this result to build the uplift of the multicharge spindle solutions in type IIB and we define a simple criterion for assessing the regularity of the uplift. We show that the type IIB uplift of the spindle is always non-regular, admitting eight codimension-six orbifold singularities. We apply the same criterion to other spindle uplifts, recovering known results and making predictions on the regularity of spindles on (quasi-)regular SE$_7$ manifolds.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 闵可夫斯基时空在(3+1)维投影霍拉瓦引力中存在红外不稳定性，为保持现象学可行性，需要探索该不稳定性演化为静态低曲率解的可能性，而非仅被宇宙膨胀等时间演化过程所掩盖。

Method: 研究作用量中高阶导数项是否能够导致存在具有平面对称性的静态非均匀周期解，类似磁性材料中的调制相；同时分类所有静态均匀各向同性解及具有平面对称性的解。

Result: 发现此类静态非均匀周期解不存在；所有分类的静态解均无法作为闵可夫斯基不稳定性演化的终点，这支持了不稳定性被时间演化过程所掩盖的假设。

Conclusion: 闵可夫斯基不稳定性无法演化为任何静态解作为终点，这进一步支持了不稳定性被哈勃膨胀等时间演化过程所掩盖的研究方向，并暗示了对重整化群流红外特性的现象学约束。

Abstract: Minkowski spacetime exhibits infrared instability in projectable Ho\v rava gravity in (3+1) dimensions. To be phenomenologically viable, the instability should be either hidden by other time-dependent processes such as the Hubble expansion of the universe and the Jeans instability, or evolve into another static solution with low average curvature. While the former scenario leads to a phenomenological constraint on the infrared properties of the renormalization group flow, this paper explores the latter possibility. We study if the presence of higher derivative terms in the action can lead to existence of static, inhomogeneous (quasi-) periodic solutions with planar symmetry, similar to modulated phases in magnetic materials. We find that such solutions do not exist. In doing so, we classify all static homogeneous and isotropic solutions and solutions with planar symmetry. We provide arguments that none of them can serve as an endpoint for the evolution of the Minkowski instability. This motivates further study of the scenario where the instability is concealed by time evolution.

</details>

A D2-brane probe perceives $Φ(w)$ as an $\mathcal{N}=2$ deformation of its 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ affine Dynkin quiver gauge theory via polynomial and monopole superpotential terms. By exploiting 3d mirror symmetry, we obtain an effective theory that correctly reproduces the quiver-collapsing mechanism known in the mathematical literature. We present several examples, including non-toric and non-resolvable cases.

### [104] [Relativistic single-electron wavepacket in quantum electromagnetic fields II: Quantum radiation emitted by a uniformly accelerated electron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09456)
*Shih-Yuin Lin,Bei-Lok Hu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究计算了相对论性单电子波包在电磁场闵可夫斯基真空中的量子辐射，发现静止电子波包的量子辐射精确为零，而匀加速电子的量子辐射功率在长时间区域呈现长期增长，这种增长具有经典解释且不会发散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过考虑电动力学原始非线性作用量中的三次项来计算量子辐射的主导阶贡献，分析静止和匀加速电子波包的辐射特性，并探讨长时间区域的行为。

Conclusion: 量子辐射的长期增长具有经典解释且不会发散，而在电子显微镜中探测Unruh效应的实验提案中，经典辐射"盲点"的量子修正主要贡献来自横向偏差关联子，且与Unruh效应无关。

Abstract: We compute the quantum radiation emitted by wavepackets of relativistic single electrons, both at rest and undergoing uniform acceleration in the Minkowski vacuum of the electromagnetic field. We find that the cubic terms in the original nonlinear action of electrodynamics should be considered in obtaining the quantum radiation to the leading order. We show that the quantum radiation from a single-electron wavepacket at rest vanishes exactly. For a uniformly accelerated electron, the quantum radiated power has secular growth in the long-time regime. We demonstrate that this secular growth has a classical interpretation, and argue that the resummed quantum radiation at late times would not diverge. Regarding experimental proposals for the detection of the Unruh effect from the quantum radiation in the `blind spots' of classical radiation we ascertain that quantum corrections in the two blind spots are fully contributed by the transverse deviation correlators, where the dominant contributions are irrelevant to the Unruh effect in electron microscopes.

In this paper, we follow the recently developed action principle for Lie-Poisson electrodynamics to derive the conservation laws of the theory. The energy-momentum tensor is obtained, along with the conserved electric charge and the momentum operator. We consider non-interacting examples for real and complex scalar fields, as well as the Dirac field, within the $κ$-Minkowski spacetime framework. ### [107] [Black hole thermodynamics is around the corner](https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.04499)
*Gerui Chen,Wei Guo,Xin Lan,Hongbao Zhang,Wei Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究提出使用带角（corner）而非锥形奇点（conical singularity）的欧几里得黑洞解，证明了Wald熵公式在一般F(R_abcd)引力理论中的可推导性，并利用特殊微分同胚直接导出了洛伦兹号差下与视界法向Killing矢量场共轭的ADM哈密顿量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用带角（corner）的欧几里得黑洞解，通过比较不含角项和作用量（action without the corner term）与含角项作用量（action with the corner term）的等价性，利用一阶变分（first order variation）推导Wald熵公式。进一步运用特殊微分同胚（special diffeomorphism）进行推导。

Result: 成功证明对于一般F(R_abcd)引力理论，Wald黑洞熵公式（Wald formula for black hole entropy）可直接从两种作用量的等价性推导得出。在洛伦兹号差（Lorentz signature）下，直接导出了与视界法向Killing矢量场共轭的ADM哈密顿量（ADM Hamiltonian），该量在巨正则系综（grand canonical ensemble）中作为逆温度（inverse temperature）的共轭变量。

Conclusion: 使用带角的欧几里得黑洞解为推导广义引力理论中的黑洞熵公式提供了更直接的方法，通过作用量等价性和特殊微分同胚技术，实现了Wald公式的简洁推导以及ADM哈密顿量的直接计算。

Abstract: We propose to work on the Euclidean black hole solution with a corner rather than with the prevalent conical singularity. As a result, we find that the Wald formula for black hole entropy can be readily obtained for generic $F(R_{abcd})$ gravity by using both the action without the corner term and the action with the corner term due to their equivalence to the first order variation. With such an equivalence, we further make use of a special diffeomorphism to accomplish a direct derivation of the ADM Hamiltonian conjugate to the Killing vector field normal to the horizon in the Lorentz signature as a conjugate variable of the inverse temperature in the grand canonical ensemble.

</details>

Abstract: We report on the high-pressure synthesis of a CrS$_2$ phase in the form of single-crystalline nanorods. Ab initio density functional theory calculations of the relaxed structure confirm the stability of this structure and indicate a strong overlap of the 3d states of Cr with the 3p states of S, thus suggesting strong covalent Cr-S bonds and metallic behavior. Electrical resistivity, $\varrho$, measurements on single nanorods confirm this behavior and yield $\varrho \sim 2-20$ m$Ω$ cm at 4 K. The proposed ladder-like structure of CrS$_2$ forms open channels along the chain direction, which may be suitable for ionic conduction.

### [109] [Pressure-stabilized dual-BCC polymorphism in a rhenium-based high-entropy alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08770)
*Raimundas Sereika,Andrew D. Pope,Hunter Kantelis,Caleb M. Knight,Kallol Chakrabarty,Yogesh K. Vohra*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵合金中亚稳态结构状态的调控为材料性能定制提供了有前景的途径，但利用高压工程化这类状态的研究仍显不足。本研究旨在探索压力如何有效调控化学复杂合金的平坦自由能景观。

Method: 采用高压驱动合成方法，对近等摩尔ReNbTiZrHf合金进行压缩处理。初始材料为六方（C14衍生）相和体心立方（BCC）相的两相混合物，通过压缩诱导六方相发生选择性、无扩散转变。

Conclusion: 研究表明压力能有效调控化学复杂合金的平坦自由能景观，为耐火高熵合金（refractory HEAs）的多晶型工程和亚稳态相设计建立了稳健的途径。

Abstract: Accessing metastable structural states in high-entropy alloys offers a promising route to tailor material properties, yet the use of high pressure to engineer such states remains underexplored. Here, we report the pressure-driven synthesis of a unique metastable dual-BCC microstructure in a near-equimolar ReNbTiZrHf alloy. Starting from an ambient two-phase mixture of hexagonal (C14-derived) and body-centered cubic (BCC) phases, compression induces a selective, diffusionless transformation of the hexagonal constituent into a second, crystallographically distinct BCC polymorph, while the original BCC phase remains stable. Upon decompression, the pressure-induced BCC phase is kinetically trapped, yielding a dual-BCC state that is inaccessible via conventional thermal processing. The pressure-stabilized BCC polymorph is Re-enriched and inherits the exceptional stiffness of its hexagonal parent (bulk modulus ~290 GPa), creating a composite microstructure with pronounced elastic and mechanical contrast relative to the softer original BCC matrix (~180 GPa). These findings demonstrate that pressure can effectively navigate the flat free-energy landscapes of chemically complex alloys, establishing a robust pathway for polymorph engineering and metastable phase design in refractory HEAs.

### [110] [Including sample shape in micromagnetics with 3D periodic boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08777)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先提供了形式化证明，表明对于足够大的磁性样品，仅平均磁化强度（average magnetisation）产生不可忽略的形状效应。基于这一洞见，对现有实现进行了简单而计算高效的修改，将形状效应纳入周期性边界条件方法中。

Result: 开发了一种改进的周期性边界条件实现方法，该方法能够有效处理形状效应，同时保持计算效率，特别适用于模拟域与样品形状不匹配的情况。

Conclusion: 通过理论证明和算法改进，本文提供了一种更高效、更灵活的周期性边界条件计算方法，解决了传统准周期性宏观几何方法在计算效率和形状匹配方面的局限性。

Abstract: Periodic boundary conditions (PBCs) for computing magnetic fields in repeating magnetic structures, e.g. in micromagnetic simulations, are typically imposed using the quasi periodic macrogeometry approach, where many copies of the simulated domain are introduced. In this work, we present a formal proof that for sufficiently large magnetic samples, only the average magnetisation gives non-negligible shape effects. Using this insight, we develop a simple, computationally efficient modification of existing implementations which incorporates shape effects in PBC methods.

Motivation: 理解纳米孔洞-溶质复合体（nanovoid-solute complexes）的结构和能量学对于阐明金属中缺陷的耦合演化至关重要，但其庞大而复杂的构型空间对传统方法构成了主要挑战。

Method: 以W-Re为代表性体系，将溶质在纳米孔洞表面的偏聚分解为直接相互作用和孔洞介导的溶质-溶质相互作用。基于第一性原理数据训练机器学习模型，将局部配位基元映射到其能量学，并开发了尺寸依赖的构型搜索框架，分别使用穷举枚举、模拟退火和贪心添加算法处理不同尺寸的复合体。

Result: 该框架构建了大型数据库，揭示了Re的阶梯状偏聚行为（staircase-like segregation behavior），并推导出基于Re表面覆盖率的简单判据用于快速能量预测。研究还建立了Re偏聚与空位介导的纳米孔洞演化之间的联系，并为现有模型和经验势提供了基准。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个物理透明、准确且可迁移的框架，用于研究金属中纳米孔洞-溶质的协同演化，为多尺度模拟提供了可靠的能量输入。扩展到Os和Ta支持了局部配位基元概念的普适性，预测的溶质偏聚行为与一系列实验观察结果一致。

Abstract: Understanding the structures and energetics of nanovoid-solute complexes is essential for elucidating the coupled evolution of defects in metals. Yet their vast and complex configurational space poses a major challenge to conventional approaches. Using W-Re as a representative system, we demonstrate that solute segregation at nanovoid surfaces can be decomposed into direct nanovoid-solute interactions and nanovoid-mediated solute-solute interactions. Both are governed by local coordination motifs, with identical motifs giving nearly identical energetics. Based on first-principles data, we trained machine-learning models to map diverse local motifs to their energetics, enabling the energetics of any nanovoid-solute complex to be reconstructed from a finite set of constituent local motifs. We further developed a size-dependent configurational-search framework to efficiently identify thermodynamically stable structures, using exhaustive enumeration, simulated annealing, and greedy addition for small, medium-sized, and large complexes, respectively. This framework enabled the construction of a large database, revealed the staircase-like segregation behavior of Re, and derived a simple criterion based on Re surface coverage for rapid energy prediction across a wide size range. It also links Re segregation to vacancy-mediated nanovoid evolution and provides benchmarks for existing models and empirical potentials. Extensions to Os and Ta support the generality of the local-motif concept, and the predicted segregation behavior of solutes at nanovoids agrees with a range of experimental observations. This work establishes a physically transparent, accurate, and transferable framework for studying nanovoid-solute co-evolution in metals and provides reliable energetic inputs for multiscale simulations.

Method: 研究预测了一种高压层状三元相RbBF5，其中12配位的截角立方体状（truncated-cube-like）氟配位环境打破了局部对称性，通过轨道分裂（orbital splitting）选择性提升了面内Rb 4px,y能级。

Result: 对称性降低的配位模式激活了Rb的4p内层电子，使其能级接近F的2p能带，实现了内层电子参与Rb-F成键并在压缩条件下稳定存在。

Conclusion: 这种对称性降低的配位基序（symmetry-lowering coordination motif）为激活其他碱金属（如K和Cs）的内层p态提供了一般机制，将内层化学扩展到更轻的主族元素，并为高压下非常规成键和氧化态的设计提供了原理。

Abstract: While the high oxidation states in heavy alkali fluorides (Cs, Ba, Ra) have been attributed to a pressure-driven upshift of energy level of inner p states, this route is largely ineffective for Rb because its smaller ionic radius suppresses the required level rise even under strong compression. Here, we predict a high-pressure layered ternary phase, RbBF5, in which 12-fold truncated-cube-like F coordination around Rb breaks local symmetry and activates the Rb 4p inner shell. The resulting orbital splitting selectively elevates the in-plane Rb 4px,y levels toward the F 2p manifold, enabling inner-shell participation and stabilizing Rb-F bonding under compression. More broadly, this symmetry-lowering coordination motif may provide a general mechanism for activating inner-shell p states in other alkali metals (e.g., K and Cs inner p states). These findings extend inner-shell chemistry to lighter main-group elements and establish a design principle for accessing unconventional bonding and oxidation states at high pressure.

### [113] [Higher-order topological insulators in two-dimensional antiferromagnetic and altermagnetic chromium-based group-IV chalcogenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08907)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合理论分析的方法，研究了一系列单层铬基IV族硫属化合物（CrCX3和CrSiS3）及其Janus化合物（Cr2C2S3Se3和Cr2Si2S3Se3）。分析包括自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）效应的影响。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了二维反铁磁和交变磁系统中高阶拓扑与磁序之间的内在联系，确认铬基IV族硫属化合物单层是探索高阶拓扑相及其在拓扑和自旋电子学中潜在应用的有前景平台。

Abstract: Based on first-principles calculations combined with theoretical analysis, we identify a family of monolayer chromium-based group-IV chalcogenides as a new class of two-dimensional (2D) magnetic higher-order topological insulators (HOTIs). Specifically, the CrC$X_3$ ($X=$ S, Se, Te) and CrSiS$_3$ monolayers are found to host conventional antiferromagnetic ground states with $\mathcal{PT}$ symmetry, whereas the Janus compounds Cr$_2$C$_2$S$_3$Se$_3$ and Cr$_2$Si$_2$S$_3$Se$_3$ exhibit altermagnetic ground states. We demonstrate that all these monolayer magnetic materials realize 2D HOTI phases, in which the nontrivial topology is protected by lattice $C_3$ rotational symmetry and manifests as zero-dimensional corner states carrying quantized fractional charges. Moreover, upon inclusion of spin-orbit coupling, these systems remain in the HOTI phase and continue to host robust corner-localized states, confirming the stability of their higher-order topological nature. Our results reveal an intrinsic connection between higher-order topology and magnetic order in 2D antiferromagnetic and altermagnetic systems, identifying chromium-based group-IV chalcogenide monolayers as promising platforms for exploring higher-order topological phases and their potential relevance for future topological and spintronic applications.

### [114] [Grain Growth Kinetics in (Cr,Mo,Ta,V,W)C1-δ High-Entropy Carbide Ceramics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08961)
*Ali Sarikhani,Gregory E. Hilmas,David W. Lipke,Douglas E. Wolfe,Stefano Curtarolo,Shen J. Dillon,Ahmad Mirzaei,William G. Fahrenholtz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用放电等离子烧结技术，在1750-1950°C温度范围内保持10分钟恒温时间，以分离温度对微观结构演变的影响；使用正常晶粒生长模型（normal grain growth model）分析晶粒生长动力学，假设生长指数n=3。

Result: 随着烧结温度升高，晶粒生长加剧且晶格参数增加，同时保持单相岩盐结构（rock salt structure）；元素映射显示Ta偏析（segregation）随温度升高而减少，表明高温下化学均匀化增强；阿伦尼乌斯分析（Arrhenius analysis）得到约620 kJ mol-1的表观活化能，与难熔过渡金属碳化物中的扩散控制过程相当。

Conclusion: 研究建立了碳化物系统中致密化温度、晶粒生长和扩散动力学之间的定量关系，为高熵超高温碳化物陶瓷的微观结构稳定性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Understanding grain-boundary mobility during spark plasma sintering can enable microstructure control in high-entropy carbides, yet quantitative grain-growth kinetics remain scarce. In this work, grain growth kinetics and densification behavior were investigated for single-phase fully dense (Cr,Mo,Ta,V,W)C1-δ high-entropy carbide ceramics. Specimens were densified by spark plasma sintering for a constant dwell time of 10 min at temperatures between 1750 °C and 1950 °C to isolate the role of temperature on microstructural evolution. Increasing sintering temperature produced grain growth and increased lattice parameter, while maintaining a single-phase rock salt structure. Elemental mapping showed a progressive reduction of Ta segregation with increasing sintering temperature, suggesting enhanced chemical homogenization at elevated temperatures. Grain growth kinetics were analyzed using a normal grain growth model with an assumed growth exponent of n=3, physically reasonable for grain-boundary-controlled growth influenced by solute and vacancy pinning. Arrhenius analysis of the growth factor yielded an apparent activation energy of approximately 620 kJ mol-1, comparable to diffusion-controlled processes in refractory transition-metal carbides. Densification curves revealed rapid consolidation prior to reaching the peak temperature followed by temperature-dominated grain coarsening. These results establish quantitative relationships between densification temperature, grain growth, and diffusion kinetics in a carbide system, providing insight into the microstructural stability of high-entropy, ultra-high-temperature carbide ceramics.

### [115] [Selective Random Structure Search (SRSS): Unbiased Exploration of Polymorphs in Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08972)
*Jiexi Song,Diwei Shi,Aixian She,Chongde Cao,Fengyuan Xuan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出选择性随机结构搜索（Selective Random Structure Search, SRSS）框架，这是一种高通量、无偏的晶体结构预测方法，能够发现传统方法可能忽略的亚稳态多形体（metastable polymorphs）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统晶体结构预测方法依赖基于原型的种子生成（prototype-based seeding），这种方法通常偏向已知的低能区域，而忽略了具有非常规对称性的亚稳态多形体（metastable polymorphs）。

Method: SRSS结合了对称性约束的随机生成（symmetry-constrained random generation）、基于特征的多样性选择（feature-based diversity selection），以及通过通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine-learning interatomic potentials, uMLIPs）实现的快速弛豫和稳定性评估。

Result: 应用于多种体系（包括块体SiC和BaPtAs、二维层状化合物NbSe2、一维纳米管GaN）时，SRSS成功恢复了已知基态，同时发现了许多先前未报道的动态稳定多形体，如复杂的笼状SiC多型体、超出实验记录的低能BaPtAs多形体、二维NbSe2的半导体正交相，以及不同的扶手椅/锯齿形GaN纳米管。

Conclusion: SRSS建立了一个稳健、可扩展的平台，用于绘制完整的晶体稳定性图谱，弥合了穷举搜索与计算可行性之间的差距。整个工作流程在标准CPU资源上高效运行，无需GPU加速，证明了即使在资源有限的环境中也能进行严格的、无假设的多形体发现。

Abstract: Crystal structure prediction has traditionally relied on prototype-based seeding, approaches that often bias sampling toward known low-energy basins and overlook metastable polymorphs with unconventional symmetries. Here, we introduce Selective Random Structure Search (SRSS), a high-throughput, unbiased framework designed to explore the configurational space of crystalline materials across all dimensions. SRSS combines symmetry-constrained random generation with feature-based diversity selection and rapid relaxation and stability evaluation via universal machine-learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs). Applied to diverse systems, including bulk system SiC and BaPtAs, 2D layered compounds NbSe2, and 1D nanotubes GaN, SRSS successfully recovers known ground states while revealing numerous previously unreported, dynamically stable polymorphs. Notable discoveries include complex cage-like SiC polytypes, low-energy BaPtAs polymorphs beyond experimental records, a semiconducting orthorhombic phase of 2D-NbSe2, and distinct armchair/zigzag GaN nanotubes. Crucially, the entire workflow operates efficiently on standard CPU resources without GPU acceleration, demonstrating that rigorous, hypothesis-free polymorph discovery is accessible even in resource-limited settings. SRSS thus establishes a robust, scalable platform for mapping the full landscape of crystal stability, bridging the gap between exhaustive search and computational feasibility.

Method: 该方法采用基于元动力学（metadynamics-based, MetaD-based）的框架，具体使用并行偏置元动力学与分区族（parallel bias MetaD with partitioned families, PB MetaDPF）技术。通过多峰策略（multi-hill strategy）利用晶体学对称性，提高了方法的效率和有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的基于元动力学的方法能够有效构建晶体空位动力学的自由能面，无需明确定义空位坐标或引入强控制参数，并通过多峰策略提高了计算效率，为研究晶体扩散过程提供了新工具。

Abstract: We propose a metadynamics-based (MetaD-based) approach for constructing the free energy surface (FES) of vacancy dynamics in crystals. In this approach, the vacancy FES can be constructed without explicitly defining a unique vacancy coordinate or introducing a set of parameters that strongly govern the FES topology, enabled by parallel bias MetaD with partitioned families (PB MetaDPF). In addition, the proposed approach is made more efficient and effective through a multi-hill strategy that exploits crystallographic symmetry. We demonstrate the validity of the proposed approach through applications to self-diffusion and impurity diffusion via monovacancies and divacancies in metallic and ionic crystals.

Abstract: Zeolitic Imidazolate Frameworks (ZIFs) are a family of metal--organic frameworks that feature metal centers tetrahedrally linked to imidazole-based ligands and adopt zeolite-like topologies. ZIFs formed by Zinc cations and imidazolate linkers exhibit a remarkable degree of polymorphism, which can be modulated by varying synthesis parameters or thermodynamic conditions (i.e., temperature and pressure). Computer simulations provide a unique way of studying these materials and their phase transitions from the microscopic standpoint, revealing their underlying molecular mechanisms. However, studying these mechanisms requires to be able to classify the phase of each molecular entity in an agnostic and automatic fashion, which is particularly challenging when the two phases involved are structurally very similar. In this work, we systematically study neural network classifiers to classify ZIF phases on-the-fly during molecular dynamics simulations. We test a variety of input features, differing both in the dimensionality and nature of the descriptors and in the kind of force field used for building the training/testing database. We reveal that even with low-dimensional descriptors the classification is highly accurate, while the use of high-dimensional descriptors leads to an even better performance. Training the classifier with configurations coming from different force fields we can remove force field bias and enhance the classifier performance and general applicability. Finally, we apply our classifiers to reveal mechanistic details of the ZIF-4-cp $\xrightarrow{}$ ZIF-4-cp-II phase transition.

*Daniel Errandonea,Robin Turnbull,Hussien H. H. Osman,Zoulikha Hebboul,Pablo Botella,Neha Bura,Peijie Zhang,Jose Luis Rodrigo Ramon,Josu Sanchez-Martin,Catalin Popescu,Francisco J. Manjon*

Abstract: Combining X-ray diffraction with density-functional theory and electron topology calculations we found that pressure substantially modifies the bonding in K2Zn(IO3)4.2H2O. We discovered that under compression there is a progressive change from primary covalent I-O bonds and secondary halogen I-O interactions towards O-I-O electron-deficient multicenter bonds. Because of this, iodine hypercoordination converts IO3 trigonal pyramids towards IO6 units. The formation of these IO6 units breaks the typical isolation of iodate molecules forming an infinite two-dimensional iodate network. Hypercoordination influences the hydrogen atoms too, such that multicenter O-H-O bonds are also promoted with increasing pressure. We have determined that K2Zn(IO3)4.2H2O is one of the most compressible iodates studied to date, with a bulk modulus of 22(3) GPa. The pressure-induced structural changes strongly modify the electronic structure as shown by optical-absorption measurements and band-structure calculations. The band-gap energy closes from 4.2(1) eV at ambient pressure to 3.4(1) eV at 20 GPa.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过原位高压中子衍射探究钨铁矿型（wolframite-type）FeWO₄的结构与磁性性质随温度的依赖关系，验证现有对钨铁矿磁性的理解，并建立其压力-体积状态方程。

Method: 采用高压中子衍射技术，在Institut Laue Langevin的XtremeD仪器上进行测量，最高压力达8.7(4) GPa，最低温度至30.0(5) K；通过Rietveld精修分析衍射数据。

Result: 研究发现，尽管压力导致5%的体积收缩，但最大压力未改变磁有序下的Shubnikov空间群；磁矩取向和Néel温度随压力轻微变化，这与现有对钨铁矿磁性的理解一致；同时确定了300 K下FeWO₄的压力-体积状态方程。

Conclusion: 高压对FeWO₄的结构和磁性影响有限，最大压力下仅引起轻微变化而未改变基本磁结构；所得状态方程与先前X射线衍射研究和密度泛函理论计算结果相符。

Abstract: The temperature dependence of the structural and magnetic properties of wolframite-type FeWO4 were studied in situ by high pressure neutron diffraction. Neutron diffraction measurements were performed at the XtremeD instrument at the Institut Laue Langevin up to a maximum pressure of 8.7(4) GPa and a minimum temperature of 30.0(5) K. The diffraction data were analyzed via Rietveld refinements. We found that despite of producing a contraction of 5% of the volume, the maximum pressure applied in this study does not modify the Shubnikov space group below magnetic order. However, the orientation of magnetic moments and the Néel temperature, are slightly modified with the pressure, which is expected according to the preexistent understanding of magnetism in wolframites. We also determined a pressure-volume equation of state of FeWO4 at 300 K, which is compared with previous X-ray diffraction studies and density-functional theory calculations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 银铌酸银作为传统钙钛矿氧化物（perovskite oxide），已知具有丰富的多态性（polymorphism），但其低温结构仍不明确。尽管常被归类为反铁电体（antiferroelectric），其确切结构存在争议。

Method: 研究采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）来探索银铌酸银的低温结构，特别关注不同相之间的能量竞争关系。

Result: 计算揭示了一个先前被忽视的菱面体铁电相（rhombohedral ferroelectric phase），具有R3对称性，是热力学基态（thermodynamic ground state）。该相结构上具有手性（chirality），源于极化与氧八面体沿[111]方向同相旋转（in-phase rotations）的耦合，形成了铁手性态（ferri-chiral state）。

Conclusion: 该相表现出与石英相当的自然光学活性（natural optical activity）。尽管在能量上有利，其实验观测可能受到动力学限制（kinetic limitations）的阻碍，这可能解释了关于银铌酸银低温结构的持续争议。

Abstract: Silver niobate is a conventional perovskite oxide compound, known to exhibit a rich polymorphism. Although often classified as antiferroelectric, its low-temperature structure remains unclear. Here, first-principles calculations reveal a previously overlooked and unusual rhombohedral ferroelectric phase with $R3$ symmetry that emerges as the thermodynamic ground state despite its close energetic competition among previously proposed structures. Remarkably, this phase is structurally chiral, with chirality emerging improperly from the coupling between polarization and in-phase rotations of the oxygen octahedra along [111], producing a ferri-chiral state with incomplete cancellation of local chiral motifs. As a consequence, the phase exhibits significant natural optical activity comparable to that of quartz. Although energetically favored, its experimental observation may be hindered by kinetic limitations, potentially contributing to the ongoing controversy surrounding the low-temperature structure of silver niobate.

Abstract: Phase equilibria in the Al-Ti-Nb-Zr-Ta refractory complex concentrated alloy system were investigated using a high throughput experimental approach. A pseudo-ternary section of the quinary compositional space was prepared by a honeycomb type powder metallurgy design, consolidated by spark plasma sintering and subsequently homogenized at 1400 °C for 168 h. Phase constitution and chemical partitioning were characterized by SEM/EDS, XRD, EBSD, and TEM, supported by a custom EDS phase clustering workflow. Equilibrium microstructures consisting primarily of BCC, B2, and secondary phases were identified across the sampled compositions, with nanoscale precipitates forming in Zr and Ta rich regions. The results provide new experimental insight into phase stability and microstructural trends in Al-Ti-Nb-Zr-Ta alloys and demonstrate the effectiveness of high throughput combinatorial approaches for mapping complex multicomponent systems.

Method: 采用第一性原理（first-principles）研究，包括密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算和推弹性能带（nudged elastic band）计算。分析了原始和Ti掺杂的MgB₂H₈体系，通过声子（phonon）和弹性分析评估结构稳定性，并进行电子结构分析解释性能改善机制。

Conclusion: Ti掺杂MgB₂H₈是一种有前景的储氢材料，通过改善脱附热力学和扩散动力学，同时保持结构稳定性和较高储氢容量。电子结构变化解释了性能改善的机制，为复杂硼氢化物的优化设计提供了见解。

Abstract: Hydrogen storage remains a key challenge for the development of a sustainable hydrogen energy system, where materials must satisfy requirements on storage capacity, thermodynamics, kinetics, and reversibility. In this work, we present a first-principles study of pristine and Ti-doped MgB2H8 as a solid-state hydrogen storage material. Density functional theory calculations show that pristine MgB2H8 has a high gravimetric hydrogen capacity of about 14.9 wt percent, but also a relatively high hydrogen desorption enthalpy of about 42 kJ per mol H2 and diffusion barriers around 0.5 eV, which limit its performance at moderate temperatures. Substitutional doping with Ti at the Mg site improves these properties while maintaining structural stability. The doped system retains a high hydrogen capacity of about 10.4 wt percent and shows a reduced desorption enthalpy of about 36 kJ per mol H2, placing it within a favorable thermodynamic range for hydrogen release. Nudged elastic band calculations show a reduction in hydrogen migration barriers to about 0.38 eV, indicating improved diffusion kinetics. Phonon and elastic analyses confirm that Ti doping preserves stability. ### [125] [Competing thermalization pathways of photoexcited hot electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09236)
*Christopher Seibel,Tobias Held,Markus Uehlein,Baerbel Rethfeld*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体中的光激发热载流子（hot carriers）能够驱动超出热平衡范围的表面光催化反应，但热电子介导的反应路径受到非平衡电子分布通过微观散射事件热化的限制。传统观点通常将热化仅归因于电子-电子散射，而电子-声子散射主要被视为与晶格能量平衡相关。

Method: 研究采用基于完整玻尔兹曼碰撞积分（full Boltzmann collision integrals）的动力学模型，分析电子-电子散射和电子-声子散射各自对电子分布热化的贡献。

Result: 研究发现每种散射机制单独都能使电子分布热化，尽管在相空间中沿着不同的轨迹。两种机制的热化时间对激发强度呈现相反的依赖关系，且在弱激发条件下（对应样品温度升高几开尔文）可以变得相当。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了电子-电子散射和电子-声子散射在整个实验激发强度范围内（直至熔化区域）对热化的贡献，有助于预测基于热载流子应用的热化时间。

Abstract: Photoexcited hot carriers in solids can drive processes, such as photocatalytic reactions on the surface, beyond those available in thermal equilibrium. Hot-electron-mediated reaction pathways are limited by the thermalization of the nonequilibrium electron distribution through microscopic scattering events. Commonly, thermalization is exclusively attributed to electron-electron scattering, whereas electron-phonon scattering is considered relevant mainly for the energy equilibration with the lattice. With a kinetic model based on full Boltzmann collision integrals, we demonstrate that each scattering mechanism alone can thermalize the electron distribution, albeit along different trajectories in phase space. We find an opposite dependence on the excitation strength of the respective thermalization times and show that both processes can become comparable for weak excitations, corresponding to a sample temperature increase of a few Kelvin. Our results unravel the contributions of electron-electron and electron-phonon scattering to the thermalization across the full range of experimental excitation strengths up to the melting regime, thus facilitating the prediction of thermalization times for hot-carrier-based applications.

### [126] [Nonlinear electron-phonon coupling drives light-induced symmetry switching in charge-density waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09242)
*Christoph Emeis,Fabio Caruso*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于海森堡绘景（Heisenberg picture）的结构动力学方法，明确考虑了四次晶格非谐性（quartic lattice anharmonicities）、非线性电子-声子相互作用（nonlinear electron-phonon interactions）以及光激发诱导的势能面修正。通过第一性原理计算模拟了单层TiSe₂（具有2×2结构重构的原型CDW晶体）中CDW序的超快熔融。

Result: 模拟结果与现有实验良好吻合，捕捉到了CDW熔融的关键特征：阻尼相干结构运动、软模（soft mode）的瞬态重整化（transient renormalization）以及在几皮秒时间尺度上CDW序的恢复。研究识别出非线性电子-声子相互作用是驱动CDW系统对称性切换的主要机制。

Abstract: Ultrafast optical excitation in charge-density wave (CDW) crystals can transiently suppress long-range order, driving the lattice toward higher symmetry on femtosecond timescales. Here, we formulate and implement a first-principles theory of light-induced melting of CDW order. The approach is based on the structural dynamics in the Heisenberg picture, and it explicitly accounts for quartic lattice anharmonicities, nonlinear electron-phonon interactions, and photoexcitation-induced modifications of the potential energy surface. We illustrate these concepts through first-principles calculations of the ultrafast melting of CDW order in monolayer TiSe$_2$ - a prototypical CDW crystal with a 2$\times$2 structural reconstruction. The simulations are in good agreement with existing experiments, and they capture the defining features of CDW melting, such as the damped coherent structural motion, the transient renormalization of the soft mode, and the restoration of CDW order over timescales of a few picoseconds. Besides identifying nonlinear electron-phonon interactions as the primary mechanism driving symmetry switching in CDW systems, our work establishes a generally applicable theoretical framework to treat quartic anharmonicities and light-induced phase transitions in first-principles ultrafast dynamics simulations.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常温光催化氮还原是实现可持续氨生产的重要途径，但其基本机制，特别是光生载流子与表面缺陷和吸附物的相互作用机制尚不明确。本研究旨在阐明这些关键相互作用在氮还原反应中的具体作用。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）结合Hubbard U修正和杂化泛函（hybrid functionals），研究TiO₂(110)表面上光生电子极化子与点缺陷的协同相互作用机制。

Result: 研究发现水吸附促进极化子从亚表面向表面位点迁移，而后续的水解离通过质子耦合电子极化子转移（proton coupled electron polaron transfer, PCEpT）稳定了氧空位附近的极化子。这种极化子的表面局域化对于有效的N₂吸附和活化至关重要。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了表面极化子在光催化固氮中的关键作用，为能够容纳小极化子的氧化物表面和界面提供了普适的机制见解，为常温条件下高效光催化剂的设计提供了新原理。

Abstract: Photocatalytic nitrogen reduction under ambient conditions represents a promising pathway toward sustainable ammonia production. However, the fundamental mechanisms, particularly the role of photogenerated charge carriers and their interactions with surface defects and adsorbates, remain elusive. Here, we employ density functional theory with Hubbard U corrections and hybrid functionals to demonstrate that the synergistic interactions between photogenerated electron polarons and point defects are essential for enabling nitrogen reduction on TiO$_2$(110). We reveal that water adsorption promotes polaron migration from subsurface to surface sites, while subsequent water dissociation stabilizes polarons near oxygen vacancies through proton coupled electron polaron transfer (PCEpT). This surface localization of polarons is critical for effective N$_2$ adsorption and activation. Our findings are consistent with previous experimental reports utilizing EPR that confirm the presence of reduced Ti species and STM, which shows the presence of water dimers on the surface. Moreover, the simultaneous interaction between polarons and reaction intermediates facilitates polaron transfer, thereby driving the completion of the nitrogen reduction reaction. Our findings elucidate the pivotal role of surface polarons in photocatalytic nitrogen fixation and provide mechanistic insights applicable to a broad range of oxide surfaces and interfaces capable of hosting small polarons, offering new design principles for efficient photocatalysts operating under ambient conditions.

</details>


### [128] [On the origin of superlattice stacking faults nucleation via climb of Frank partial in CoNi-based superalloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09329)
*Zhida Liang,Yinan Cui,Li Wang,Xin Liu,Bin Liu,Yong Liu,Fengxian Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在CoNi基高温合金中，a/3<111>弗兰克不全位错（Frank partials）的非保守攀移（non-conservative climb）是形成超点阵内禀堆垛层错（SISFs）和外禀堆垛层错（SESFs）的普遍且动力学可行的途径，首次实验证实了负攀移辅助的SESF形核机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为γ'相中的超点阵堆垛层错（superlattice stacking faults）主要通过保守的肖克利不全位错（Shockley partial）滑移形核。本研究旨在探索非保守的弗兰克不全位错攀移是否构成一种更普遍的层错形成机制，特别是在高温变形条件下。

Method: 采用高分辨透射电子显微镜（high-resolution transmission electron microscopy）观察CoNi基高温合金在850°C压缩变形后的微观结构。通过能量和动力学分析（energetic and kinetic analyses）评估弗兰克不全位错攀移的可行性，并进行定量比较不同机制的迁移率。

Result: 实验首次证实负攀移（negative climb）辅助的SESF形核，并观察到正攀移（positive climb）辅助的SISF构型与先前报道机制有根本区别。弗兰克不全位错源于领先30°肖克利不全位错与共轭{111}面上60°混合位错（mixed dislocation）的反应，形成能量稳定的构型促进后续攀移。溶质偏聚（solute segregation）诱导的层错能降低对弗兰克不全位错攀移起主导作用。

Conclusion: 攀移辅助的堆垛层错形成是γ'相中统一的变形机制，SISF和SESF扩展均可通过弗兰克不全位错攀移实现。在高温下，溶质拖曳控制的肖克利滑移（solute drag-controlled Shockley glide）与空位扩散控制的弗兰克攀移（vacancy diffusion-controlled Frank climb）具有相当的迁移率。

Abstract: High-temperature deformation in superalloys is governed by the cooperative glide-climb motion of dislocations. Superlattice stacking faults (SFs) in the gamma prime phase are predominantly interpreted as nucleating via conservative Shockley partial glide. Here, we demonstrate that non-conservative climb of a/3<111> Frank partials constitutes a general and kinetically viable pathway for both superlattice intrinsic (SISFs) and extrinsic stacking faults (SESFs) formation in the L12 structure of CoNi-based superalloys during compression at 850 Celsius. High-resolution transmission electron microscopy reveals that Frank partials form at gamma/gamma prime interface can climb into the gamma prime phase, generating SISFs via positive climb and SESFs via negative climb. Importantly, the negative climb-assisted nucleation of SESFs is experimentally confirmed for the first time, and the observed positive climb-assisted SISF configuration differs fundamentally from previously reported mechanisms. We show that these Frank partials originate from the reaction between a leading 30 degree Shockley partial and a 60 degree mixed dislocation on conjugate {111} planes, producing energetically stable configurations that promote subsequent climb. Energetic and kinetic analyses demonstrate that solute segregation induced reduction of SF energy provides a dominant contribution to Frank partial climb, enabling sustained climb and consequent SF expansion. Quantitative comparisons further indicate that, at elevated temperatures, solute drag-controlled Shockley glide can achieve mobilities comparable to vacancy diffusion-controlled Frank climb. These findings establish climb-assisted SF formation as a unified deformation mechanism in gamma prime phase, and that both SISF and SESF expansion can proceed through Frank partial climb.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究为射频磁控溅射工艺对银纳米线网络的降解机制提供了实验依据，并提出了有效的缓解策略，为AgNW网络在多层器件中的可靠集成奠定了技术基础。

Abstract: As silver nanowire (AgNW) networks reach increasing technological maturity, research efforts are progressively shifting toward their integration into functional devices. In this context, it is essential to assess how thin film coating processes affect the structural and functional integrity of these transparent conducting networks. Radio Frequency (RF) magnetron sputtering is among the most widely used and industrially scalable deposition techniques, making a detailed understanding of its impact on AgNW networks particularly critical. In this work, we experimentally investigate the degradation of AgNW networks observed under specific RF magnetron sputtering regimes. By varying deposition time, oxygen partial pressure, target material, buffer layers and plasma power, we analyze how sputtering conditions influence the electrical, morphological, and structural properties of the networks. Based on these observations, we identify viable strategies to mitigate or suppress network degradation, thereby enabling safer and more reliable coating protocols. These results provide practical guidelines for the integration of AgNW networks into multilayer device architectures.

### [130] [Oxygen-Mediated Phase Evolution in Sputtered Cu-W-O: Insights into Surface Chemistry Variability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09401)
*José Montero-Amenedo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过直流磁控共溅射（DC magnetron co-sputtering）在不同氧分压下制备Cu-W-O三元化合物薄膜，低氧条件形成单一CuWO4相，高氧条件则产生CuWO4与Cu3WO6混合相。结构、光学和表面化学分析揭示了相共存、择优取向变化以及Cu迁移导致的成分不均匀性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索溅射制备的Cu-W-O薄膜在不同氧分压条件下的相形成、结构演变和电子态特性。关注合成条件对三元氧化物（ternary oxide）结构和电子性质的影响，强调严格表征对确保研究可重复性的重要性。

Method: 采用直流磁控共溅射技术从Cu和W金属靶材在控制氧分压下制备薄膜，随后进行热退火处理。使用X射线衍射（XRD）分析结构，分光光度法（spectrophotometry）研究光学性质，X射线光电子能谱（XPS）进行表面化学环境分析，并通过Wagner图（Wagner plot）分析区分初始态和终态效应。

Conclusion: 溅射制备的Cu-W-O薄膜即使名义上被识别为CuWO4，其结构和电子态也会因合成条件而显著不同。研究强调了在二元氧化物研究中需要进行严格表征以确保可重复性，并揭示了Cu迁移和偏析导致的表面-体相差异。

Abstract: Thin films of Cu-W-O ternary compounds were fabricated via DC magnetron co-sputtering from Cu and W metallic targets under controlled oxygen partial pressures, followed by thermal annealing. Low-oxygen conditions favored the formation of a single CuWO4 phase, whereas higher oxygen levels produced a mixture of CuWO4 and Cu3WO6. Structural and optical properties were investigated by X-ray diffraction (XRD) and spectrophotometry, revealing phase coexistence and changes in preferential orientation depending on the deposition conditions. A detailed and carefully validated X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS) analysis provides insight into the surface chemical environment of Cu and W, indicating the presence of compositional inhomogeneities and surface-bulk differences associated with Cu migration and segregation. While the W 4f core levels remain remarkably stable across all tested oxygen partial pressures, a systematic shift is observed in the Cu 2p3/2 binding energy. Wagner plot analysis confirms that this displacement is dominated by initial-state effects, reflecting modifications of the Cu ground-state electronic structure and Cu-O-W hybridization rather than changes in final-state screening. Our findings demonstrate that sputtered Cu-W-O films, even when nominally identified as CuWO4, can exhibit substantially different structural and electronic states depending on synthesis conditions, highlighting the need for rigorous characterization to ensure reproducibility in ternary oxide research.

### [131] [Bounding axion dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09141)
*Gary Shiu,Flavio Tonioni,Hung V. Tran*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究推导了周期性势能（pseudo）标量理论在宇宙学背景下的解析界限，结合观测数据约束轴子暗能量参数空间，并发现量子引力约束与基本轴子精质模型存在张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究周期性势能（periodic potentials）的（伪）标量理论在包含任意宇宙学流体（包括正负宇宙学常数）背景下的宇宙学解，旨在为解冻精质（thawing quintessence）模型提供自然应用。

Method: 推导了与初始失配角（initial misalignment angle）和场速度无关的解析界限，该界限描述了宇宙减速过程中轴子质量参数和衰变常数（decay constant）需满足的关系，并应用于轴子暗能量模型的参数约束。

Result: 结合DESI和超新星观测数据，该解析界限为轴子暗能量提供了约束；进一步结合量子引力约束，排除了参数空间的广阔区域，导致轴子质量远大于哈勃尺度（Hubble scale）。

Conclusion: 解析界限与量子引力约束的组合将轴子质量推向远大于哈勃尺度的范围，这与基本的轴子精质（axion quintessence）模型存在显著张力。

Abstract: We study cosmological solutions of (pseudo)scalar theories with periodic potentials, in the presence of arbitrary cosmological fluids -- including a cosmological constant of either sign. Independently of the initial misalignment angle and field velocity, we derive an analytic bound that the axion mass parameter and decay constant fulfill as the universe decreases its acceleration rate, finding a natural application in models of thawing quintessence. As a first application, we illustrate the analytic handle our bound provides in bounding axion dark energy, after observational inputs from DESI and various supernovae data sets are taken into account. As a second application, we argue that our analytic bounds in combination with proposed quantum gravity constraints on axions exclude vast regions of parameter space. The combined constraints push the axion masses to be much larger than the Hubble scale, in tension with basic models of axion quintessence.

### [132] [Long time dynamics close to large amplitude quasi-periodic traveling waves in two dimensional forced rotating fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09302)
*Roberto Feola,Luca Franzoi,Riccardo Montalto*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究β-平面方程（β-plane equation）在接近大振幅准周期行波解时的长时间动力学行为，证明了初始数据充分接近行波解时，解能长时间保持接近该行波解，从而得到大初始数据的几乎全局存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在分析β-平面方程在光滑外力作用下的长时间动力学行为，该外力是具有大振幅O(λ^{α-1})（1<α<2）和大传播速度O(λ)的准周期行波。先前研究已证明存在大振幅准周期行波解，本文则关注接近这些行波解的初始数据的长时间演化。

Method: 证明结合了多种技术：通过正规形方法（normal form methods）分析任意行波解处的线性化偏微分方程；在坐标变换对角化线性化方程后，对变换后的非线性问题进行精细分析；以及能量估计（energy estimates）。

Result: 证明了对于在H^s拓扑中充分接近固定行波解的初始数据，相应解能在任意长时间内保持接近该行波解（与行波解的大小无关）。由此得到大初始数据的开集具有几乎全局存在性（almost global existence），即相应解能在任意长时间内保持与初始数据相同的大小。

Conclusion: 本文建立了β-平面方程接近大振幅准周期行波解的长时间稳定性结果，证明了初始数据充分接近行波解时解的长时间行为可控，为大振幅初始数据的动力学分析提供了理论保证。

Abstract: In this paper we consider the $β$-plane equation with a smooth external force which is a quasi-periodic traveling wave of large amplitude $O(λ^{α- 1})$, $1 < α< 2$, and with large speed of propagation of size $O(λ)$. In a previous paper, the second and the third author proved the existence of quasi-periodic traveling wave solutions of large amplitude of order $O(λ^θ)$, for some $θ> 0$. The purpose of this paper is to analyze the long time dynamics for smooth initial data close to these traveling wave solutions. In particular, we shall prove that, for initial data sufficiently close to a fixed traveling wave solution (in the $H^s$ topology), the corresponding solution remains close to the traveling wave solution for arbitrary long time (independent of the size of the traveling wave solution). As a consequence, we prove that there are open sets of large initial for which one has almost global existence, namely such that the corresponding solution remains of the same size of the initial datum for arbitrary long time (independent of the size of the initial data). The proof combines several ingredients: an analysis of the linearized PDE at any traveling wave solution via normal form methods, a sharp analysis of the transformed nonlinear problem under the change of coordinates that diagonalizes the linearized equation and energy estimates.

### [133] [Massless Maxwell fields on sub-extremal Kerr-Newman exteriors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09298)

Abstract: We study the massless Maxwell system on fixed sub--extremal Kerr-Newman exteriors. In the weak Kerr--Newman regimes with $0<|a|\le c_a M$, $0<|Q|\le c_Q M$, and $c_a,c_Q \in (0,1) $, we prove non--degenerate boundedness, Morawetz / integrated local energy decay, the outgoing $r^p$ hierarchy, radiation fields, polynomial decay, and two--sided scattering for the stationary-subtracted Maxwell field. In the axisymmetric relative slow--rotation regime $0<|a|\le \varepsilon_{\mathrm{KN}}|Q|<M$ with $\varepsilon_{\mathrm{KN}} \in (0,1)$, the same conclusions hold on the axisymmetric sector, with no perturbative restriction on $|Q|/M$ beyond sub--extremality. For the full sub-extremal range $a^2+Q^2<M^2$, by adding one order--zero radiative local--energy estimate for this master system, we could obtain similar results as the weak regimes. This separates the unconditional weak theory from the conditional full--range theory within one reconstruction/scattering framework.

### [134] [Graded Casimir elements and central extensions of color Lie algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08900)
*N. Aizawa,I. Fujii,J. Segar,J. Van der Jeugt*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种构造彩色李代数（color Lie algebra）及其环路代数（loop algebra）的二级分级卡西米尔元（graded Casimir elements）和分级中心扩张（graded central extensions）的通用方法，并通过三个具体代数实例验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 彩色李代数作为李（超）代数（Lie (super)algebra）通过阿贝尔群（Abelian group）Γ的推广，具有分级结构并允许分级卡西米尔元。其环路代数也允许分级中心扩张，但需要系统的方法来构造这些结构。

Method: 作者提出了一种通用方法来分别构造给定彩色李代数的二级分级卡西米尔元及其环路代数的分级中心扩张。该方法适用于具有分级结构的代数体系。

Result: 通过三个具体实例证明了存在大量彩色李代数允许此类分级结构：对于Γ=ℤ₃²的𝔰𝔩(2)，以及对于Γ=ℤ₂²的𝔮(n)和𝔬𝔰𝔭(m|2n)。这些代数均能构造出相应的分级卡西米尔元和中心扩张。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，所提出的方法能够有效构造彩色李代数及其环路代数的分级结构，为这类广义代数体系的研究提供了系统的理论框架和具体构造技术。

Abstract: A color Lie algebra is a generalization of a Lie (super)algebra by an Abelian group $Γ$. The underlying vector space and defining relations of the algebra are graded by $Γ$, and the color Lie algebra admits graded Casimir elements. Furthermore, its loop algebra admits graded central extensions. We present a general method for constructing 2nd order graded Casimir elements and graded central extensions for a given color Lie algebra and its loop algebra, respectively. We also show that there exists a large class of color Lie algebras admitting such graded Casimir elements or central extensions by providing three examples, namely, $\mathfrak{sl}(2)$ for $Γ= \mathbb{Z}_3^2$, and $\mathfrak{q}(n)$ and $\mathfrak{osp}(m|2n)$ for $Γ= \mathbb{Z}_2^2$.

### [135] [Symmetry-driven thermalization via finite de Finetti theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09410)
*Uttam Singh,Nicolas J. Cerf*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于对称性而非统计原理的量子热化新机制，证明了在能量守恒幺正变换下的不变性足以确定性地产生热结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，封闭量子系统中子系统的热行为通常归因于统计机制，如动力学混沌、量子遍历性或本征态热化假设。本文旨在探索一种不依赖统计论证的替代机制，仅从对称性考虑出发确定性地解释热结构的产生。

Method: 作者证明了针对能量守恒幺正变换（energy-preserving unitaries）不变量子态的有限de Finetti型定理，建立了此类不变N-qudit态的约化边缘态与热乘积态凸混合的接近性。同时提供了能量守恒Lindblad动力学的实例，其长时间极限满足所需对称性。

Result: 研究结果表明，在能量守恒幺正变换下的不变性足以作为唯一的基本确定性原理来强制热结构的形成。约化边缘态在迹距离和相对熵意义上都接近热乘积态的凸混合，且误差界限随N→∞而消失。

Conclusion: 仅凭能量守恒幺正变换下的对称性不变性这一确定性原理，就足以解释热结构的涌现，为量子热化提供了不依赖统计论证的替代机制。

Abstract: Thermal behavior in subsystems of closed quantum systems is commonly attributed to dynamical chaos, quantum ergodicity, canonical typicality, or the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, suggesting a fundamentally statistical origin of thermalization. Here, we propose a potential alternative mechanism in which thermal structures emerge deterministically from symmetry considerations alone, without recourse to statistical arguments. We prove a finite de Finetti-type theorem for quantum states invariant under energy-preserving unitaries, establishing that the reduced marginals of any such invariant $N$-qudit state are close (both in trace distance and relative entropy) to convex mixtures of thermal product states, with explicit error bounds vanishing as $N \to \infty$. We further present an example of energy-conserving Lindblad dynamics whose long-time limit is invariant under energy-preserving unitaries, providing a dynamical realization of the desired symmetry class. These results imply that invariance under energy-preserving unitaries suffices as a sole fundamental, deterministic principle to enforce thermal structures.

</details>


### [136] [Quantum Randomized Subspace Iteration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09483)
*Stefano Scali,Brian Coyle,Giuseppe Buonaiuto,Michal Krompiec*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出量子随机子空间迭代（QRSI）方法，通过并行随机酉变换和本征态制备原语，完全覆盖简并量子本征空间，解决了传统方法难以自然覆盖多维简并子空间的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有变分（variational）和投影（projective）算法难以自然覆盖多维简并子空间（degenerate subspace），通常需要顺序正交约束。解决简并量子本征空间（包括拓扑有序基态和阻挫磁体）需要制备覆盖目标流形所有方向的高保真态。

Method: 引入量子随机子空间迭代（quantum randomized subspace iteration, QRSI），通过并行独立随机酉变换（random unitaries）共轭哈密顿量，分支数与简并度g相同，然后在每个分支上调用任意选择的本征态制备原语（eigenstate-preparation primitive）。目标子空间通过标准子空间估计从结果系综中识别。

Result: 证明该构造几乎必然覆盖完整本征空间，并在每个分支上精确保持谱隙（spectral gap）。当随机旋转满足简并流形上的反集中条件（anti-concentration condition）时，这些保证仍然成立，比完全Haar随机性要求更弱。在环面码（toric code）上演示了QRSI，恢复了所有四个拓扑基态。

Conclusion: QRSI提供了一种完全并行的方法来解决简并量子本征空间问题，能够覆盖多维简并子空间的所有方向，为处理拓扑有序基态和阻挫磁体等系统提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Resolving degenerate quantum eigenspaces - including topologically ordered ground states and frustrated magnets - requires preparing high-fidelity states that span every direction of the target manifold. Existing variational and projective algorithms do not naturally cover a multi-dimensional degenerate subspace without sequential orthogonality constraints. We introduce the quantum randomized subspace iteration (QRSI), a fully parallel construction that conjugates the Hamiltonian by independent random unitaries across as many branches as the degeneracy g, then invokes any chosen eigenstate-preparation primitive on each branch. The target subspace is identified from the resulting ensemble via standard subspace estimation, either classically through the coefficient matrix or on hardware through Gram-matrix measurements. We prove that the construction spans the full eigenspace almost surely and preserves the spectral gap exactly on every branch. For practical use, we show that these guarantees hold whenever the random rotations satisfy an anti-concentration condition over the degenerate manifold, substantially weaker than full Haar randomness. We demonstrate QRSI on the toric code, recovering all four topological ground states, and on random Hamiltonians with planted degeneracies.

</details>

Method: 采用一种替代方法，利用物理上不同、本质上更冷的声子浴（phononic bath）重置超导量子比特。具体通过将transmon量子比特与高频体声波谐振器（high-overtone bulk acoustic resonator, HBAR）接口，使量子比特冷却到GHz频率模式。

Result: 实现了量子比特剩余激发态布居低于$10^{-4}$，相比现有重置方案提升1-2个数量级。这展示了声子浴在超导电路中实现高保真度量子比特初始化的潜力。

Abstract: Achieving sufficiently low residual excited-state populations remains a key challenge in superconducting quantum circuits, particularly for protocols operating close to noise limits or requiring repeated qubit initialization. Existing protocols primarily address this challenge through sophisticated control, engineered dissipation, or feedback mechanisms. Here, we demonstrate an alternative approach in which a superconducting qubit is reset using a physically distinct, intrinsically colder phononic bath. Specifically, we interface a transmon with a high-overtone bulk acoustic resonator (HBAR), enabling cooling of the qubit into GHz-frequency modes. Using this approach, we achieve a residual excited-state population of the qubit below $10^{-4}$, representing an improvement of one to two orders of magnitude compared to existing reset schemes. These results highlight the potential of phononic baths as a resource for high-fidelity qubit initialization in superconducting circuits.

### [138] [Geometry-Induced Long-Range Correlations in Recurrent Neural Network Quantum States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.08661)
*Asif Bin Ayub,Amine Mohamed Aboussalah,Mohamed Hibat-Allah*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种扩张循环神经网络（dilated RNN）波函数，通过扩张连接机制有效捕捉量子态的长程关联，相比传统RNN在计算效率上具有优势，成功应用于临界伊辛模型和一维Cluster态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自回归循环神经网络（RNN）波函数虽然能避免马尔可夫链自相关，但其架构偏向有限长度关联，难以处理具有长程依赖的量子态。而采用Transformer自注意力机制通常带来显著的计算和内存开销。

Method: 本文引入扩张循环神经网络（dilated RNN）波函数，通过扩张连接使循环单元能够访问远距离格点，注入明确的长程归纳偏置，同时保持有利的$\mathcal{O}(N \log N)$前向传播复杂度。

Result: 分析表明扩张机制改变了关联几何结构，在简化的线性化微扰设定中可诱导幂律关联标度。数值计算显示，对于一维横场伊辛模型临界点，扩张RNN再现了预期的幂律关联，而传统RNN ansätze通常呈现指数衰减。扩张RNN还能准确近似一维Cluster态，该态具有长程条件关联，此前被报道对基于RNN的波函数具有挑战性。

Conclusion: 这些结果突显了扩张作为一种简单的几何机制，可用于构建具有关联感知能力的自回归神经量子态（neural quantum states），在保持计算效率的同时有效处理长程量子关联。

Abstract: Neural Quantum States based on autoregressive recurrent neural network (RNN) wave functions enable efficient sampling without Markov-chain autocorrelation, but standard RNN architectures are biased toward finite-length correlations and can fail on states with long-range dependencies. A common response is to adopt transformer-style self-attention, but this typically comes with substantially higher computational and memory overhead. Here we introduce dilated RNN wave functions, where recurrent units access distant sites through dilated connections, injecting an explicit long-range inductive bias while retaining a favorable $\mathcal{O}(N \log N)$ forward pass scaling. We show analytically that dilation changes the correlation geometry and can induce power-law correlation scaling in a simplified linearized and perturbative setting. Numerically, for the critical 1D transverse-field Ising model, dilated RNNs reproduce the expected power-law connected two-point correlations in contrast to the exponential decay typical of conventional RNN ansätze. We further show that the dilated RNN accurately approximates the one-dimensional Cluster state, a paradigmatic example with long-range conditional correlations that has previously been reported to be challenging for RNN-based wave functions. These results highlight dilation as a simple geometric mechanism for building correlation-aware autoregressive neural quantum states.

### [139] [Tantalum-Encapsulated Niobium Superconducting Resonators: High Internal Quality Factor and Improved Temporal Stability via Surface Passivation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09050)
*Anas Alkhazaleh,Juan Villegas,Florent Ravaux,Alexey Zharinov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过在铌薄膜上原位沉积薄层钽作为覆盖层，抑制Nb2O5形成并改善界面氧化物质量，从而提升超导共面波导谐振器的内禀品质因子（Qi）和时间稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导共面波导谐振器（superconducting coplanar waveguide resonators）是量子处理器关键组件，其内禀品质因子限制量子比特相干时间和读取保真度。铌器件在毫开温度下的微波损耗主要受与复杂NbOx表面氧化物相关的二能级系统（two-level systems, TLS）影响。

Method: 采用表面工程方法，在铌薄膜上原位覆盖薄钽层以抑制Nb2O5形成，并用钽基氧化物替代原生NbOx界面。在高阻硅衬底上制备Nb/Ta双层结构和参考铌谐振器，使用相同直流溅射和湿法刻蚀条件，并在毫开温度下表征其性能。

Result: 新鲜钽封装器件在近单光子区域展现出高达2.4×10^6的内禀品质因子，功率依赖性表明金属-空气界面处的TLS相关损耗降低。对照铌器件在相同工艺下表现出相对较低的Q_TLS，证实钽覆盖层的积极作用。六个月老化测试显示Nb/Ta谐振器的Q_TLS相对初始值适度降低，但性能仍优于新制备的纯铌器件。

Conclusion: 薄钽封装增强了界面质量并有助于改善时间稳定性，同时保持与铌基制造工艺的兼容性。该表面工程方法为提升超导量子器件的相干性能提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Superconducting coplanar waveguide resonators are essential components in quantum processors, where their internal quality factor (Qi) constrains qubit coherence and readout fidelity. In niobium devices, microwave losses at millikelvin temperatures are strongly influenced by two-level systems (TLS) associated with the complex NbOx surface oxide. To mitigate these losses, we investigate a surface-engineering approach in which Nb films are capped in situ with a thin tantalum layer to suppress Nb2O5 formation and replace the native NbOx interface with a Ta-based oxide.
  We fabricate Nb/Ta bilayer and reference Nb resonators on high-resistivity silicon using identical DC sputtering and wet etching conditions, and characterize their performance at millikelvin temperatures. Fresh Ta-encapsulated devices exhibit internal quality factors up to 2.4 x 10^6 in the near-single-photon regime, with power dependence consistent with reduced TLS-related loss at the metal-air interface. A control Nb device fabricated under the same process shows comparatively lower Q_TLS, consistent with the beneficial effect of the Ta capping layer. Furthermore, ageing tests performed on Nb/Ta resonators after six months reveal a moderate reduction in Q_TLS relative to their initial values, yet the performance remains superior to newly fabricated Nb-only devices. These results suggest that thin Ta encapsulation enhances interface quality and contributes to improved temporal stability while remaining compatible with Nb-based fabrication workflows.

### [140] [Coherent Control of Nanoscale Nuclear Spin Ensembles in the Spin Noise Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.09310)
*Ana Martin,Roberto Rizzato,Carlos Munuera-Javaloy,Dileep Singh,Dominik B. Bucher,Jorge Casanova*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在自旋噪声（spin-noise）体系中，射频（RF）场的相位和方向对基于关联光谱（correlation spectroscopy）的核自旋控制的关键影响，这些参数的不完美校准会导致信号对比度模糊和核自旋动力学误判。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体中的自旋缺陷（如金刚石中的氮空位中心）已成为纳米尺度核自旋检测的关键工具。虽然主动核自旋控制对于标准自旋噪声检测通常不必要，但对于多维纳米尺度核磁共振（NMR）等高级协议至关重要。本研究旨在探索使用关联光谱技术进行核自旋控制。

Method: 研究采用关联光谱技术（correlation spectroscopy techniques）进行核自旋控制，通过理论和实验相结合的方法，分析射频场的初始相位及其相对于氮空位晶体轴方向对核自旋动力学的影响。

Result: 研究结果表明，核自旋动力学关键取决于初始射频相位及其相对于氮空位晶体轴的方向。根据这些参数，相同的核旋转在氮空位读出中可产生完全、部分甚至消失的对比度，揭示了射频场相位和方向与基于关联实验的直接影响之间的关联。

Conclusion: 这些发现突显了自旋噪声体系中自旋操纵的一个先前未被充分认识的方面：所施加射频场的相位和方向与基于关联实验的直接影响之间的关联。研究结果为纳米尺度自旋控制提供了更深入的见解，并为可靠的多维自旋共振实验铺平了道路。

Abstract: Spin defects in solids, such as the nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center in diamond, have emerged as a key tool for detecting nuclear spins at the nanoscale. While active nuclear spin control via radio-frequency (RF) irradiation is often unnecessary for standard spin-noise detection, it becomes essential for advanced protocols like multidimensional nanoscale NMR. In this work, we investigate nuclear spin control using correlation spectroscopy techniques. We demonstrate, both theoretically and experimentally, that the resulting nuclear spin dynamics depend critically on the initial RF phase and its orientation relative to the NV crystalline axis. Depending on these parameters, identical nuclear rotations can yield full, partial, or even vanishing contrast in the NV readout. These findings highlight a previously underappreciated aspect of spin manipulation in the spin-noise regime: the link between the phase and direction of the applied RF field and its direct impact on correlation-based experiments. Consequently, imperfect calibration of these parameters can lead to ambiguous signal contrasts and misinterpretation of the underlying nuclear spin dynamics. Our results provide deeper insight into nanoscale spin control and pave the way toward reliable multidimensional spin resonance experiments.

</details>
